5366 src/polaris_graph/generator/weighted_enrichment.py
     1	"""I-arch-007 ITEM 2 (#1264) — BREADTH: weighted unbound-SUPPORTS enrichment selection.
     2	
     3	THE PROBLEM (the 485-in / ~13-cited collapse): the V30 contract render universe is the
     4	5 required contract entities + a handful of LLM-planner enrichment picks. On a FULLY
     5	SUCCESSFUL credibility pass that weighted + basketed hundreds of sources, the ~437 sources
     6	that are NOT bound to a contract ``v30_entity_id`` are never *offered* to any section — a
     7	purely STRUCTURAL funnel (it fires even when nothing times out). This module surfaces those
     8	unbound-but-span-verified SUPPORTS sources into ONE extra legacy (field-agnostic) section so
     9	they flow through the UNCHANGED ``_run_section`` -> ``strict_verify`` path.
    10	
    11	§-1.3 DNA — WEIGHT-AND-CONSOLIDATE, never FILTER-AND-CAP:
    12	  * WEIGHT, DON'T FILTER (I-arch-011 B18, the keystone): candidates are ORDERED by
    13	    relevance-to-question THEN basket ``weight_mass`` (priority of consideration). There is NO cap /
    14	    target / top-N / FLOOR DROP — the FULL surviving list is offered. KEEP-ALL-AND-SORT-BELOW-FLOOR-
    15	    LAST: a member whose source row scores BELOW ``PG_RELEVANCE_FLOOR`` is NOT excluded — it is KEPT
    16	    and sorted LAST (a below-floor ORDERING demotion, never a drop), exactly the way the retrieval
    17	    pool itself down-weights a below-floor row under the redesign (evidence_selector.py:2066-2070,
    18	    ``kept = list(scored)``). The pre-I-arch-011 code RE-IMPOSED a hard ``selection_relevance < 0.30``
    19	    DROP here — the SECTION-1.3-FORBIDDEN filter-and-cap anti-pattern the selector docstring
    20	    (evidence_selector.py:1944-1953) explicitly forbids, which killed 729/746 unbound SUPPORTS so the
    21	    enrichment appended NOTHING. That drop is REMOVED. ``below_floor_count`` is now pure TELEMETRY
    22	    (how many kept rows sit below the floor), never an exclusion.
    23	  * CONSOLIDATE, DON'T DROP: the members come straight from the already-computed claim baskets
    24	    (``ClaimBasket.supporting_members``) — the consolidated multi-source groups.
    25	  * BASKET FAITHFULNESS: a member is offered ONLY if its OWN isolated ``span_verdict`` is
    26	    ``"SUPPORTS"`` (computed by the credibility pass at credibility_pass.py:442-457). It is then
    27	    re-verified against its own span by the section's UNCHANGED ``strict_verify``. Breadth
    28	    EMERGES from how many survive that gate — it is never forced.
    29	
    30	RECONCILIATION WITH RETRIEVAL P0-A6 (evidence_selector.py:2036-2070): the retrieval POOL
    31	WEIGHTS-not-FILTERS — under the default redesign a below-floor row is KEPT and down-weighted in the
    32	pool, never hard-dropped (P0-A6 is UNTOUCHED). The breadth ENRICHMENT section now behaves
    33	IDENTICALLY: a below-floor unbound SUPPORTS member is KEPT and sorted LAST, never dropped — the
    34	relevance floor is an ORDERING weight at the surfacing boundary, not a re-introduction of the
    35	retrieval filter P0-A6 removed. The ONLY hard gate remains the faithfulness engine (strict_verify /
    36	NLI / 4-role / span-grounding), which is untouched.
    37	
    38	FAITHFULNESS-NEUTRALITY: this module only READS already-computed state and builds a candidate
    39	``SectionPlan``. It moves NO strict_verify / NLI / 4-role D8 / span-grounding / section-floor /
    40	sentinel threshold. The master flag defaults OFF (=> empty selection => byte-identical) and a
    41	degraded pass (``credibility_analysis is None``) also yields an empty selection (byte-identical).
    42	"""
    43	
    44	from __future__ import annotations
    45	
    46	import logging
    47	import os
    48	import re
    49	from collections import Counter
    50	from typing import Any, Callable, NamedTuple
    51	
    52	logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    53	
    54	# LAW VI: env-overridable, default OFF (unset => byte-identical legacy render).
    55	_ENV_BREADTH_ENRICHMENT = "PG_BREADTH_ENRICHMENT_ENABLED"
    56	
    57	# A NON-contract title => ``is_contract_section()`` (an isinstance(ContractSectionPlanExt) check)
    58	# is False => the section dispatches through ``_run_legacy_bounded`` -> field-agnostic
    59	# ``_run_section`` -> the same three-stream strict_verify the contract sentences use.
    60	_ENRICHMENT_TITLE = "Corroborated Weighted Findings"
    61	_ENRICHMENT_FOCUS = (
    62	    "Additional independently span-verified findings drawn from the weighted source corpus that "
    63	    "were not bound to a contract entity. Each sentence must survive the same strict_verify gate as "
    64	    "every other section; unsupported material is dropped, never padded."
    65	)
    66	
    67	_SUPPORTS = "SUPPORTS"
    68	
    69	# The per-row topicality sidecar the retrieval relevance gate stamps (evidence_selector.py:2128)
    70	# and finding_dedup reads (finding_dedup.py:212). It is THE existing relevance standard.
    71	_RELEVANCE_FIELD = "selection_relevance"
    72	
    73	# Constant sentinel for the relevance ORDERING key when a row carries no usable relevance score.
    74	# Using a constant (not the parsed value, not 0.0) ensures a pool of all-missing-relevance rows
    75	# ties on the relevance key, so the weight_mass tiebreak reproduces today's pure weight-desc order.
    76	_MISSING_RELEVANCE_SORT_KEY = 0.0
    77	
    78	
    79	def _row_relevance(row: Any) -> float | None:
    80	    """The row's ``selection_relevance`` topicality score, or ``None`` when not usable.
    81	
    82	    Returns ``None`` (=> relevance-gate FALLBACK = keep, ordering = sentinel) when the row is
    83	    missing, has no ``selection_relevance``, or carries an unparseable value. Deliberately NOT
    84	    ``float(row.get(field, 0.0) or 0.0)`` (finding_dedup's coercion): that maps a missing/None
    85	    score to 0.0, which would push it below any floor and wrongly EXCLUDE a member whose pool
    86	    membership already implies the retrieval relevance floor passed once.
    87	    """
    88	    if not isinstance(row, dict):
    89	        return None
    90	    raw = row.get(_RELEVANCE_FIELD)
    91	    if raw is None:
    92	        return None
    93	    try:
    94	        return float(raw)
    95	    except (TypeError, ValueError):
    96	        return None
    97	
    98	
    99	def _relevance_sort_key(relevance: float | None) -> float:
   100	    """Relevance value for the ORDERING key; the constant sentinel when relevance is unknown."""
   101	    return _MISSING_RELEVANCE_SORT_KEY if relevance is None else relevance
   102	
   103	
   104	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   105	# I-deepfix-001 (#1344) DEFER-1 — off-topic CITE-SURFACE suppression.
   106	#
   107	# drb_72 cited OFF-TOPIC sources (B1 supply-chain blogs, B2 Russian cosmetics, B3
   108	# recycling journal, B4 post-merger M&A) as numbered findings in the breadth
   109	# "Corroborated Weighted Findings" section. The keystone (I-arch-011 B18) correctly
   110	# forbids the lexical ``selection_relevance < floor`` DROP (it killed 729/746 real
   111	# unbound SUPPORTS and also suppressed REAL on-topic low-cred sources). So the
   112	# discriminator is NOT the noisy score — it is the SEMANTIC confirmed-OFF verdict
   113	# the topic gate / W2 content-relevance judge already produced and stamped on the
   114	# row (``topic_offtopic_demoted`` / ``content_relevance_label``). A confirmed
   115	# "this is about cosmetics, not AI labor" verdict is, by definition, not a
   116	# corroborator of an AI-labor claim, so withholding it from CITATION is not a
   117	# §-1.3 hard-drop: the source STAYS in evidence_pool + the credibility disclosure
   118	# (kept-and-disclosed). Gated default-ON; ``PG_OFFTOPIC_CITE_SUPPRESS=0`` restores
   119	# the byte-identical legacy cite-surface.
   120	_CONFIRMED_OFFTOPIC_LABELS = frozenset({"demoted", "escalated_demoted"})
   121	
   122	
   123	def offtopic_cite_suppress_enabled() -> bool:
   124	    """Kill-switch ``PG_OFFTOPIC_CITE_SUPPRESS`` (default ON). OFF => the cite
   125	    surface is byte-identical to the legacy keep-all-and-cite behaviour."""
   126	    return os.environ.get("PG_OFFTOPIC_CITE_SUPPRESS", "1").strip().lower() not in (
   127	        "0", "false", "no", "off",
   128	    )
   129	
   130	
   131	_POSITIVE_RELEVANCE_LABELS = frozenset({"relevant", "escalated_relevant"})
   132	
   133	
   134	def _offtopic_relevance_override_enabled() -> bool:
   135	    """Kill-switch ``PG_OFFTOPIC_RELEVANCE_OVERRIDE`` (default ON). OFF => the
   136	    legacy byte-identical ``_is_confirmed_offtopic`` (topic-flag wins)."""
   137	    return os.environ.get("PG_OFFTOPIC_RELEVANCE_OVERRIDE", "1").strip().lower() not in (
   138	        "0", "false", "no", "off",
   139	    )
   140	
   141	
   142	def _is_confirmed_offtopic(row: Any) -> bool:
   143	    """True iff a SEMANTIC judge confirmed this source is OFF-topic.
   144	
   145	    Keys ONLY on the topic-gate sidecar (``topic_offtopic_demoted is True``) OR the
   146	    W2 content-relevance LABEL (``content_relevance_label`` in
   147	    {``demoted``, ``escalated_demoted``}) — NEVER on the noisy lexical/embedding
   148	    ``selection_relevance`` score (that is the §-1.3-banned keystone DROP). A
   149	    missing/absent label is keep-neutral (NOT off-topic): an unjudged or
   150	    judged-RELEVANT row is never suppressed.
   151	
   152	    I-deepfix-001 (drb_72 forensic): when the TWO semantic judges DISAGREE — the
   153	    W2 content-relevance judge affirmatively rated the source ``relevant`` /
   154	    ``escalated_relevant`` (high weight) while the topic gate stamped
   155	    ``topic_offtopic_demoted=True`` — the AFFIRMATIVE relevance verdict WINS and the
   156	    source is NOT suppressed. This is the §-1.3 weight-not-filter rule: a false-positive
   157	    off-topic flag must never bury a source the content-relevance judge judged relevant.
   158	    (The drb_72 corpus buried the SEMINAL papers this way — GPTs-are-GPTs / World Bank /
   159	    Humlum all carried content_relevance_label='relevant' weight=1.0 BUT
   160	    topic_offtopic_demoted=True, so the old predicate suppressed them from the finding
   161	    surface.) Behind ``PG_OFFTOPIC_RELEVANCE_OVERRIDE`` (default ON); OFF = byte-identical."""
   162	    if not isinstance(row, dict):
   163	        return False
   164	    label = str(row.get("content_relevance_label", "") or "").strip().lower()
   165	    if _offtopic_relevance_override_enabled() and label in _POSITIVE_RELEVANCE_LABELS:
   166	        # judges conflict (relevant vs off-topic-demoted) -> trust the positive relevance, KEEP.
   167	        return False
   168	    if row.get("topic_offtopic_demoted") is True:
   169	        return True
   170	    return label in _CONFIRMED_OFFTOPIC_LABELS
   171	
   172	
   173	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   174	# I-deepfix-001 wave-2 — OFF-TOPIC FAIL-CLOSED QUARANTINE (Fable design).
   175	#
   176	# THE BUG (box2 wave-1): a RESUME reloads the corpus_snapshot post-selection and
   177	# SKIPS the topic judge, so every reloaded row carries NO topic verdict. The
   178	# ``_is_confirmed_offtopic`` seam keys ONLY on a POSITIVE confirmed-OFF verdict
   179	# (``topic_offtopic_demoted`` / ``content_relevance_label`` in demoted/escalated),
   180	# so an unjudged off-topic row (a funeral / tree-cover / face-recognition source
   181	# leaked into an AI-labor report) sails through and anchors a numbered finding.
   182	#
   183	# THE FIX — §-1.3 WITHHOLD-and-disclose, NEVER a lexical DROP: the BANNED discriminator
   184	# is the noisy lexical ``selection_relevance < floor`` (weighted_enrichment keystone:
   185	# it killed 729/746 real sources). This fix uses ONLY the ABSENCE of a semantic verdict
   186	# as a FAIL-CLOSED signal: a row the judge NEVER judged is WITHHELD from the finding
   187	# surface (kept in evidence_pool + the disclosure — never a pool drop, never deleted),
   188	# but ONLY when we can prove the judge actually ran this run (``topic_judge_ran``), and
   189	# ONLY within a blast-radius ceiling (``PG_QUARANTINE_MAX_FRACTION``). If the judge was
   190	# legitimately SKIPPED (a resume without PG_RESUME_RUN_TOPIC_JUDGE, or the topic gate
   191	# off), NOTHING is unjudged-in-the-leak-sense => nothing is quarantined. The faithfulness
   192	# engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role D8 / provenance / span-grounding) is UNTOUCHED —
   193	# withholding a citation is a SURFACE-placement decision, never a grounding change.
   194	# Gated default-OFF (LAW VI): PG_QUARANTINE_UNJUDGED_TOPIC unset => byte-identical.
   195	_ENV_QUARANTINE_UNJUDGED = "PG_QUARANTINE_UNJUDGED_TOPIC"      # master flag, default OFF
   196	_ENV_QUARANTINE_MAX_FRACTION = "PG_QUARANTINE_MAX_FRACTION"    # blast-radius ceiling (LAW VI)
   197	# Run-scoped signal the orchestrator sets when the topic judge demonstrably ran this run
   198	# (fresh OR the PG_RESUME_RUN_TOPIC_JUDGE resume path). Mirrored as a plain env name so the
   199	# generator never imports the retrieval-side gate on the hot path; ``topic_judge_ran`` ALSO
   200	# derives the same fact from the data (any row carrying a verdict), so the coupling holds
   201	# even if the orchestrator never set the flag.
   202	_ENV_TOPIC_JUDGE_RAN = "PG_TOPIC_JUDGE_RAN"
   203	_DEFAULT_QUARANTINE_MAX_FRACTION = 0.5
   204	_QUARANTINE_REASON = "unjudged_topic_no_verdict"
   205	
   206	
   207	def quarantine_unjudged_topic_enabled() -> bool:
   208	    """Master kill-switch ``PG_QUARANTINE_UNJUDGED_TOPIC`` (default OFF, LAW VI). OFF => no
   209	    row is ever quarantined on missing-verdict => byte-identical to the legacy cite surface."""
   210	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_QUARANTINE_UNJUDGED, "").strip().lower() in (
   211	        "1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled",
   212	    )
   213	
   214	
   215	def _quarantine_max_fraction() -> float:
   216	    """Blast-radius ceiling in [0.0, 1.0] (default 0.5). If quarantine WOULD withhold a
   217	    larger fraction of the surface than this, the guard trips (FAIL LOUD + disable). A
   218	    garbage value is an operator config error => ValueError (LAW VI: fail-loud, never
   219	    swallowed)."""
   220	    raw = os.environ.get(_ENV_QUARANTINE_MAX_FRACTION)
   221	    if raw is None or not str(raw).strip():
   222	        return _DEFAULT_QUARANTINE_MAX_FRACTION
   223	    val = float(str(raw).strip())  # ValueError on garbage: fail loud
   224	    if not (0.0 <= val <= 1.0):
   225	        raise ValueError(
   226	            f"{_ENV_QUARANTINE_MAX_FRACTION} must be in [0.0, 1.0]; got {val!r}"
   227	        )
   228	    return val
   229	
   230	
   231	def _topic_judge_ran_env() -> bool:
   232	    """The explicit run-scoped signal ``PG_TOPIC_JUDGE_RAN`` the orchestrator sets once the
   233	    topic judge has executed this run (fresh or resume). Absent => rely on the data-derived
   234	    corroboration in ``topic_judge_ran``."""
   235	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_TOPIC_JUDGE_RAN, "").strip().lower() in (
   236	        "1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled",
   237	    )
   238	
   239	
   240	def is_topic_unjudged(row: Any) -> bool:
   241	    """True iff a row carries NO topic verdict at all — the topic/content-relevance judge
   242	    never stamped it (``topic_offtopic_demoted`` absent AND ``content_relevance_label``
   243	    empty). A row a judge stamped — either a ``topic_offtopic_demoted`` sidecar (True/False)
   244	    OR a non-empty ``content_relevance_label`` (relevant / demoted / escalated_* /
   245	    wall_rescue_floor) — returns False. A non-dict returns False (keep-neutral; never
   246	    quarantined). PURE read of already-computed state; no faithfulness gate is touched and
   247	    NO lexical ``selection_relevance`` score is consulted (that is the §-1.3-banned DROP)."""
   248	    if not isinstance(row, dict):
   249	        return False
   250	    if row.get("topic_offtopic_demoted") is not None:
   251	        return False  # a topic-gate verdict (True/False) was stamped => judged
   252	    label = str(row.get("content_relevance_label", "") or "").strip()
   253	    return label == ""  # no content-relevance label => the judge never saw this row
   254	
   255	
   256	def _row_has_judgment(row: Any) -> bool:
   257	    """True iff SOME upstream relevance judge stamped this row — a ``topic_offtopic_demoted`` verdict,
   258	    a non-empty ``content_relevance_label``, OR a usable numeric ``selection_relevance``. F2 2b: when a
   259	    row carries a judged label we USE that judged decision (positive keeps, below-floor/off demotes)
   260	    and DO NOT re-apply the noisy lexical question-overlap override; the lexical fallback fires ONLY on
   261	    a fully-unjudged row. PURE read; no faithfulness touch."""
   262	    if not isinstance(row, dict):
   263	        return False
   264	    if row.get("topic_offtopic_demoted") is not None:
   265	        return True
   266	    if str(row.get("content_relevance_label", "") or "").strip():
   267	        return True
   268	    return _row_relevance(row) is not None
   269	
   270	
   271	def topic_judge_ran(rows: Any = None) -> bool:
   272	    """Run-scoped: True iff the topic/content-relevance judge demonstrably ran this run.
   273	
   274	    OR of two POSITIVE signals (either alone is sufficient proof the judge ran; only when
   275	    NEITHER holds do we conclude the judge was legitimately SKIPPED and stand quarantine
   276	    down):
   277	      (1) the explicit orchestrator env flag ``PG_TOPIC_JUDGE_RAN`` (set the moment
   278	          ``classify_topic_relevance`` executed this run — including the resume path opened
   279	          by ``PG_RESUME_RUN_TOPIC_JUDGE``), OR
   280	      (2) at least one provided row carries a topic verdict (``not is_topic_unjudged`` — a
   281	          stamp only a judge could have written).
   282	
   283	    This is the coupling that makes the quarantine NEVER fire when the judge was skipped:
   284	    a skipped-judge run has no env flag AND no stamped row, so this returns False."""
   285	    if _topic_judge_ran_env():
   286	        return True
   287	    for row in (rows or ()):
   288	        if isinstance(row, dict) and not is_topic_unjudged(row):
   289	            return True
   290	    return False
   291	
   292	
   293	def partition_unjudged_topic_rows(
   294	    rows: Any,
   295	    *,
   296	    judged_universe: Any = None,
   297	    anchor_predicate: "Callable[[Any], bool] | None" = None,
   298	) -> "tuple[list, list]":
   299	    """Split ``rows`` into ``(kept, quarantined)`` on ``is_topic_unjudged``, FAIL-CLOSED.
   300	
   301	    Quarantine fires ONLY when ALL of:
   302	      * ``PG_QUARANTINE_UNJUDGED_TOPIC`` is ON (default OFF => ``(list(rows), [])``), AND
   303	      * the topic judge ran this run (``topic_judge_ran`` over ``judged_universe`` or
   304	        ``rows``) — so a legitimately-skipped judge NEVER quarantines, AND
   305	      * the blast-radius guard passes: the withheld fraction ``<= PG_QUARANTINE_MAX_FRACTION``
   306	        (default 0.5). If it WOULD exceed the ceiling, the guard TRIPS: ``logger.error``
   307	        (FAIL LOUD) + disable for this call (return every row kept). A mass-withhold is the
   308	        signature of a judge that did not actually stamp the corpus, so we refuse to nuke it.
   309	
   310	    A marquee/required-entity anchor (via ``anchor_predicate``) is NEVER quarantined. A
   311	    quarantined row is WITHHELD from the finding surface only — the caller keeps it in
   312	    ``evidence_pool`` + the off-topic disclosure; nothing is deleted; the faithfulness engine
   313	    is untouched. OFF / judge-skipped / no unjudged row => ``(list(rows), [])``."""
   314	    row_list = list(rows or [])
   315	    if not quarantine_unjudged_topic_enabled():
   316	        return row_list, []
   317	    universe = list(judged_universe) if judged_universe is not None else row_list
   318	    if not topic_judge_ran(universe):
   319	        # The judge was legitimately skipped this run => absence of a verdict is EXPECTED,
   320	        # not a leak. Never quarantine (byte-identical keep-all).
   321	        return row_list, []
   322	
   323	    def _is_anchor(r: Any) -> bool:
   324	        if anchor_predicate is None:
   325	            return False
   326	        try:
   327	            return bool(anchor_predicate(r))
   328	        except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — a broken predicate must never quarantine an anchor
   329	            return False
   330	
   331	    candidates = [r for r in row_list if is_topic_unjudged(r) and not _is_anchor(r)]
   332	    if not candidates:
   333	        return row_list, []
   334	    max_fraction = _quarantine_max_fraction()
   335	    fraction = (len(candidates) / len(row_list)) if row_list else 0.0
   336	    if fraction > max_fraction:
   337	        logger.error(
   338	            "[weighted_enrichment] PG_QUARANTINE_UNJUDGED_TOPIC blast-radius guard TRIPPED: "
   339	            "would withhold %d/%d rows (%.1f%%) > ceiling %.1f%% — DISABLING quarantine for "
   340	            "this run and KEEPING ALL rows (fail-loud; a mass-withhold means the judge did not "
   341	            "actually stamp the corpus, so refusing to nuke it).",
   342	            len(candidates), len(row_list), 100.0 * fraction, 100.0 * max_fraction,
   343	        )
   344	        return row_list, []
   345	    quarantined_ids = {id(r) for r in candidates}
   346	    kept = [r for r in row_list if id(r) not in quarantined_ids]
   347	    logger.info(
   348	        "[weighted_enrichment] PG_QUARANTINE_UNJUDGED_TOPIC (%s): WITHHELD %d/%d unjudged-topic "
   349	        "row(s) from the finding surface (kept in evidence_pool + disclosed; faithfulness engine "
   350	        "untouched)",
   351	        _QUARANTINE_REASON, len(candidates), len(row_list),
   352	    )
   353	    return kept, candidates
   354	
   355	
   356	def breadth_enrichment_enabled() -> bool:
   357	    """True iff the default-OFF master flag is explicitly enabled (LAW VI)."""
   358	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_BREADTH_ENRICHMENT, "").strip().lower() in (
   359	        "1", "true", "on", "yes",
   360	    )
   361	
   362	
   363	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   364	# I-deepfix-001 (#1344 follow-on, M5) — PROMOTION-ELIGIBILITY PARTITION.
   365	#
   366	# drb_72 let near-zero-weight, single-origin, non-journal sources anchor standalone
   367	# numbered findings exactly like a corroborated NEJM/AEA source: cognifit blog
   368	# (weight 0.03), inboundlogistics (0.00), procom (0.01), protolabs (0.00), a wsu
   369	# blog (0.06), an IZA working paper (0.05), a predatory 10.5555 DOI (0.00), and an
   370	# off-topic 10.26163 DOI (0.00). Each is on-topic enough to span-verify (the body
   371	# sentence is verbatim from the source span, so it self-entails and PASSES the
   372	# UNCHANGED strict_verify), yet carries ~0 credibility weight and is corroborated by
   373	# nobody. Whether a source EARNED a top-level cited claim is a SURFACE-placement
   374	# (credibility / corroboration) decision, NOT a grounding decision — it is handled
   375	# here at the cite surface, NEVER in the frozen faithfulness engine.
   376	#
   377	# §-1.3 — WEIGHT-and-CONSOLIDATE, never FILTER-and-DROP: this is a ROUTING decision,
   378	# not a removal. A member is PROMOTED (earns a standalone cited claim) if ANY of:
   379	#   * corroboration >= K distinct verified origins (the CONSOLIDATE leg), OR
   380	#   * credibility weight >= W (the WEIGHT leg), OR
   381	#   * its host is a recognized peer-reviewed journal venue (over-demotion guard).
   382	# A single-origin AND below-W AND non-journal member is ROUTED to ``disclosed_only``:
   383	# KEPT in evidence_pool + the credibility disclosure + a dedicated report block, but
   384	# NOT promoted to a standalone numbered finding. Nothing is dropped; conservation holds
   385	# (promoted UNION disclosed_only == the original ordered list). The faithfulness engine
   386	# (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role D8 / span-grounding / provenance) is untouched — weight
   387	# and corroboration are credibility judgments, never a faithfulness gate. The OR-with-
   388	# corroboration leg IS the §-1.3 CONSOLIDATE principle (any source another agrees with is
   389	# rescued). Gated default-ON; ``PG_CWF_PROMOTION_ELIGIBILITY=0`` fails OPEN to promote-all
   390	# => the partition is byte-identical to the legacy keep-all-and-cite selection.
   391	_ENV_PROMOTION = "PG_CWF_PROMOTION_ELIGIBILITY"                 # default ON
   392	_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_WEIGHT = "PG_CWF_PROMOTION_MIN_WEIGHT"       # LAW VI override (default below)
   393	_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_CORROBORATION = "PG_CWF_PROMOTION_MIN_CORROBORATION"
   394	_DEFAULT_PROMOTION_MIN_WEIGHT = 0.10   # WEIGHT leg threshold (LAW VI overridable)
   395	_DEFAULT_PROMOTION_MIN_CORROBORATION = 2  # CONSOLIDATE leg: distinct verified origins (LAW VI overridable)
   396	_DISCLOSED_ONLY_REASON = "single_origin_low_weight_non_journal"
   397	
   398	# I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-C — OFF-TOPIC single-origin CITE gate (M5 promotion override).
   399	# drb_72 promoted single-origin spans whose direct quote shares ZERO topical content with the
   400	# research question (MWCNT/graphene materials-science, an unrelated NYSE-IPO CV blurb, a
   401	# corruption/poverty span) into standalone GenAI-labor findings. §-1.3 ROUTE-don't-DROP: such a
   402	# member is routed to ``disclosed_only`` (KEPT in evidence_pool + the credibility disclosure), not
   403	# deleted. FAIL-OPEN by construction — a member PROMOTES whenever ANY of: empty research_question /
   404	# gate OFF / the quote has < 6 content words (too terse to judge topicality) / ANY question-term
   405	# overlap > the min / corroborated (>= K verified origins). Only a corroborated-by-nobody,
   406	# >=6-word, ZERO-overlap span is demoted. The faithfulness engine is UNTOUCHED (topicality is a
   407	# credibility/surface judgment, never a grounding gate). Default-ON; OFF => promote-all =>
   408	# byte-identical to the pre-FIX-C partition.
   409	_ENV_PROMOTION_TOPICAL_GATE = "PG_CWF_PROMOTION_TOPICAL_GATE"              # default ON
   410	_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_TOPICAL_OVERLAP = "PG_CWF_PROMOTION_MIN_TOPICAL_OVERLAP"  # default 0.0 (LAW VI)
   411	_DEFAULT_PROMOTION_MIN_TOPICAL_OVERLAP = 0.0  # zero-overlap only (LAW VI overridable)
   412	_PROMOTION_TOPICAL_MIN_QUOTE_WORDS = 6  # a quote below this is too terse to judge -> keep-neutral promote
   413	
   414	
   415	def promotion_topical_gate_enabled() -> bool:
   416	    """Kill-switch ``PG_CWF_PROMOTION_TOPICAL_GATE`` (default ON). OFF => the off-topic demotion
   417	    override never fires => the promotion partition is byte-identical to pre-FIX-C."""
   418	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1369) FIX E — default-ON via the NEGATIVE idiom so an unset AND an empty-string
   419	    # value both read ON (matching the four fix-4-corrected CWF sub-flags). Force-on in the benchmark
   420	    # slate, so this is consistency hardening, not a live-behavior change.
   421	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_PROMOTION_TOPICAL_GATE, "1").strip().lower() not in (
   422	        "0", "false", "no", "off",
   423	    )

   425	
   426	def _parse_promotion_min_topical_overlap(raw: Any) -> float:
   427	    """The topical-overlap demotion threshold in [0.0, 1.0] (LAW VI). A member with quote-vs-question
   428	    overlap <= this (and >= 6 quote words and single-origin) is routed to disclosed-only. Garbage =>
   429	    ValueError (fail-loud, never swallowed)."""
   430	    if raw is None or not str(raw).strip():
   431	        value = _DEFAULT_PROMOTION_MIN_TOPICAL_OVERLAP
   432	    else:
   433	        try:
   434	            value = float(str(raw).strip())
   435	        except ValueError as e:
   436	            raise ValueError(
   437	                f"{_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_TOPICAL_OVERLAP} must be a float in [0.0, 1.0]; got {raw!r}"
   438	            ) from e
   439	    if not (0.0 <= value <= 1.0):
   440	        raise ValueError(
   441	            f"{_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_TOPICAL_OVERLAP} out of range [0.0, 1.0]: {value}"
   442	        )
   443	    return value
   444	
   445	
   446	def promotion_eligibility_enabled() -> bool:
   447	    """Kill-switch ``PG_CWF_PROMOTION_ELIGIBILITY`` (default ON). OFF => promote-all =>
   448	    the enrichment selection is byte-identical to the legacy keep-all-and-cite list."""
   449	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_PROMOTION, "1").strip().lower() in (
   450	        "1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled",
   451	    )

   454	def _parse_promotion_min_weight(raw: Any) -> float:
   455	    """The WEIGHT-leg threshold W in [0.0, 1.0] (LAW VI). Garbage => ValueError (fail-loud)."""
   456	    if raw is None or not str(raw).strip():
   457	        value = _DEFAULT_PROMOTION_MIN_WEIGHT
   458	    else:
   459	        try:
   460	            value = float(str(raw).strip())
   461	        except ValueError as e:
   462	            raise ValueError(
   463	                f"{_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_WEIGHT} must be a float in [0.0, 1.0]; got {raw!r}"
   464	            ) from e
   465	    if not (0.0 <= value <= 1.0):
   466	        raise ValueError(f"{_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_WEIGHT} out of range [0.0, 1.0]: {value}")
   467	    return value
   468	
   469	
   470	def _parse_promotion_min_corroboration(raw: Any) -> int:
   471	    """The CONSOLIDATE-leg threshold K (distinct verified origins), int >= 1 (LAW VI).
   472	    Garbage => ValueError (fail-loud)."""
   473	    if raw is None or not str(raw).strip():
   474	        return _DEFAULT_PROMOTION_MIN_CORROBORATION
   475	    try:
   476	        value = int(str(raw).strip())
   477	    except ValueError as e:
   478	        raise ValueError(
   479	            f"{_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_CORROBORATION} must be an int >= 1; got {raw!r}"
   480	        ) from e
   481	    if value < 1:
   482	        raise ValueError(f"{_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_CORROBORATION} must be >= 1: {value}")
   483	    return value

   485	
   486	def _host_is_known_journal(url: str) -> bool:
   487	    """Over-demotion guard: a recognized peer-reviewed journal article is ALWAYS
   488	    promotion-eligible regardless of weight, so a freak-low weight can never demote a
   489	    real journal. Pure read of the EXISTING ``PEER_REVIEWED_JOURNAL_DOMAINS`` weighting
   490	    table (a credibility classifier, not a faithfulness gate). Lazy import keeps this
   491	    module free of any retrieval-side dependency; any error fails-CLOSED (not a journal)
   492	    so the guard can only RESCUE, never accidentally demote."""
   493	    if not url:
   494	        return False
   495	    try:
   496	        from urllib.parse import urlparse
   497	
   498	        from src.polaris_graph.retrieval.tier_classifier import (
   499	            PEER_REVIEWED_JOURNAL_DOMAINS,
   500	            _domain_matches,
   501	        )
   502	
   503	        host = (urlparse(url).hostname or "").lower()
   504	        return bool(host) and _domain_matches(host, PEER_REVIEWED_JOURNAL_DOMAINS)
   505	    except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — guard fails CLOSED (treat as non-journal); never raises
   506	        return False
   507	
   508	
   509	def contract_bound_evidence_ids(contract_plans: Any) -> set[str]:
   510	    """The evidence_ids already inside the contract render universe (excluded from enrichment).
   511	
   512	    Robust against duck-typed plan shapes: unions a plan's ``ev_ids`` (the SectionPlan field
   513	    every contract plan mirrors) with every ``slot.entity_ids`` it carries. Missing attrs are
   514	    treated as empty so a shape change can NEVER over-exclude into an empty enrichment.
   515	    """
   516	    bound: set[str] = set()
   517	    for plan in contract_plans or ():
   518	        for eid in (getattr(plan, "ev_ids", None) or ()):
   519	            if eid:
   520	                bound.add(str(eid))
   521	        for slot in (getattr(plan, "slots", None) or ()):
   522	            for eid in (getattr(slot, "entity_ids", None) or ()):
   523	                if eid:
   524	                    bound.add(str(eid))
   525	    return bound
   526	
   527	
   528	# I-arch-007 #1264 CHOKE-FIX (observability): the enrichment had several independent silent-empty
   529	# exits (credibility None / no baskets / no SUPPORTS members at all / every SUPPORTS member already
   530	# bound or pool-absent) and the call site logged ONLY the success branch. That is why the operator
   531	# saw "zero appended weighted-enrichment section log lines in ALL reports" and could not tell WHICH
   532	# gate killed it. Each reason below is a stable machine-readable token the call site logs LOUDLY so a
   533	# no-op is never silent again.
   534	#
   535	# I-arch-007 #1264 had a FIFTH exit — "every remaining member below the relevance floor" — because
   536	# the selection HARD-DROPPED below-floor rows. I-arch-011 (B18) REMOVED that drop (keep-all-sort-
   537	# below-floor-last), so a below-floor row can NEVER cause an empty exit any more. The empty case is
   538	# now honestly one of: degraded credibility / no baskets / no SUPPORTS member / all bound-or-pool-
   539	# absent. The `_REASON_ALL_BELOW_FLOOR` token is therefore RETIRED (it can no longer be reached).
   540	_REASON_OK = "ok"
   541	_REASON_CREDIBILITY_NONE = "credibility_analysis_none"  # degrade / flag-off path
   542	_REASON_NO_BASKETS = "no_baskets"
   543	_REASON_NO_SUPPORTS_MEMBERS = "no_supports_members"  # baskets exist but no SUPPORTS member at all
   544	_REASON_ALL_BOUND_OR_ABSENT = "all_supports_bound_or_pool_absent"
   545	
   546	
   547	class UnboundSupportsSelection(NamedTuple):
   548	    """The selection result + a diagnostic breakdown of WHY it is what it is.
   549	
   550	    ``ev_ids`` is the FULL ordered surviving list (no cap, no floor drop). The counters make every
   551	    empty-exit auditable: the call site logs ``reason`` LOUDLY so a degraded credibility pass can
   552	    never silently no-op the breadth fix again. ALL counters are pure READS — nothing here touches a
   553	    faithfulness gate.
   554	
   555	    I-arch-011 (B18): ``excluded_below_floor`` is RETAINED as the field NAME (the call site at
   556	    multi_section_generator.py:6794/6822 reads it) but its MEANING is now pure TELEMETRY — the count
   557	    of KEPT rows that sit below ``PG_RELEVANCE_FLOOR`` (sorted LAST), NOT an exclusion. A below-floor
   558	    row is never dropped any more, so this counter can never reduce ``ev_ids``.
   559	    """
   560	    ev_ids: list[str]
   561	    reason: str
   562	    baskets_seen: int
   563	    supports_members_seen: int
   564	    excluded_bound: int
   565	    excluded_pool_absent: int
   566	    # I-arch-011 (B18): kept-but-below-floor count (telemetry); NOT an exclusion. Field name held
   567	    # stable for the out-of-lane consumer (multi_section_generator.py:6794/6822).
   568	    excluded_below_floor: int
   569	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1344) DEFER-1: evidence_ids of SUPPORTS members SUPPRESSED FROM
   570	    # CITATION because a SEMANTIC judge confirmed them OFF-topic (kept in
   571	    # evidence_pool + the credibility disclosure — never deleted, never a faithfulness
   572	    # change). Default () keeps the legacy 7-positional constructors valid + the OFF
   573	    # path (PG_OFFTOPIC_CITE_SUPPRESS=0 => empty) byte-identical. Pure TELEMETRY +
   574	    # the disclosed off-topic-excluded-from-citation set the call site surfaces.
   575	    offtopic_suppressed: tuple[str, ...] = ()
   576	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1344 M5): PROMOTION-ELIGIBILITY partition — the members ROUTED to
   577	    # DISCLOSED-ONLY (kept in evidence_pool + the credibility disclosure, re-surfaced in a
   578	    # dedicated report block, but NOT promoted to a standalone numbered finding) because each is
   579	    # single-origin (uncorroborated) AND below the credibility-weight bar AND not a recognized
   580	    # journal venue. Each record: ``{evidence_id, source_url, source_tier, credibility_weight,
   581	    # reason}``. Append-only LAST field (default () keeps every legacy positional constructor valid
   582	    # AND the OFF path byte-identical). NOT a drop — a ROUTE; conservation holds (``ev_ids`` UNION
   583	    # ``disclosed_only`` == the full ordered list); the faithfulness engine is untouched.
   584	    disclosed_only: tuple[dict[str, Any], ...] = ()
   585	
   586	
   587	# I-deepfix-001 WS-8 (D4) part 2: COMPOSITION-ordering recency leg. The bibliography re-rank alone did not
   588	# stop the headline breach (Codex: the 1986 source headlined from the selection/composition path). This
   589	# demotes an OLD source in the unbound-supports selection ORDERING so it no longer anchors a top finding —
   590	# a WEIGHT on the sort key only, NEVER a filter (the full list is kept; nothing is dropped/capped — §-1.3).
   591	# Journal-class only: gated on PG_DOCUMENT_TYPE_WEIGHT (the journal-class signal, same as the bib re-rank)
   592	# AND PG_COMPOSITION_RECENCY (default-ON); OFF, non-journal-class, or unknown/absent year => factor 1.0 =>
   593	# byte-identical ordering. Reuses the SAME env-tunable curve as the bibliography leg (PG_M2_RECENCY_*).
   594	_COMPOSITION_RECENCY_ENV = "PG_COMPOSITION_RECENCY"
   595	_WE_YEAR_RE = re.compile(r"\b(?:19|20)\d{2}\b")
   596	
   597	
   598	def _composition_recency_enabled() -> bool:
   599	    """Journal-class gate: the composition recency leg fires only when PG_DOCUMENT_TYPE_WEIGHT is ON (the
   600	    journal-class run signal) AND PG_COMPOSITION_RECENCY is not disabled (default-ON)."""
   601	    dtw = os.environ.get("PG_DOCUMENT_TYPE_WEIGHT", "").strip().lower() in ("1", "true", "on", "yes")
   602	    comp = os.environ.get(_COMPOSITION_RECENCY_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "no", "off")
   603	    return dtw and comp
   604	
   605	
   606	def _we_publication_year(entry: "dict | None") -> "int | None":
   607	    """Publication year of an evidence-pool entry: an explicit year field, else the first plausible
   608	    4-digit year in title/statement/direct_quote/url/doi. None when none found (=> no penalty)."""
   609	    if not isinstance(entry, dict):
   610	        return None
   611	    for k in ("year", "publication_year", "pub_year"):
   612	        v = entry.get(k)
   613	        if v is None:
   614	            continue
   615	        try:
   616	            y = int(str(v).strip()[:4])
   617	        except (TypeError, ValueError):
   618	            continue
   619	        if 1500 <= y <= 2100:
   620	            return y
   621	    for k in ("title", "statement", "direct_quote", "url", "doi"):
   622	        m = _WE_YEAR_RE.search(str(entry.get(k) or ""))
   623	        if m:
   624	            y = int(m.group(0))
   625	            if 1500 <= y <= 2100:
   626	                return y
   627	    return None
   628	
   629	
   630	def _we_recency_factor(year: "int | None", reference_year: "int | None") -> float:
   631	    """A [floor, 1.0] ordering multiplier: 1.0 within ``grace`` years of the corpus-newest source, decaying
   632	    linearly by ``decay`` per year older, FLOORED (an old source is DEMOTED for headline order, never
   633	    dropped). Same env curve as the bibliography leg. Missing year / disabled => 1.0."""
   634	    if year is None or reference_year is None or not _composition_recency_enabled():
   635	        return 1.0
   636	    try:
   637	        grace = int(os.getenv("PG_M2_RECENCY_GRACE_YEARS", "5"))
   638	        decay = float(os.getenv("PG_M2_RECENCY_DECAY_PER_YEAR", "0.02"))
   639	        floor = float(os.getenv("PG_M2_RECENCY_FLOOR", "0.25"))
   640	    except (TypeError, ValueError):
   641	        grace, decay, floor = 5, 0.02, 0.25
   642	    age = max(0, int(reference_year) - int(year) - grace)
   643	    return max(floor, 1.0 - decay * age)
   644	
   645	
   646	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   647	# I-deepfix-001 (U9) — TOPICAL question-overlap ORDERING weight.
   648	#
   649	# THE BUG (drb_72 AI-labor cited logistics blogs; a PD-DBS run cited elder-abuse
   650	# sources): query-decomposition emits off-topic sub-queries and the ONLY per-row
   651	# relevance signal on the surfacing path is ``selection_relevance`` — a per-passage
   652	# SEMANTIC score. A semantically-fluent but topically-foreign passage (a
   653	# supply-chain article that reads coherently) can score a high ``selection_relevance``
   654	# and, being the PRIMARY sort key here, WRRF-fuse to the TOP of the cited breadth
   655	# surface — so an off-topic source LEADS the findings. The semantic score does not
   656	# capture whether the source is ABOUT the research question's topic.
   657	#
   658	# THE FIX — §-1.3 WEIGHT, DON'T FILTER: add a second, TOPICAL relevance signal —
   659	# the lexical overlap between the source text and the research-question topic terms —
   660	# as an ORDERING multiplier on the existing relevance sort key. An off-topic source
   661	# (near-zero question-term overlap) is DEMOTED in the order (its relevance key is
   662	# scaled toward ``PG_TOPICAL_RELEVANCE_FLOOR``) so it no longer top-fuses, while an
   663	# on-topic source keeps its full relevance key. This is a pure RE-ORDER over the
   664	# SAME kept set — NOTHING is dropped, capped, or thinned; conservation holds (the
   665	# returned ev_ids are the identical set, only re-ordered). It is the exact same class
   666	# as the WS-8 recency ordering leg above and the ``key_findings`` sentence-relevance
   667	# re-order weight, and it reuses the EXISTING grounding tokenizer
   668	# (``provenance_generator._content_words``) — no new model, no new word list, no spend.
   669	# The faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role D8 / span-grounding /
   670	# provenance) is UNTOUCHED. Default-ON, gated by ``PG_TOPICAL_RELEVANCE_WEIGHT``; an
   671	# empty ``research_question`` (every legacy caller) or the gate OFF => factor 1.0 for
   672	# every row => byte-identical legacy ordering.
   673	_ENV_TOPICAL_RELEVANCE_WEIGHT = "PG_TOPICAL_RELEVANCE_WEIGHT"
   674	_ENV_TOPICAL_RELEVANCE_FLOOR = "PG_TOPICAL_RELEVANCE_FLOOR"
   675	# The row text fields scanned for question-term overlap (the same source-content
   676	# fields finding_dedup / provenance read). Read-only; order-insensitive.
   677	_TOPIC_TEXT_FIELDS = (
   678	    "title", "statement", "claim", "direct_quote", "snippet", "summary", "text", "body",
   679	)
   680	
   681	
   682	def topical_relevance_weight_enabled() -> bool:
   683	    """Kill-switch ``PG_TOPICAL_RELEVANCE_WEIGHT`` (default ON). OFF => every topical
   684	    factor is 1.0 => the surfacing ORDER is byte-identical to the legacy ordering."""
   685	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_TOPICAL_RELEVANCE_WEIGHT, "1").strip().lower() not in (
   686	        "0", "false", "no", "off",
   687	    )
   688	
   689	
   690	def _topical_relevance_floor() -> float:
   691	    """The [floor, 1.0] ORDERING multiplier's lower bound for a zero-overlap (off-topic)
   692	    row. Default 0.25 (an off-topic row keeps at most 25% of its relevance sort value, so
   693	    it sinks below every on-topic row — a DEMOTION, never a drop). A garbage value is an
   694	    operator config error and raises ValueError (LAW VI: fail-loud, never swallowed)."""
   695	    raw = os.environ.get(_ENV_TOPICAL_RELEVANCE_FLOOR)
   696	    if raw is None or not str(raw).strip():
   697	        return 0.25
   698	    val = float(raw)  # ValueError on garbage: fail loud
   699	    if not (0.0 <= val <= 1.0):
   700	        raise ValueError(
   701	            f"{_ENV_TOPICAL_RELEVANCE_FLOOR} must be in [0.0, 1.0]; got {val!r}"
   702	        )
   703	    return val
   704	
   705	
   706	def _question_topic_terms(research_question: str) -> frozenset[str]:
   707	    """Content-word topic terms of the research question, or an empty set when the
   708	    question is blank / has no content words (=> topical factor 1.0 => byte-identical).
   709	    Reuses the EXISTING grounding tokenizer (alphabetic, >=3 chars, stopword-stripped);
   710	    imported LAZILY (mirrors ``key_findings``) so this module keeps its import-time
   711	    independence. PURE — no network, no GPU, no LLM."""
   712	    if not research_question or not research_question.strip():
   713	        return frozenset()
   714	    from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (  # noqa: PLC0415
   715	        _content_words,
   716	    )
   717	    return frozenset(_content_words(research_question))
   718	
   719	
   720	def _topical_overlap(row: Any, question_terms: frozenset[str]) -> float:
   721	    """Overlap coefficient of the row's source text against the question topic terms:
   722	    ``|row_terms & question_terms| / |question_terms|`` in [0.0, 1.0]. Returns 1.0
   723	    (keep-neutral) when there are no question terms; 0.0 when the row carries no usable
   724	    text. A missing row (not a dict) is keep-neutral (1.0) — pool membership already
   725	    implies the row passed the upstream retrieval relevance gate once. PURE."""
   726	    if not question_terms:
   727	        return 1.0
   728	    if not isinstance(row, dict):
   729	        return 1.0
   730	    from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (  # noqa: PLC0415
   731	        _content_words,
   732	    )
   733	    parts = [str(row.get(f) or "") for f in _TOPIC_TEXT_FIELDS]
   734	    row_terms = _content_words(" ".join(p for p in parts if p))
   735	    if not row_terms:
   736	        return 0.0
   737	    return len(row_terms & question_terms) / len(question_terms)
   738	
   739	
   740	def _topical_factor(overlap: float, floor: float) -> float:
   741	    """Map a question-topic overlap in [0.0, 1.0] to a [floor, 1.0] ORDERING multiplier:
   742	    overlap 1.0 => 1.0 (on-topic, full weight), overlap 0.0 => ``floor`` (off-topic,
   743	    demoted but KEPT). Linear so the demotion is monotone in topicality."""
   744	    ov = max(0.0, min(1.0, overlap))
   745	    return floor + (1.0 - floor) * ov
   746	
   747	
   748	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   749	# I-deepfix-001 (#1344 SPAN-TOPICALITY) — HIGH-PRECISION, fail-OPEN per-SPAN
   750	# off-topic WITHHOLD (§-1.3 WITHHOLD-and-disclose per span; the SOURCE is NEVER
   751	# dropped — it stays in evidence_pool + the credibility disclosure, and every other
   752	# span it carries still cites; the frozen faithfulness engine strict_verify / NLI /
   753	# 4-role D8 / provenance / span-grounding is UNTOUCHED).
   754	#
   755	# PRIOR-FIX DEFECT (Codex P1): the first cut flagged a span off-topic whenever it
   756	# shared ZERO exact ``_content_words`` with ONLY the top-level research question. That
   757	# over-withheld genuinely on-topic spans that phrase the topic with SYNONYMS, ACRONYMS,
   758	# ENTITY NAMES, or lower-level terms (a "labor" question vs an on-topic span about
   759	# "automation exposure in clerical occupations"; a "GLP-1 obesity" question vs a
   760	# "semaglutide reduces BMI" span). If every one of a source's spans missed the exact
   761	# question vocabulary the whole source silently vanished from citation though on-topic.
   762	#
   763	# PRECISION-SAFE REWRITE: a span is CONFIDENTLY foreign ONLY when it shares nothing with
   764	# EITHER of TWO references — (1) the research-question topic terms AND (2) the source's
   765	# OWN rich local topic (its title/metadata fields UNIONED with every SIBLING span's
   766	# content words). A synonym/acronym/entity/lower-level on-topic span still shares
   767	# vocabulary with the rest of its OWN coherent document, so it clears reference (2) and
   768	# is KEPT. Only a paragraph foreign to the question AND to its own document — a Gaza-
   769	# ceasefire sentence embedded in an AI-labor report — is WITHHELD. Every ambiguity
   770	# fails OPEN (KEEP): empty question, a short span, a thin local reference, or ANY shared
   771	# term on EITHER reference. This never nukes an off-topic SOURCE (its spans share the
   772	# source's own dominant topic, so they are all KEPT — the source's fate is decided at
   773	# the basket/source level by ``_is_confirmed_offtopic``, not here). Gated default-ON;
   774	# ``PG_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_SUPPRESS=0`` restores the byte-identical legacy keep-all behaviour.
   775	_ENV_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_SUPPRESS = "PG_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_SUPPRESS"                    # default ON
   776	_ENV_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_MIN_CONTENT_WORDS = "PG_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_MIN_CONTENT_WORDS"  # LAW VI override
   777	_ENV_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_MIN_LOCAL_TERMS = "PG_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_MIN_LOCAL_TERMS"      # LAW VI override
   778	# A span shorter than this many content words is too terse to judge foreign confidently
   779	# => KEEP (fail-open). A local reference (title + siblings) thinner than the min-local
   780	# floor cannot attest the source's topic reliably => KEEP (fail-open).
   781	_DEFAULT_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_MIN_CONTENT_WORDS = 6
   782	_DEFAULT_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_MIN_LOCAL_TERMS = 8
   783	# The source's TITLE / METADATA fields that describe its dominant topic. DELIBERATELY
   784	# EXCLUDES the quote-body fields (``direct_quote`` / ``statement`` / ``text`` / ``body``
   785	# that ``_TOPIC_TEXT_FIELDS`` carries): the spans being judged ARE the quote body, so
   786	# folding it into the local reference would make every span trivially self-overlap and
   787	# silently NO-OP the gate. The source's OTHER spans are the SIBLING reference, added
   788	# separately in ``_withhold_offtopic_spans``.
   789	_SOURCE_TOPIC_TITLE_FIELDS = (
   790	    "source_title", "title", "page_title", "name", "section_title",
   791	    "topic", "subject", "keywords",
   792	)
   793	
   794	
   795	def offtopic_span_suppress_enabled() -> bool:
   796	    """Kill-switch ``PG_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_SUPPRESS`` (default ON). OFF => no span is ever
   797	    withheld on topicality => byte-identical to the legacy keep-all cite behaviour."""
   798	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_SUPPRESS, "1").strip().lower() not in (
   799	        "0", "false", "no", "off",
   800	    )
   801	
   802	
   803	def _env_positive_int(name: str, default: int) -> int:
   804	    """Parse a positive-int env override (fail LOUD on garbage per LAW VI); unset => default."""
   805	    raw = os.environ.get(name)
   806	    if raw is None or not str(raw).strip():
   807	        return default
   808	    try:
   809	        val = int(str(raw).strip())
   810	    except ValueError as e:
   811	        raise ValueError(f"{name} must be an int >= 1; got {raw!r}") from e
   812	    if val < 1:
   813	        raise ValueError(f"{name} must be >= 1: {val}")
   814	    return val
   815	
   816	
   817	def _offtopic_span_min_content_words() -> int:
   818	    return _env_positive_int(
   819	        _ENV_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_MIN_CONTENT_WORDS, _DEFAULT_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_MIN_CONTENT_WORDS
   820	    )
   821	
   822	
   823	def _offtopic_span_min_local_terms() -> int:
   824	    return _env_positive_int(
   825	        _ENV_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_MIN_LOCAL_TERMS, _DEFAULT_OFFTOPIC_SPAN_MIN_LOCAL_TERMS
   826	    )
   827	
   828	
   829	def _span_is_confidently_offtopic(
   830	    unit_terms: "frozenset[str] | set[str]",
   831	    question_terms: "frozenset[str] | set[str]",
   832	    local_topic_terms: "frozenset[str] | set[str]",
   833	    min_content_words: int,
   834	    min_local_terms: int,
   835	) -> bool:
   836	    """True ONLY when a span is CONFIDENTLY foreign to BOTH the research question AND its
   837	    OWN source's rich local topic. Every ambiguity fails OPEN (returns False => KEEP)."""
   838	    if not question_terms:
   839	        return False                        # no question topic => never judge => KEEP
   840	    if len(unit_terms) < min_content_words:
   841	        return False                        # span too terse to judge => KEEP
   842	    if unit_terms & question_terms:
   843	        return False                        # shares a QUESTION term => on-topic => KEEP
   844	    if len(local_topic_terms) < min_local_terms:
   845	        return False                        # local reference too thin to judge => KEEP
   846	    if unit_terms & local_topic_terms:
   847	        return False                        # coherent with its OWN document => KEEP
   848	    # Zero overlap with the question AND with the source's own dominant topic: a genuinely
   849	    # foreign paragraph (a Gaza-ceasefire sentence in an AI-labor report) => WITHHOLD.
   850	    return True
   851	
   852	
   853	def _corpus_topic_terms(pool: "dict[str, Any]") -> "dict[str, int]":
   854	    """Map each on-topic content word to the NUMBER OF DISTINCT SOURCES that contain it
   855	    (across every source's title/metadata fields + quote body). The per-span off-topic
   856	    gate treats a word as shared corpus vocabulary only when it appears in a source OTHER
   857	    than the one being judged (Codex iter-2 P1: a plain union self-overlaps because a
   858	    source's own quote is in it, which would keep every span incl a foreign one). Counting
   859	    distinct sources lets the gate subtract the current source's SOLE-authored words while
   860	    retaining genuinely shared on-topic vocabulary. Computed once per pass."""
   861	    from collections import Counter  # noqa: PLC0415
   862	    from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (  # noqa: PLC0415
   863	        _content_words,
   864	    )
   865	    counts: "Counter[str]" = Counter()
   866	    for ev in (pool or {}).values():
   867	        if not isinstance(ev, dict):
   868	            continue
   869	        source_terms = set(
   870	            _content_words(
   871	                " ".join(str(ev.get(f) or "") for f in _SOURCE_TOPIC_TITLE_FIELDS)
   872	            )
   873	        )
   874	        source_terms |= set(_content_words(str(_member_quote(ev) or "")))
   875	        for term in source_terms:
   876	            counts[term] += 1
   877	    return dict(counts)
   878	
   879	
   880	def _withhold_offtopic_spans(
   881	    units: "list[str]",
   882	    ev: "dict[str, Any]",
   883	    question_terms: "frozenset[str] | set[str]",
   884	    min_content_words: int,
   885	    min_local_terms: int,
   886	    corpus_topic_terms: "frozenset[str] | set[str] | None" = None,
   887	) -> "list[str]":
   888	    """Return ``units`` with CONFIDENTLY-foreign spans withheld from CITATION (fail-open).
   889	
   890	    Builds the source's RICH local topic reference ONCE — its title/metadata fields
   891	    (``_SOURCE_TOPIC_TITLE_FIELDS``, which EXCLUDE the quote body) UNIONED with the
   892	    content words of the source's OTHER spans — then keeps every span except those
   893	    foreign to BOTH the question and that reference. No question terms / no units =>
   894	    unchanged (byte-identical). The source is never dropped; the frozen faithfulness
   895	    engine is never touched (this only chooses which verbatim spans of an already-
   896	    verified source are surfaced as citations)."""
   897	    if not question_terms or not units:
   898	        return units
   899	    from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (  # noqa: PLC0415
   900	        _content_words,
   901	    )
   902	    title_terms = _content_words(
   903	        " ".join(str((ev or {}).get(f) or "") for f in _SOURCE_TOPIC_TITLE_FIELDS)
   904	    )
   905	    unit_terms = [set(_content_words(u or "")) for u in units]
   906	    # Codex-P1 (iter 2 -> iter 3) answer: a span is withheld only when it is foreign to the
   907	    # OTHER sources' established on-topic vocabulary. `corpus_topic_terms` maps each word to
   908	    # the number of DISTINCT sources containing it; the current source's OWN words (title +
   909	    # every unit) are excluded unless another source ALSO uses them. This KEEPS a lower-level
   910	    # / synonym / entity on-topic span ("clerical occupations": occupations/workers appear in
   911	    # OTHER sources -> retained) while a truly foreign span (a Gaza-ceasefire sentence whose
   912	    # gaza/ceasefire/hostages words appear in NO other source) is still WITHHELD. Without this
   913	    # subtraction the source's own quote self-overlaps and the gate keeps everything.
   914	    corpus_counts: "dict[str, int]" = dict(corpus_topic_terms or {})
   915	    own_terms: set = set(title_terms)
   916	    for terms in unit_terms:
   917	        own_terms |= terms
   918	    corpus_ref: set = {
   919	        w for w, c in corpus_counts.items()
   920	        if c > (1 if w in own_terms else 0)
   921	    }
   922	    kept: list[str] = []
   923	    for i, unit in enumerate(units):
   924	        # Local reference = title/metadata terms + EVERY OTHER span's terms (never this
   925	        # span's own words, which would self-overlap and defeat the foreign test). A
   926	        # synonym/acronym on-topic span shares vocabulary with a sibling span here.
   927	        sibling_terms: set[str] = set()
   928	        for j, terms in enumerate(unit_terms):
   929	            if j != i:
   930	                sibling_terms |= terms
   931	        local_ref = title_terms | sibling_terms | corpus_ref
   932	        if _span_is_confidently_offtopic(
   933	            unit_terms[i], question_terms, local_ref, min_content_words, min_local_terms
   934	        ):
   935	            logger.info(
   936	                "[weighted_enrichment] I-deepfix-001 SPAN-TOPICALITY: WITHHELD "
   937	                "confidently-foreign span from citation (source kept in evidence_pool + "
   938	                "disclosure; faithfulness engine untouched): %r",
   939	                (unit or "")[:160],
   940	            )
   941	            continue
   942	        kept.append(unit)
   943	    # FAIL-OPEN SAFETY (Codex-P1 answer): the span gate must NEVER empty a source. If
   944	    # every span was judged foreign (a pathological source of only-unrelated paragraphs),
   945	    # KEEP the source's spans unchanged — a source's fate is decided at the basket/source
   946	    # level (``_is_confirmed_offtopic``), never by this per-span citation gate.
   947	    if not kept:
   948	        return units
   949	    return kept
   950	
   951	
   952	def diagnose_unbound_supports_selection(
   953	    *,
   954	    evidence_pool: Any,
   955	    credibility_analysis: Any,
   956	    contract_plans: Any,
   957	    research_question: str = "",
   958	) -> UnboundSupportsSelection:
   959	    """``select_unbound_supports_by_weight`` + a diagnostic breakdown (the same selection logic).
   960	
   961	    Identical surviving list + ordering as ``select_unbound_supports_by_weight`` (which delegates
   962	    here), PLUS the per-exit counters that make a silent no-op impossible. Faithfulness-neutral:
   963	    this only READS already-computed state; it surfaces nothing into the report by itself.
   964	    """
   965	    if credibility_analysis is None:
   966	        return UnboundSupportsSelection([], _REASON_CREDIBILITY_NONE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
   967	    baskets = getattr(credibility_analysis, "baskets", None) or []
   968	    if not baskets:
   969	        return UnboundSupportsSelection([], _REASON_NO_BASKETS, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
   970	    bound = contract_bound_evidence_ids(contract_plans)
   971	    pool = evidence_pool or {}
   972	
   973	    # EXISTING relevance gate (no new constant): reuse the retrieval gate's parser so the breadth
   974	    # surfacing applies the SAME PG_RELEVANCE_FLOOR (default 0.30) + the SAME fail-loud (0.0, 1.0]
   975	    # validation. Lazy import (reading, not a cross-module edit) mirrors live_retriever.py:3186.
   976	    from src.polaris_graph.retrieval.evidence_selector import parse_relevance_floor
   977	
   978	    relevance_floor = parse_relevance_floor(os.environ.get("PG_RELEVANCE_FLOOR"))
   979	
   980	    # Per-eid: the HIGHEST basket weight_mass it appears under (ordering only, never a filter) and
   981	    # its topicality score for the relevance-first ordering.
   982	    best_weight: dict[str, float] = {}
   983	    relevance_by_eid: dict[str, float | None] = {}
   984	    supports_members_seen = 0
   985	    excluded_bound = 0
   986	    excluded_pool_absent = 0
   987	    below_floor_count = 0  # I-arch-011 (B18): KEPT-but-below-floor (telemetry); NEVER an exclusion.
   988	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1344) DEFER-1: SEMANTIC confirmed-OFF members withheld from the
   989	    # CITED breadth surface (kept in pool + disclosure; NOT a faithfulness change).
   990	    suppress_offtopic = offtopic_cite_suppress_enabled()
   991	    offtopic_suppressed: list[str] = []
   992	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1344 M5) PROMOTION-ELIGIBILITY accumulators (most-favorable-to-promotion so
   993	    # any demotion is conservative): per-eid the MAX member ``credibility_weight`` seen (absent =>
   994	    # unknown => keep-neutral promote), the MAX basket ``verified_support_origin_count`` (the
   995	    # CONSOLIDATE leg), whether ANY member's host is a recognized peer-reviewed journal venue (the
   996	    # over-demotion guard), and a tier label for the disclosure surface. Pure READS of already-
   997	    # computed credibility state — no faithfulness gate is touched.
   998	    best_cred_weight: dict[str, float] = {}
   999	    max_origin: dict[str, int] = {}
  1000	    is_journal: dict[str, bool] = {}
  1001	    best_tier: dict[str, str] = {}
  1002	    # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-C: per-eid topical signals for the off-topic promotion override.
  1003	    # ``q_terms`` is the question's content-word topic set (empty => fail-open promote-all).
  1004	    # ``best_quote_overlap`` = MAX quote-vs-question overlap; ``quote_words`` = quote content-word
  1005	    # count. Computed ONLY when the gate is enabled (else empty => the override never fires).
  1006	    _promo_topical_gate = promotion_topical_gate_enabled()
  1007	    _promo_q_terms = _question_topic_terms(research_question) if _promo_topical_gate else frozenset()
  1008	    best_quote_overlap: dict[str, float] = {}
  1009	    quote_words: dict[str, int] = {}
  1010	    for basket in baskets:
  1011	        try:
  1012	            weight = float(getattr(basket, "weight_mass", 0.0) or 0.0)
  1013	        except (TypeError, ValueError):
  1014	            weight = 0.0
  1015	        # I-deepfix-001 (#1344 M5): the basket's distinct isolated-verified origin count (the
  1016	        # CONSOLIDATE-leg signal). Non-int / missing => 0 (conservative: no corroboration credit).
  1017	        try:
  1018	            verified_origin = int(getattr(basket, "verified_support_origin_count", 0) or 0)
  1019	        except (TypeError, ValueError):
  1020	            verified_origin = 0
  1021	        for member in (getattr(basket, "supporting_members", None) or ()):
  1022	            if str(getattr(member, "span_verdict", "")).strip().upper() != _SUPPORTS:
  1023	                continue  # CONSOLIDATE: only isolated-verified SUPPORTS members are offered
  1024	            supports_members_seen += 1
  1025	            eid = str(getattr(member, "evidence_id", "") or "")
  1026	            if not eid:
  1027	                continue
  1028	            if eid in bound:
  1029	                excluded_bound += 1
  1030	                continue
  1031	            if eid not in pool:
  1032	                excluded_pool_absent += 1
  1033	                continue
  1034	            # I-deepfix-001 (#1344) DEFER-1: a member a SEMANTIC judge confirmed OFF-topic
  1035	            # (topic-gate / W2 label) is WITHHELD FROM CITATION — not surfaced into the
  1036	            # breadth section's ev_ids, so the bibliography numberer never assigns it [N].
  1037	            # §-1.3-SAFE: it is NOT a lexical ``relevance < floor`` drop (that is the banned
  1038	            # keystone DROP); it keys ONLY on the confirmed-OFF verdict, and the source STAYS
  1039	            # in evidence_pool + the credibility disclosure (kept-and-disclosed, never deleted).
  1040	            # The faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role / span-grounding) is
  1041	            # untouched. OFF (PG_OFFTOPIC_CITE_SUPPRESS=0) => no member is skipped => the
  1042	            # ev_ids list is byte-identical to the legacy keep-all-and-cite behaviour.
  1043	            if suppress_offtopic and _is_confirmed_offtopic(pool.get(eid)):
  1044	                offtopic_suppressed.append(eid)
  1045	                continue
  1046	            # I-arch-011 (B18) — WEIGHT, DON'T FILTER (§-1.3, the keystone): the pre-fix code
  1047	            # RE-IMPOSED a hard ``relevance < floor`` DROP here — the FILTER-AND-CAP anti-pattern the
  1048	            # selector docstring (evidence_selector.py:1944-1953) forbids, which killed 729/746
  1049	            # unbound SUPPORTS. KEEP-ALL-AND-SORT-BELOW-FLOOR-LAST: a below-floor row is NEVER
  1050	            # excluded; it is KEPT and demoted in the ORDER (sorted last) exactly the way the
  1051	            # retrieval pool down-weights a below-floor row (evidence_selector.py:2066-2070). A
  1052	            # missing/unparseable score is keep-neutral (sentinel 0.0), NOT below-floor — pool
  1053	            # membership already implies the retrieval floor passed once. ``below_floor_count`` is
  1054	            # pure telemetry: how many KEPT rows sit below the floor, never an exclusion. The ONLY
  1055	            # hard gate is the UNCHANGED strict_verify each surfaced sentence still must pass.
  1056	            relevance = _row_relevance(pool.get(eid))
  1057	            if relevance is not None and relevance < relevance_floor:
  1058	                below_floor_count += 1  # KEPT (sorts last), never dropped
  1059	            if eid not in best_weight or weight > best_weight[eid]:
  1060	                best_weight[eid] = weight
  1061	            # First-seen relevance is deterministic across baskets (same row); keep it stable.
  1062	            relevance_by_eid.setdefault(eid, relevance)
  1063	            # I-deepfix-001 (#1344 M5): accumulate the promotion-eligibility signals for this eid
  1064	            # (most-favorable-to-promotion). ``credibility_weight`` is the MEMBER's own credibility
  1065	            # (BasketMember.credibility_weight); None/unparseable is left unknown (=> promote-neutral).
  1066	            _mw = getattr(member, "credibility_weight", None)
  1067	            if _mw is not None:
  1068	                try:
  1069	                    _mw = float(_mw)
  1070	                except (TypeError, ValueError):
  1071	                    _mw = None
  1072	            if _mw is not None:
  1073	                _prev_w = best_cred_weight.get(eid)
  1074	                best_cred_weight[eid] = _mw if _prev_w is None else max(_prev_w, _mw)
  1075	            if verified_origin > max_origin.get(eid, 0):
  1076	                max_origin[eid] = verified_origin
  1077	            if not is_journal.get(eid, False):
  1078	                _murl = str(getattr(member, "source_url", "") or "") or str(
  1079	                    (pool.get(eid) or {}).get("source_url")
  1080	                    or (pool.get(eid) or {}).get("url")
  1081	                    or ""
  1082	                )
  1083	                if _host_is_known_journal(_murl):
  1084	                    is_journal[eid] = True
  1085	            if not best_tier.get(eid):
  1086	                _mt = str(getattr(member, "source_tier", "") or "")
  1087	                if _mt:
  1088	                    best_tier[eid] = _mt
  1089	            # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-C: quote-vs-question topical overlap + quote content-word
  1090	            # count for the off-topic promotion override. Computed once per eid (the member quote
  1091	            # is stable across baskets); only when the gate is enabled and the question has terms.
  1092	            if _promo_topical_gate and _promo_q_terms and eid not in quote_words:
  1093	                from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (  # noqa: PLC0415
  1094	                    _content_words,
  1095	                )
  1096	                _qw = set(_content_words(str(_member_quote(pool.get(eid)) or "")))
  1097	                quote_words[eid] = len(_qw)
  1098	                best_quote_overlap[eid] = len(_qw & _promo_q_terms) / len(_promo_q_terms)
  1099	
  1100	    # I-arch-011 (B18) ORDER, KEEP-ALL-SORT-BELOW-FLOOR-LAST:
  1101	    #   1. ``is_below_floor`` (False before True) — a PRESENT-and-below-floor row sorts AFTER every
  1102	    #      at/above-floor row AND after every missing-relevance row (a missing score is keep-neutral,
  1103	    #      NOT below-floor, so it ranks ahead of a genuine below-floor row).
  1104	    #   2. relevance-to-question DESC (within the same below-floor bucket).
  1105	    #   3. weight_mass DESC (priority of consideration).
  1106	    #   4. evidence_id (deterministic tiebreak).
  1107	    # A missing relevance uses the CONSTANT sentinel (0.0) and ``is_below_floor=False`` so a pool of
  1108	    # all-missing-relevance rows reproduces today's pure weight-desc order. FULL list — no cap/top-N,
  1109	    # no floor DROP.
  1110	    def _is_below_floor(eid: str) -> bool:
  1111	        rel = relevance_by_eid.get(eid)
  1112	        return rel is not None and rel < relevance_floor
  1113	
  1114	    # WS-8 (D4) part 2: corpus-relative recency factor applied to the weight_mass ORDERING term (never to
  1115	    # relevance, never a filter). Journal-class only + byte-identical when off/unknown-year. Computed once.
  1116	    _year_by_eid = {eid: _we_publication_year(pool.get(eid)) for eid in best_weight}
  1117	    _years = [y for y in _year_by_eid.values() if y is not None]
  1118	    _ref_year = max(_years) if _years else None
  1119	
  1120	    # I-deepfix-001 (U9): TOPICAL question-overlap ORDERING factor, computed once. Multiplies the
  1121	    # relevance sort key (a WEIGHT on the order, never a filter): an off-topic row (near-zero question-
  1122	    # term overlap) is DEMOTED toward the floor so it no longer top-fuses, while an on-topic row keeps
  1123	    # its full relevance key. Gate OFF or empty ``research_question`` => empty term set => factor 1.0 for
  1124	    # every row => byte-identical legacy ordering. The full kept set is preserved (nothing dropped).
  1125	    _q_terms = (
  1126	        _question_topic_terms(research_question)
  1127	        if topical_relevance_weight_enabled()
  1128	        else frozenset()
  1129	    )
  1130	    _topical_floor = _topical_relevance_floor()
  1131	    _topical_factor_by_eid = {
  1132	        eid: _topical_factor(_topical_overlap(pool.get(eid), _q_terms), _topical_floor)
  1133	        for eid in best_weight
  1134	    }
  1135	
  1136	    ev_ids = [
  1137	        eid
  1138	        for eid, _ in sorted(
  1139	            best_weight.items(),
  1140	            key=lambda kv: (
  1141	                _is_below_floor(kv[0]),                       # False (0) before True (1)
  1142	                # I-deepfix-001 (U9): relevance sort key scaled by the TOPICAL question-overlap factor
  1143	                # (demotes an off-topic row within its bucket; factor 1.0 when the leg is off / no
  1144	                # question / no question terms => byte-identical). §-1.3 WEIGHT, never a drop.
  1145	                -(_relevance_sort_key(relevance_by_eid.get(kv[0]))
  1146	                  * _topical_factor_by_eid.get(kv[0], 1.0)),
  1147	                # WS-8 (D4): demote an OLD source in the weight_mass ordering (still kept — §-1.3); factor
  1148	                # 1.0 when the recency leg is off / non-journal-class / year unknown => byte-identical.
  1149	                -(kv[1] * _we_recency_factor(_year_by_eid.get(kv[0]), _ref_year)),
  1150	                kv[0],
  1151	            ),
  1152	        )
  1153	    ]
  1154	
  1155	    # I-arch-011 (B18): the empty case can no longer be "all below floor" (the floor never
  1156	    # excludes). Report the TRUE reason: no SUPPORTS member at all, else everything bound/pool-absent.
  1157	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1344 M5): ``reason`` is computed from the FULL surviving list BEFORE the
  1158	    # promotion partition, so it honestly reports whether any unbound SUPPORTS member was FOUND —
  1159	    # the partition only ROUTES the found members into promoted vs disclosed-only, it never changes
  1160	    # whether members existed.
  1161	    if ev_ids:
  1162	        reason = _REASON_OK
  1163	    elif supports_members_seen == 0:
  1164	        reason = _REASON_NO_SUPPORTS_MEMBERS
  1165	    else:
  1166	        reason = _REASON_ALL_BOUND_OR_ABSENT
  1167	
  1168	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1344 M5) PROMOTION-ELIGIBILITY PARTITION — route (NOT drop) near-zero,
  1169	    # single-origin, non-journal members to ``disclosed_only`` (kept + re-surfaced, never deleted).
  1170	    # §-1.3: WEIGHT-and-CONSOLIDATE — a member is PROMOTED if its weight clears W OR another source
  1171	    # corroborates it (>= K verified origins) OR it is a recognized journal venue; only a member
  1172	    # failing ALL three is routed to disclosed-only. Conservation holds: ``promoted`` UNION
  1173	    # ``disclosed_only`` == the full ``ev_ids`` above (nothing vanishes). The faithfulness engine is
  1174	    # untouched — weight/corroboration are credibility judgments, never a grounding gate.
  1175	    disclosed_only: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
  1176	    if promotion_eligibility_enabled():
  1177	        # FAIL-LOUD env parse (LAW VI): a garbage threshold is an operator config error and raises
  1178	        # ValueError, NOT swallowed by the fail-open guard below.
  1179	        min_w = _parse_promotion_min_weight(os.environ.get(_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_WEIGHT))
  1180	        min_c = _parse_promotion_min_corroboration(os.environ.get(_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_CORROBORATION))
  1181	        # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-C: FAIL-LOUD topical-overlap threshold parse (LAW VI).
  1182	        min_t = _parse_promotion_min_topical_overlap(
  1183	            os.environ.get(_ENV_PROMOTION_MIN_TOPICAL_OVERLAP)
  1184	        )
  1185	        try:
  1186	            def _topical_demote(eid: str) -> bool:
  1187	                # FIX-C off-topic single-origin CITE gate: a corroborated-by-nobody, >=6-word,
  1188	                # <= min-overlap quote is routed to disclosed_only (KEPT, not dropped). FAIL-OPEN
  1189	                # on empty question / gate off / terse quote / any overlap above min / corroboration.
  1190	                # F2 2b (#1371): this LEXICAL question-overlap override is the FALLBACK — it fires ONLY
  1191	                # on a fully-UNJUDGED row. A row an upstream judge stamped (positive/off ``content_
  1192	                # relevance_label`` or a numeric ``selection_relevance``) uses THAT judged decision:
  1193	                # a positive label already keeps (line 157-166), a confirmed-off label is already
  1194	                # suppressed (line 1028), and a below-floor score already routes via the WEIGHT leg —
  1195	                # so the noisy lexical override must never re-bury a judged-relevant source (the drb_72
  1196	                # seminal-paper burial). §-1.3 WEIGHT-not-FILTER: judged label first, lexical fallback.
  1197	                if _row_has_judgment(pool.get(eid)):
  1198	                    return False
  1199	                return (
  1200	                    _promo_topical_gate
  1201	                    and bool(_promo_q_terms)
  1202	                    and best_quote_overlap.get(eid) is not None
  1203	                    and quote_words.get(eid, 0) >= _PROMOTION_TOPICAL_MIN_QUOTE_WORDS
  1204	                    and best_quote_overlap[eid] <= min_t
  1205	                    and max_origin.get(eid, 0) < min_c
  1206	                )
  1207	
  1208	            def _promotion_eligible(eid: str) -> bool:
  1209	                if _topical_demote(eid):
  1210	                    return False                                  # FIX-C off-topic single-origin override
  1211	                w = best_cred_weight.get(eid)
  1212	                if w is None:
  1213	                    return True                                   # unknown weight => keep-neutral (promote)
  1214	                if w >= min_w:
  1215	                    return True                                   # WEIGHT leg
  1216	                if max_origin.get(eid, 0) >= min_c:
  1217	                    return True                                   # CONSOLIDATE leg (corroboration rescues)
  1218	                if is_journal.get(eid, False):
  1219	                    return True                                   # journal carve-out (over-demotion guard)
  1220	                return False
  1221	
  1222	            _promoted = [e for e in ev_ids if _promotion_eligible(e)]
  1223	            disclosed_only = [
  1224	                {
  1225	                    "evidence_id": e,
  1226	                    "source_url": str(
  1227	                        (pool.get(e) or {}).get("source_url")
  1228	                        or (pool.get(e) or {}).get("url")
  1229	                        or ""
  1230	                    ),
  1231	                    "source_tier": best_tier.get(e, ""),
  1232	                    "credibility_weight": best_cred_weight.get(e),
  1233	                    "reason": (
  1234	                        "off_topic_single_origin" if _topical_demote(e)
  1235	                        else _DISCLOSED_ONLY_REASON
  1236	                    ),
  1237	                }
  1238	                for e in ev_ids
  1239	                if not _promotion_eligible(e)
  1240	            ]
  1241	            ev_ids = _promoted
  1242	            # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-C: honest realized-effect [activation] marker — emitted once
  1243	            # per selection whenever the topical gate is enabled (demoted=0 is still a live marker).
  1244	            if _promo_topical_gate:
  1245	                logger.info(
  1246	                    "[activation] promotion_topical_gate: demoted=%d promoted=%d",
  1247	                    sum(1 for e in disclosed_only if e.get("reason") == "off_topic_single_origin"),
  1248	                    len(_promoted),
  1249	                )
  1250	        except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — fail-OPEN to promote-all = byte-identical legacy keep-all
  1251	            logger.warning(
  1252	                "[weighted_enrichment] M5 promotion-eligibility partition failed; FAIL-OPEN to "
  1253	                "promote-all (byte-identical legacy keep-all-and-cite). ev_ids left unchanged.",
  1254	                exc_info=True,
  1255	            )
  1256	            disclosed_only = []
  1257	
  1258	    return UnboundSupportsSelection(
  1259	        ev_ids=ev_ids,
  1260	        reason=reason,
  1261	        baskets_seen=len(baskets),
  1262	        supports_members_seen=supports_members_seen,
  1263	        excluded_bound=excluded_bound,
  1264	        excluded_pool_absent=excluded_pool_absent,
  1265	        excluded_below_floor=below_floor_count,  # field name held stable; meaning = kept-below-floor
  1266	        offtopic_suppressed=tuple(offtopic_suppressed),  # I-deepfix-001 DEFER-1 (kept+disclosed)
  1267	        disclosed_only=tuple(disclosed_only),  # I-deepfix-001 M5 (routed-to-disclosed, never dropped)
  1268	    )
  1269	
  1270	
  1271	def select_unbound_supports_by_weight(
  1272	    *,
  1273	    evidence_pool: Any,
