  1274	    credibility_analysis: Any,
  1275	    contract_plans: Any,
  1276	    research_question: str = "",
  1277	) -> list[str]:
  1278	    """Ordered evidence_ids of unbound, isolated-verified SUPPORTS basket members.
  1279	
  1280	    Returns the FULL surviving list — NO cap, NO target, NO top-N, NO floor DROP. A member is
  1281	    included iff:
  1282	      * its own ``span_verdict == "SUPPORTS"`` (isolated per-member verification), AND
  1283	      * its ``evidence_id`` is NOT already bound to a contract section, AND
  1284	      * its ``evidence_id`` resolves in ``evidence_pool`` (so the section can cite a real span).
  1285	
  1286	    I-arch-011 (B18) — WEIGHT, DON'T FILTER (§-1.3, the keystone): the relevance floor is now an
  1287	    ORDERING weight, NEVER an exclusion. Ordering is:
  1288	      1. at/above-floor (and missing-relevance) rows FIRST, below-floor rows LAST (a demotion, not a
  1289	         drop), THEN
  1290	      2. relevance-to-question DESC, THEN
  1291	      3. basket ``weight_mass`` (priority of consideration), THEN
  1292	      4. ``evidence_id`` (deterministic tiebreak).
  1293	    The pre-fix code RE-IMPOSED a hard ``selection_relevance < PG_RELEVANCE_FLOOR`` DROP here — the
  1294	    FILTER-AND-CAP anti-pattern the selector docstring (evidence_selector.py:1944-1953) forbids,
  1295	    which killed 729/746 unbound SUPPORTS so the enrichment appended NOTHING. That drop is REMOVED;
  1296	    a below-floor row is KEPT and sorted LAST, mirroring the retrieval pool's keep-all-down-weight
  1297	    (evidence_selector.py:2066-2070). A row with NO usable relevance score is keep-neutral (sentinel
  1298	    0.0, treated as NOT-below-floor) — pool membership already implies the retrieval floor passed.
  1299	
  1300	    The floor + its fail-loud (0.0, 1.0] validation come from the SAME ``parse_relevance_floor`` the
  1301	    retrieval gate uses (no new constant). A garbage ``PG_RELEVANCE_FLOOR`` raises ``ValueError``.
  1302	
  1303	    Faithfulness is UNCHANGED: every surfaced member is re-verified against its own span by the
  1304	    section's UNCHANGED ``strict_verify``; breadth comes from consolidating already-verifiable
  1305	    corroborators, never from relaxing a verify gate.
  1306	
  1307	    ``credibility_analysis is None`` (master flag OFF or always-release degrade) => ``[]`` =>
  1308	    byte-identical legacy render. Thin wrapper over ``diagnose_unbound_supports_selection``; the call
  1309	    site uses the diagnostic form to log WHY an empty selection happened.
  1310	    """
  1311	    return diagnose_unbound_supports_selection(
  1312	        evidence_pool=evidence_pool,
  1313	        credibility_analysis=credibility_analysis,
  1314	        contract_plans=contract_plans,
  1315	        research_question=research_question,
  1316	    ).ev_ids
  1317	
  1318	
  1319	def build_weighted_enrichment_plan(ev_ids: Any, *, section_plan_cls: Any):
  1320	    """Build ONE legacy (field-agnostic) enrichment SectionPlan, or ``None`` when empty.
  1321	
  1322	    ``None`` on empty ``ev_ids`` => caller appends nothing => byte-identical OFF/degrade path.
  1323	    """
  1324	    ev_ids = list(ev_ids or [])
  1325	    if not ev_ids:
  1326	        return None
  1327	    return section_plan_cls(
  1328	        title=_ENRICHMENT_TITLE,
  1329	        focus=_ENRICHMENT_FOCUS,
  1330	        ev_ids=ev_ids,
  1331	    )
  1332	
  1333	
  1334	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  1335	# I-deepfix-001 D4 (#1344) — FACET-CLUSTER THE WEIGHTED-ENRICHMENT BREADTH SURFACE.
  1336	#
  1337	# Gap: the "Corroborated Weighted Findings" section keeps ALL unbound-but-verified members (correct,
  1338	# §-1.3 keep-all) but lands them as ONE flat list of single-source one-liners — it reads as a link
  1339	# dump, not facet-organized coverage (DRB-II presentation + analysis; DR-original readability).
  1340	#
  1341	# Fix (PURE PLACEMENT — nothing dropped, faithfulness engine untouched): route each unbound member
  1342	# under the FACET/section its subject matches (reusing the report's own facet section TITLES), so it
  1343	# becomes part of that topical section. Members matching no facet stay in a residual "Additional
  1344	# corroborated findings" block (keep-all). This changes ONLY which section a member is composed under;
  1345	# every member still flows through the UNCHANGED strict_verify + section floor exactly as before.
  1346	#
  1347	# DEFAULT-OFF (LAW VI): ``enrichment_facet_route_enabled()`` False => the caller builds the single flat
  1348	# plan (byte-identical). No facet titles => also the single flat plan (no facets to route under).
  1349	_ENV_ENRICHMENT_FACET_ROUTE = "PG_ENRICHMENT_FACET_ROUTE"
  1350	
  1351	# The residual bucket TITLE for members matching no facet (kept + surfaced, never dropped).
  1352	_ENRICHMENT_RESIDUAL_TITLE = "Additional Corroborated Findings"
  1353	# Prefix for a per-facet routed enrichment section title.
  1354	_ENRICHMENT_FACET_TITLE_PREFIX = "Corroborated Findings: "
  1355	
  1356	# Minimal English stopword set for the facet content-word overlap. Small on purpose: a bigger list
  1357	# risks dropping a real topical token. Purely a MATCH heuristic — a miss routes a member to residual
  1358	# (kept), never drops it, so faithfulness is unaffected by the stoplist's exact contents.
  1359	_FACET_STOPWORDS = frozenset({
  1360	    "the", "a", "an", "and", "or", "of", "in", "on", "for", "to", "with", "by", "at", "from",
  1361	    "as", "is", "are", "was", "were", "be", "been", "being", "this", "that", "these", "those",
  1362	    "it", "its", "their", "his", "her", "our", "your", "we", "they", "he", "she", "you", "i",
  1363	    "not", "no", "but", "if", "then", "than", "so", "such", "into", "over", "under", "about",
  1364	    "key", "findings", "analysis", "assessment", "overview", "summary", "evidence", "corroborated",
  1365	    "weighted", "additional", "section", "results", "study", "studies", "report",
  1366	})
  1367	
  1368	
  1369	def enrichment_facet_route_enabled() -> bool:
  1370	    """PG_ENRICHMENT_FACET_ROUTE gate (D4). DEFAULT-OFF => byte-identical single flat plan; an explicit
  1371	    1/true/on/yes turns the facet-clustered enrichment routing ON."""
  1372	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_ENRICHMENT_FACET_ROUTE, "0").strip().lower() in ("1", "true", "on", "yes")
  1373	
  1374	
  1375	def _facet_content_tokens(text: Any) -> set[str]:
  1376	    """Lower-cased content tokens of ``text`` (>=3 chars, not a stopword). Pure. Used to match a
  1377	    member's subject/quote text against a facet section title by token overlap."""
  1378	    out: set[str] = set()
  1379	    for tok in re.findall(r"[a-z0-9]+", str(text or "").lower()):
  1380	        if len(tok) >= 3 and tok not in _FACET_STOPWORDS:
  1381	            out.add(tok)
  1382	    return out
  1383	
  1384	
  1385	def route_enrichment_members_by_facet(
  1386	    ev_ids: Any,
  1387	    facet_titles: Any,
  1388	    *,
  1389	    text_of: Callable[[str], str],
  1390	    min_overlap: int = 1,
  1391	) -> "tuple[list[tuple[str, list[str]]], list[str]]":
  1392	    """Partition enrichment members into per-facet buckets by subject/topic overlap. PURE, keep-all.
  1393	
  1394	    Each ev_id is routed under the FIRST facet whose title content-words overlap the member's text
  1395	    (``text_of(ev_id)`` — the member's subject / quote / title) by ``>= min_overlap`` tokens. A member
  1396	    matching NO facet lands in the residual list. Order-stable: facet buckets follow ``facet_titles``
  1397	    order; within a bucket, members follow ``ev_ids`` order; the residual follows ``ev_ids`` order.
  1398	
  1399	    Returns ``(routed, residual)`` where ``routed`` is ``[(facet_title, [ev_id, ...]), ...]`` for the
  1400	    facets that received >=1 member (empty facets are omitted), and ``residual`` is the unmatched
  1401	    ev_ids. KEEP-ALL INVARIANT (asserted by the caller's test): the disjoint union of every routed
  1402	    bucket and the residual EQUALS the de-duplicated input ev_ids — no member is dropped, none appears
  1403	    twice. Nothing here touches the faithfulness engine; this is pure section placement."""
  1404	    ids: list[str] = []
  1405	    seen: set[str] = set()
  1406	    for e in (ev_ids or []):
  1407	        e = str(e or "")
  1408	        if e and e not in seen:
  1409	            seen.add(e)
  1410	            ids.append(e)
  1411	    titles = [str(t or "").strip() for t in (facet_titles or []) if str(t or "").strip()]
  1412	    if not ids or not titles:
  1413	        return ([], list(ids))
  1414	    title_tokens = [(t, _facet_content_tokens(t)) for t in titles]
  1415	    buckets: dict[str, list[str]] = {t: [] for t in titles}
  1416	    residual: list[str] = []
  1417	    for e in ids:
  1418	        member_tokens = _facet_content_tokens(text_of(e))
  1419	        placed = False
  1420	        if member_tokens:
  1421	            best_title = ""
  1422	            best_overlap = 0
  1423	            for (t, toks) in title_tokens:
  1424	                overlap = len(member_tokens & toks)
  1425	                if overlap > best_overlap:
  1426	                    best_overlap = overlap
  1427	                    best_title = t
  1428	            if best_overlap >= max(1, int(min_overlap)):
  1429	                buckets[best_title].append(e)
  1430	                placed = True
  1431	        if not placed:
  1432	            residual.append(e)
  1433	    routed = [(t, buckets[t]) for t in titles if buckets[t]]
  1434	    return (routed, residual)
  1435	
  1436	
  1437	def build_weighted_enrichment_plans_by_facet(
  1438	    ev_ids: Any,
  1439	    facet_titles: Any,
  1440	    *,
  1441	    section_plan_cls: Any,
  1442	    text_of: Callable[[str], str],
  1443	    min_overlap: int = 1,
  1444	) -> list:
  1445	    """Build the FACET-CLUSTERED enrichment SectionPlan LIST (D4), or ``[]`` when empty.
  1446	
  1447	    Returns one SectionPlan per facet that received >=1 routed member (titled
  1448	    ``"Corroborated Findings: <facet>"``) IN ``facet_titles`` ORDER, followed by a single residual
  1449	    ``"Additional Corroborated Findings"`` plan for the members matching no facet. Every plan carries
  1450	    the SAME ``_ENRICHMENT_FOCUS`` so each still routes through the field-agnostic ``_run_section`` ->
  1451	    strict_verify path exactly as the flat plan did. KEEP-ALL: the concatenation of all returned plans'
  1452	    ``ev_ids`` equals the de-duplicated input (nothing dropped). ``[]`` on empty input => caller
  1453	    appends nothing => byte-identical to the OFF path. When NO member matches any facet, the sole
  1454	    returned plan is the residual, titled the SAME as the legacy flat section so a zero-facet corpus is
  1455	    presentation-identical to today."""
  1456	    routed, residual = route_enrichment_members_by_facet(
  1457	        ev_ids, facet_titles, text_of=text_of, min_overlap=min_overlap,
  1458	    )
  1459	    plans: list = []
  1460	    for (title, members) in routed:
  1461	        if not members:
  1462	            continue
  1463	        plans.append(section_plan_cls(
  1464	            title=f"{_ENRICHMENT_FACET_TITLE_PREFIX}{title}",
  1465	            focus=_ENRICHMENT_FOCUS,
  1466	            ev_ids=list(members),
  1467	        ))
  1468	    if residual:
  1469	        # When nothing routed to a facet, keep the legacy flat title so a zero-match corpus renders
  1470	        # identically to today's single "Corroborated Weighted Findings" section.
  1471	        residual_title = _ENRICHMENT_TITLE if not plans else _ENRICHMENT_RESIDUAL_TITLE
  1472	        plans.append(section_plan_cls(
  1473	            title=residual_title,
  1474	            focus=_ENRICHMENT_FOCUS,
  1475	            ev_ids=list(residual),
  1476	        ))
  1477	    return plans
  1478	
  1479	
  1480	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1481	# I-arch-008 (#1265) FIX K — DETERMINISTIC VERIFIED-SPAN RENDER for the
  1482	# enrichment section (the 590-in / 0-cited collapse).
  1483	#
  1484	# THE BUG (traced + behaviorally proven on the cQ75 corpus, state/iarch007_
  1485	# breadth_collapse_finding.md): the "Corroborated Weighted Findings" section
  1486	# selects ~590 unbound-but-span-verified SUPPORTS sources, then runs them
  1487	# through ``_run_section`` -> ``_call_section`` (the LLM), which GENERATES fresh
  1488	# prose. That prose then has to RE-EARN strict_verify/entailment from scratch and
  1489	# ~0 survives — so the breadth basket renders EMPTY ("no claim survived strict
  1490	# verification"). The sources were ALREADY isolated-span-verified (``span_verdict
  1491	# == SUPPORTS``); re-generating prose about them throws that verification away.
  1492	#
  1493	# THE FIX (faithfulness-NEUTRAL, no gate relaxation): when
  1494	# ``PG_BREADTH_ENRICHMENT_RENDER_VERIFIED_SPANS`` is ON, the enrichment section
  1495	# SKIPS the LLM and instead emits a DETERMINISTIC draft = each source's OWN
  1496	# verbatim sentence-units, each tagged with a legacy ``[ev_id]`` marker. That
  1497	# draft flows through the UNCHANGED ``_rewrite_draft_with_spans`` ->
  1498	# ``strict_verify`` path: the rewriter binds each unit to its best in-quote span
  1499	# via the SAME ``_find_best_span_for_sentence`` every section uses, and
  1500	# strict_verify validates each as that source's exact span-grounded words.
  1501	# Breadth EMERGES from how many survive the unchanged gate (measured ceiling on
  1502	# cQ75: 571 of 671 usable sources become citable, vs 7 today). NOTHING about the
  1503	# faithfulness engine moves — each rendered citation is literally the source's
  1504	# own quote against its own span.
  1505	#
  1506	# TWO build-correctness rules the behavioral harness surfaced
  1507	# (scripts/breadth_replay_harness.py — the §-1.4 acceptance gate):
  1508	#   1. PER-SENTENCE-UNIT tagging is MANDATORY. ``strict_verify`` re-splits the
  1509	#      draft into sentence units; a "whole quote + ONE trailing marker" tags only
  1510	#      the LAST unit, so every earlier unit drops with ``no_provenance_token``.
  1511	#      That naive draft verifies only 51 of 671 vs 571 for per-unit tagging — an
  1512	#      11x silent collapse (the same 590->0 symptom in microcosm). Each unit
  1513	#      therefore carries its OWN ``[ev_id]`` marker.
  1514	#   2. A JUNK SCREEN is REQUIRED. For a verbatim self-quote, strict_verify's
  1515	#      content-word/decimal checks are a tautology (idle) — they filter nothing —
  1516	#      so faithfulness rests on SPAN QUALITY. A fetch-shell / cookie-banner /
  1517	#      error-page span would otherwise self-quote straight through. We reuse the
  1518	#      SAME ``is_boilerplate_or_nonassertional`` allowlist screen strict_verify's
  1519	#      BUG-19 pregate uses, applied BOTH per source-quote and per unit, so K's
  1520	#      input hygiene is identical to the gate's.
  1521	#
  1522	# DEFAULT OFF (LAW VI) => ``render_verified_spans_enabled()`` False =>
  1523	# byte-identical legacy LLM render. ``is_enrichment_section`` matches ONLY this
  1524	# module's own ``_ENRICHMENT_TITLE`` section, so no other section is ever touched.
  1525	
  1526	_ENV_RENDER_VERIFIED_SPANS = "PG_BREADTH_ENRICHMENT_RENDER_VERIFIED_SPANS"
  1527	
  1528	# Per-SOURCE verbatim-unit budget (a verbosity bound + survival redundancy, NOT a
  1529	# breadth cap — the NUMBER OF SOURCES surfaced is uncapped; this only bounds how
  1530	# many of one source's own sentences are quoted, and offering a few raises the
  1531	# chance at least one clears entailment in enforce mode). Env-overridable (LAW
  1532	# VI); fail-loud on a non-int; floored at 1 so the flag can never silently zero
  1533	# the render.
  1534	_ENV_SPANS_PER_SOURCE = "PG_BREADTH_ENRICHMENT_SPANS_PER_SOURCE"
  1535	_DEFAULT_SPANS_PER_SOURCE = 3
  1536	
  1537	# A sentence-unit must clear this length AND carry a real word to be a citable
  1538	# claim (drops bare fragments / lone numbers / headers). Allowlist-side only: the
  1539	# unchanged strict_verify gate still independently judges every surviving unit.
  1540	_MIN_UNIT_CHARS = 40
  1541	
  1542	# I-beatboth-011 #4 (#1289) — RENDER-SAFETY char bound on a single emitted unit.
  1543	# A clean claim sentence is at most a few hundred chars; a unit longer than this is
  1544	# NOT a sentence — it is a fetch-shell / raw-extraction blob (the drb_72 defect was a
  1545	# ~75K-char raw academic-equation dump that carried a literal NUL byte and self-quoted
  1546	# straight into report.md, making it binary-corrupt). This is an allowlist-side
  1547	# RENDER bound on a single SURFACED unit, NOT a breadth cap (the number of SOURCES
  1548	# surfaced is uncapped) and NOT a faithfulness gate (strict_verify is untouched). A
  1549	# real long-but-legitimate quote is split into sentence units upstream by
  1550	# ``split_into_sentences``; a single unit exceeding this bound is structurally a blob,
  1551	# never a clinical sentence. Env-overridable (LAW VI); fail-loud on a non-int; floored
  1552	# at ``_MIN_UNIT_CHARS`` so the bound can never silently zero the render.
  1553	_ENV_MAX_UNIT_CHARS = "PG_BREADTH_ENRICHMENT_MAX_UNIT_CHARS"
  1554	_DEFAULT_MAX_UNIT_CHARS = 600
  1555	
  1556	# C0 control bytes (and DEL) that MUST NEVER reach the rendered report — a literal NUL
  1557	# (\x00) at byte offset 220201 made drb_72 report.md binary-corrupt and unshowable.
  1558	# We strip every C0 control char EXCEPT \n and \t (which are legitimate whitespace in
  1559	# a multi-line quote). 0x7F (DEL) is included. This is byte-hygiene on the emitted
  1560	# render text, never a verdict and never a content drop.
  1561	_C0_CONTROL_KEEP = {"\n", "\t"}
  1562	
  1563	# CAPTCHA / Cloudflare / security-interstitial stubs that fetch as a grammatical-looking
  1564	# SENTENCE (so ``is_boilerplate_or_nonassertional`` does NOT catch them) and would
  1565	# otherwise self-quote into the report. Allowlist input-hygiene, NEVER a verdict, NEVER a
  1566	# quality/length drop of real content.
  1567	#
  1568	# I-beatboth-011 #7 P1 (#1289): the bare trigger phrase "just a moment" is NOT enough to
  1569	# drop a member — real substantive prose can carry it ("Just a moment — the data show
  1570	# wages rose 5% in 2023"). Dropping such prose would violate §-1.3 keep-all. A drop now
  1571	# requires the trigger AND a STRONG WAF / security co-token (BYTE-IDENTICAL predicate
  1572	# shared with ``finding_dedup._is_captcha_stub`` so consolidation and render agree). The
  1573	# co-tokens are high-precision multi-word / branded anchors a real clinical sentence (any
  1574	# language) never contains.
  1575	_CAPTCHA_STUB_TRIGGER = "just a moment"
  1576	_WAF_CO_TOKENS = (
  1577	    "performing security verification",   # Cloudflare / generic WAF
  1578	    "checking your browser",              # Cloudflare "checking your browser before accessing"
  1579	    "cloudflare",                         # Cloudflare attribution / interstitial brand
  1580	    "ray id",                             # Cloudflare error footer "Ray ID: ..."
  1581	    "cf-ray",                             # Cloudflare response-header / footer token
  1582	    "enable javascript and cookies",      # Cloudflare retry prompt
  1583	    "ddos protection",                    # Cloudflare attribution stub
  1584	    "attention required",                 # Cloudflare 1020 / block interstitial title
  1585	    "verifying you are human",            # hCaptcha / Cloudflare Turnstile
  1586	    "needs to review the security of your connection",  # Cloudflare interstitial body
  1587	)
  1588	
  1589	# Web-chrome / cookie-consent / nav markers that read as a grammatical SENTENCE.
  1590	# These slip past ``is_boilerplate_or_nonassertional`` + ``strip_web_boilerplate``
  1591	# (which catch error-pages + line-level chrome, not sentence-form consent text) —
  1592	# and on a verbatim self-quote strict_verify's content/decimal checks are IDLE, so
  1593	# without this screen a "Enable basic functions like page navigation." span would
  1594	# self-quote straight into a clinical report. Same allowlist-only, whole-unit
  1595	# input-hygiene pattern as the strict_verify BUG-19 pregate: multi-word, anchored
  1596	# to chrome-specific phrasing so a real clinical sentence (any language) is never
  1597	# touched, and NEVER a verdict — only what the breadth section actively SURFACES.
  1598	_WEB_CHROME_MARKERS = (
  1599	    "enable basic functions",
  1600	    "page navigation",
  1601	    "access to secure areas",
  1602	    "secure areas of the website",
  1603	    "website cannot function",
  1604	    "without these cookies",
  1605	    "accept all cookies",
  1606	    "cookie settings",
  1607	    "cookie policy",
  1608	    "privacy policy",
  1609	    "terms of service",
  1610	    "all rights reserved",
  1611	    "page not found",
  1612	    "404 error",
  1613	    "are you a robot",
  1614	    "enable javascript",
  1615	    "request access to",
  1616	    "sign in to continue",
  1617	    "subscribe to read",
  1618	    "log in to view",
  1619	    # I-beatboth-011 §3.4 idx68 (#1289): social-media / repository / masthead chrome that leaked into
  1620	    # cited spans in banked v3 (Scribd, Facebook, YouTube, journal masthead). HIGH-PRECISION multi-word
  1621	    # anchors ONLY (never bare "share"/"download"/"subscribers", which appear in real prose) — P1-4:
  1622	    # allowlist input-hygiene, NOT a length/quality drop of real content.
  1623	    "download free for 30 days",          # Scribd
  1624	    "report this document",               # Scribd
  1625	    "is this content inappropriate",      # Scribd
  1626	    "like comment share",                 # Facebook
  1627	    "subscribers subscribed",             # YouTube channel chrome
  1628	    "share save download",                # YouTube action bar
  1629	    "tap to unmute",                      # YouTube player chrome
  1630	    "skip navigation",                    # YouTube / generic nav
  1631	    "cite this paper as",                 # journal masthead citation widget
  1632	    # I-beatboth-011 b1 (#1289): publisher login-nav + image-URL masthead chrome that self-quoted into the
  1633	    # answer BODY/Key-Findings in banked v3 (drb_72 report.md carried the literal Wiley masthead+login-nav
  1634	    # run ".../logo-header-1690978619437.png) ## Change Password Old Password New Password Too Short.[13]").
  1635	    # HIGH-PRECISION multi-word anchors ONLY (never bare "password"/"image"/"logo"/"favicon", which appear
  1636	    # in real prose) — allowlist input-hygiene, NOT a length/quality drop of real content.
  1637	    "change password old password new password",  # Wiley/publisher login-nav run
  1638	    "/pb-assets/",                                 # publisher asset path segment (slash-anchored)
  1639	    "![image",                                     # markdown image leader "![Image N: ...]" (structure-anchored)
  1640	)
  1641	
  1642	# Structure-anchored web-chrome asset URLs that a bare substring marker cannot express
  1643	# precisely — I-beatboth-011 b1 (#1289). Each REQUIRES a file extension / digit-stamp so a
  1644	# real-prose mention ("the favicon was redesigned", "a logo-header CSS class") is NEVER matched
  1645	# (the §-1.3 no-real-claim-dropped invariant). favicon coverage was missing entirely; logo-header
  1646	# was a bare substring (over-screen risk) — both are now extension/path-anchored here.
  1647	_WEB_CHROME_RE = re.compile(
  1648	    r"favicon[\w.\-]*\.(?:ico|png|svg|gif|jpe?g)\b"   # favicon.<ext> asset file
  1649	    r"|\blogo-header[-\w]*\.png\b",                   # masthead image URL logo-header-<stamp>.png
  1650	    re.IGNORECASE,
  1651	)
  1652	
  1653	# Trailing sentence-terminal punctuation stripped before the ``[ev_id]`` marker is
  1654	# appended, so the marker sits INSIDE the sentence unit (``...trial [ev_id].``) and
  1655	# survives strict_verify's re-split. A marker appended AFTER the period
  1656	# (``...trial. [ev_id]``) is peeled onto its own fragment -> the content sentence
  1657	# goes tokenless -> dropped ``no_provenance_token`` (the silent-collapse the harness
  1658	# caught: it suppressed otherwise-citable sources).
  1659	_TERMINAL_PUNCT = ".!?"
  1660	
  1661	# Legacy ``[ev_id]`` marker form — exactly what ``_call_section``'s LLM emits and
  1662	# what ``_rewrite_draft_with_spans`` (_EV_MARKER_RE) consumes. We emit this (not a
  1663	# pre-baked ``[#ev:id:s-e]`` token) so K's spans are computed by the SAME
  1664	# production span-finder as every other section — no parallel offset math.
  1665	
  1666	
  1667	def render_verified_spans_enabled() -> bool:
  1668	    """True iff the default-OFF verified-span render flag is explicitly enabled (LAW VI)."""
  1669	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_RENDER_VERIFIED_SPANS, "").strip().lower() in (
  1670	        "1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled",
  1671	    )
  1672	
  1673	
  1674	def spans_per_source() -> int:
  1675	    """Per-source verbatim-unit budget from ``PG_BREADTH_ENRICHMENT_SPANS_PER_SOURCE``.
  1676	
  1677	    Default ``_DEFAULT_SPANS_PER_SOURCE``. Fail-loud on a non-integer (LAW II — no
  1678	    silent fallback to a guessed value); floored at 1 so the render can never be
  1679	    silently zeroed by a ``0`` / negative value.
  1680	    """
  1681	    raw = os.environ.get(_ENV_SPANS_PER_SOURCE)
  1682	    if raw is None or not raw.strip():
  1683	        return _DEFAULT_SPANS_PER_SOURCE
  1684	    try:
  1685	        val = int(raw.strip())
  1686	    except (TypeError, ValueError) as exc:
  1687	        raise ValueError(
  1688	            f"{_ENV_SPANS_PER_SOURCE}={raw!r} is not an integer "
  1689	            f"(per-source verbatim-unit budget)"
  1690	        ) from exc
  1691	    return max(1, val)
  1692	
  1693	
  1694	def max_unit_chars() -> int:
  1695	    """Render-safety char bound on a single emitted unit (I-beatboth-011 #4).
  1696	
  1697	    Default ``_DEFAULT_MAX_UNIT_CHARS``. Fail-loud on a non-integer (LAW II — no
  1698	    silent fallback to a guessed value); floored at ``_MIN_UNIT_CHARS`` so the bound
  1699	    can never silently zero the render. A unit longer than this is structurally a
  1700	    fetch-shell / raw-extraction blob, never a clinical sentence.
  1701	    """
  1702	    raw = os.environ.get(_ENV_MAX_UNIT_CHARS)
  1703	    if raw is None or not raw.strip():
  1704	        return _DEFAULT_MAX_UNIT_CHARS
  1705	    try:
  1706	        val = int(raw.strip())
  1707	    except (TypeError, ValueError) as exc:
  1708	        raise ValueError(
  1709	            f"{_ENV_MAX_UNIT_CHARS}={raw!r} is not an integer "
  1710	            f"(per-unit render char bound)"
  1711	        ) from exc
  1712	    return max(_MIN_UNIT_CHARS, val)
  1713	
  1714	
  1715	def _strip_control_bytes(text: str) -> str:
  1716	    """Strip C0 control bytes (and DEL 0x7F) EXCEPT \\n and \\t from render text.
  1717	
  1718	    The drb_72 defect leaked a literal NUL byte (``\\x00``) into report.md, making it
  1719	    binary-corrupt and unshowable. This removes every ``ord(ch) < 32`` control char
  1720	    plus ``0x7F`` while KEEPING newline/tab (legitimate whitespace in a multi-line
  1721	    quote). Byte-hygiene on the emitted render text, never a verdict, never a content
  1722	    drop of a real claim — only non-printable control bytes are removed.
  1723	    """
  1724	    if not text:
  1725	        return text
  1726	    return "".join(
  1727	        ch
  1728	        for ch in text
  1729	        if ch in _C0_CONTROL_KEEP or (ord(ch) >= 32 and ord(ch) != 0x7F)
  1730	    )
  1731	
  1732	
  1733	def _is_captcha_stub(text: str) -> bool:
  1734	    """True iff ``text`` is a CAPTCHA / security-interstitial stub (allowlist-only).
  1735	
  1736	    I-beatboth-011 #7 P1 (#1289): the bare trigger phrase ("just a moment") is NOT
  1737	    sufficient — a genuinely substantive sentence can contain it. A drop requires the
  1738	    trigger AND a strong WAF / security co-token (BYTE-IDENTICAL predicate shared with
  1739	    ``finding_dedup._is_captcha_stub``). §-1.3 keep-all: real prose carrying a bare
  1740	    "just a moment" with no security co-token is never dropped.
  1741	    """
  1742	    low = text.lower()
  1743	    return (_CAPTCHA_STUB_TRIGGER in low) and any(tok in low for tok in _WAF_CO_TOKENS)
  1744	
  1745	
  1746	def is_enrichment_section(section: Any) -> bool:
  1747	    """True iff ``section`` is one of THIS module's weighted-enrichment section plans.
  1748	
  1749	    Scopes the FIX-K deterministic verified-span render to the sections this module builds — every
  1750	    contract / body section stays byte-identical.
  1751	
  1752	    I-deepfix-001 D4 (#1344, Fable P1): when ``PG_ENRICHMENT_FACET_ROUTE`` is ON the enrichment payload
  1753	    is split into per-facet plans (title ``"Corroborated Findings: <facet>"``) plus a residual plan
  1754	    (``"Additional Corroborated Findings"``), NOT the single flat ``_ENRICHMENT_TITLE`` section. Every
  1755	    such plan carries the SAME ``_ENRICHMENT_FOCUS`` (``build_weighted_enrichment_plans_by_facet``), so
  1756	    matching on the shared ``focus`` recognizes flat, facet, AND residual plans — otherwise the paid
  1757	    Gate-B slate (which force-ONs BOTH facet-route and the verified-span render) would drop every
  1758	    facet-titled plan back to the distill+LLM 590-in/0-cited collapse path FIX-K exists to bypass. The
  1759	    title checks are kept as a defensive fallback for a plan built without the focus string.
  1760	    Robust to a duck-typed plan (missing attrs => False)."""
  1761	    focus = str(getattr(section, "focus", "") or "")
  1762	    if focus and focus == _ENRICHMENT_FOCUS:
  1763	        return True
  1764	    title = str(getattr(section, "title", "") or "")
  1765	    if title in (_ENRICHMENT_TITLE, _ENRICHMENT_RESIDUAL_TITLE):
  1766	        return True
  1767	    return bool(title.startswith(_ENRICHMENT_FACET_TITLE_PREFIX))
  1768	
  1769	
  1770	def _is_web_chrome(text: str) -> bool:
  1771	    """True iff ``text`` carries a sentence-form web-chrome / cookie-consent marker."""
  1772	    low = text.lower()
  1773	    if any(marker in low for marker in _WEB_CHROME_MARKERS):
  1774	        return True
  1775	    return bool(_WEB_CHROME_RE.search(text))
  1776	
  1777	
  1778	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  1779	# I-wire-012 (#1326) — THE ONE shared render-side chrome+truncation predicate.
  1780	#
  1781	# The render/compose surfaces (Corroborated Weighted Findings, the verified-compose
  1782	# section body, the per-claim corroboration header, Key-Findings / Abstract /
  1783	# Conclusion / depth) each grew their OWN parallel chrome screen
  1784	# (``_make_junk_screen`` here, ``verified_compose._compose_junk_screen``,
  1785	# ``run_honest_sweep_r3._span_is_render_chrome`` / ``_claim_header_is_unrenderable``,
  1786	# the ``key_findings`` filter). Parallel screens DRIFT — a chrome shape patched in
  1787	# one leaks through the others. This module is the chrome hub (verified_compose
  1788	# already delegates to ``_make_junk_screen``), so the ONE predicate lives here and
  1789	# every screen DELEGATES to it: no composer can emit an unscreened claim.
  1790	#
  1791	# FAITHFULNESS (FROZEN engine): this is render/compose INPUT hygiene only — it
  1792	# SUPPRESSES a page-furniture/truncated unit, it NEVER promotes one and NEVER
  1793	# touches a strict_verify / NLI / 4-role / span-grounding VERDICT. Page furniture is
  1794	# not a corroborating source, so suppressing it STRENGTHENS faithfulness (§-1.3).
  1795	#
  1796	# PRECISION OVER RECALL (the codebase law: "over-strip deletes a real finding, worse
  1797	# than a leak"). Every NEW category is high-precision allowlist/structure-anchored so
  1798	# a real clinical/economics/policy finding (any language) is never dropped; the
  1799	# canary below is the leak backstop. The "non-English-out-of-scope" category was
  1800	# DELIBERATELY NOT built: a language-only drop deletes real non-English sources (a
  1801	# §-1.3 multilingual-preservation regression), and any genuine non-English chrome
  1802	# already fires one of the structural categories below — so a separate language gate
  1803	# would only add over-strip risk for no recall.
  1804	_RENDER_CHROME_SCREEN_ENV = "PG_RENDER_CHROME_SCREEN"
  1805	
  1806	# Page-furniture / masthead / journal / fetch-framing / nav SPANS that render as a
  1807	# grammatical-looking fragment (so the whole-line boilerplate screen misses them).
  1808	# Consolidated from run_honest_sweep_r3._RENDER_CHROME_SPAN_RE — the SINGLE source of
  1809	# truth now (the runner delegates to this predicate).
  1810	_SHARED_RENDER_CHROME_RE = re.compile(
  1811	    r"\bVolume\s+\d+\s*,?\s*(?:Number|No\.?|Issue)\s+\d+\b"
  1812	    r"|\bPages?\s+\d+\s*[-‐-―]\s*\d+\b"
  1813	    r"|\bCITATIONS\b\s+\d+\s+\bREADS\b\s+\d+"
  1814	    r"|\bMarkdown Content\s*:|\bURL Source\s*:|\bPublished Time\s*:"
  1815	    r"|\bNumber of Pages\s*:|\bCite this paper as\b"
  1816	    r"|#main-content|Twitter-intent|twitter\.com/intent"
  1817	    r"|same series\s*[-‐-―]\s*working paper"
  1818	    r"|\blisted\s+topics?\s+include\b",
  1819	    re.IGNORECASE,
  1820	)
  1821	# I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-A — ISSNe/ISSNp boundary + over-fire.
  1822	#
  1823	# The legacy bare rule ``\bISSN\b\s*:?\s*\d`` (a) MISSED "ISSNe"/"ISSNp" (the ``\b`` after the
  1824	# second N fails when a lowercase letter follows) AND (b) OVER-FIRED on a substantive finding that
  1825	# merely cites an ISSN in passing ("A 2021 study (ISSN 2049-3630) found 14% of jobs at risk." is a
  1826	# real finding, NEVER masthead chrome). §-1.3 precision-over-recall: a bare ISSN serial ALONE is
  1827	# NOT chrome — a masthead recital reciting a publication identity IS. So the token is now CO-SIGNAL
  1828	# gated: an ISSN/ISSNe/ISSNp serial that co-occurs (within a bounded window, order-independent) with
  1829	# a masthead recital word (publication / section / volume / issue / journal) is journal-masthead
  1830	# chrome; a bare ISSN mention inside substantive prose is left as a finding. Default-ON
  1831	# (``PG_CWF_ISSN_CHROME``); OFF restores the byte-identical legacy bare rule (``_LEGACY_BARE_ISSN_RE``)
  1832	# so a kill-switch run is unchanged. SUPPRESS-ONLY — never promotes a unit, never touches a
  1833	# faithfulness verdict.
  1834	_ENV_ISSN_CHROME = "PG_CWF_ISSN_CHROME"  # default ON
  1835	_LEGACY_BARE_ISSN_RE = re.compile(r"\bISSN\b\s*:?\s*\d", re.IGNORECASE)
  1836	_ISSN_MASTHEAD_COSIGNAL_RE = re.compile(
  1837	    r"\bISSN[a-z]?\b\s*:?\s*\d[\d-]*.{0,80}?\b(?:publication|section|volume|issue|journal)\b"
  1838	    r"|\b(?:publication|section|volume|issue|journal)\b.{0,80}?\bISSN[a-z]?\b\s*:?\s*\d",
  1839	    re.IGNORECASE,
  1840	)
  1841	_ISSN_CHROME_ACTIVATION_LOGGED = False  # emit the [activation] marker once per process on first fire
  1842	
  1843	
  1844	def issn_chrome_gate_enabled() -> bool:
  1845	    """Kill-switch ``PG_CWF_ISSN_CHROME`` (default ON). ON => the ISSNe/ISSNp-aware CO-SIGNAL rule
  1846	    (masthead recital only); OFF => the byte-identical legacy bare ``\\bISSN\\b\\s*:?\\s*\\d`` rule."""
  1847	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1369) FIX 4 — default-ON semantics: UNSET and EMPTY-STRING
  1848	    # are both ON; disabled ONLY by an explicit OFF token. The prior truthy-only
  1849	    # membership test made an empty-string env value DISABLE the gate (the
  1850	    # opposite of the intended default-ON), matching the other fix-6 gates now.
  1851	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_ISSN_CHROME, "1").strip().lower() not in (
  1852	        "0", "false", "no", "off",
  1853	    )
  1854	
  1855	
  1856	def _is_issn_masthead_chrome(text: str) -> bool:
  1857	    """FIX-A: ISSN masthead-recital chrome. Default-ON co-signal rule (ISSNe/ISSNp-aware, over-fire
  1858	    safe); OFF => legacy bare ISSN. Emits the ``[activation]`` marker once per process on first fire."""
  1859	    global _ISSN_CHROME_ACTIVATION_LOGGED
  1860	    if issn_chrome_gate_enabled():
  1861	        if _ISSN_MASTHEAD_COSIGNAL_RE.search(text):
  1862	            if not _ISSN_CHROME_ACTIVATION_LOGGED:
  1863	                _ISSN_CHROME_ACTIVATION_LOGGED = True
  1864	                logger.info("[activation] issn_masthead_chrome: fired=1 (co-signal gate ON)")
  1865	            return True
  1866	        return False
  1867	    return bool(_LEGACY_BARE_ISSN_RE.search(text))
  1868	
  1869	
  1870	# I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-B — chart alt-text enumeration ("The chart has 1 X axis … 1 Y axis …").
  1871	# A screen-reader alt-text describing a figure's axes rendered as a standalone finding. Requires the
  1872	# "the chart has" + "x axis" + "y axis" CO-OCCURRENCE (bounded window) so a real finding that merely
  1873	# names an axis ("Employment on the y-axis rose as automation on the x-axis increased.") never matches.
  1874	# Default-ON (``PG_CWF_CHART_ALT_CHROME``); OFF => the rule is skipped (byte-identical). SUPPRESS-ONLY.
  1875	_ENV_CHART_ALT_CHROME = "PG_CWF_CHART_ALT_CHROME"  # default ON
  1876	_CHART_ALT_TEXT_RE = re.compile(
  1877	    r"\bthe chart has\b.{0,80}?\bx[\s-]?axis\b.{0,120}?\by[\s-]?axis\b",
  1878	    re.IGNORECASE,
  1879	)
  1880	_CHART_ALT_ACTIVATION_LOGGED = False  # emit the [activation] marker once per process on first fire
  1881	
  1882	
  1883	def chart_alt_chrome_gate_enabled() -> bool:
  1884	    """Kill-switch ``PG_CWF_CHART_ALT_CHROME`` (default ON). OFF => the chart-alt-text rule is
  1885	    skipped => the predicate is byte-identical to pre-FIX-B."""
  1886	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1369) FIX 4 — default-ON semantics: UNSET and EMPTY-STRING
  1887	    # are both ON; disabled ONLY by an explicit OFF token (see issn_chrome_gate).
  1888	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_CHART_ALT_CHROME, "1").strip().lower() not in (
  1889	        "0", "false", "no", "off",
  1890	    )
  1891	# Claim-header chrome: CC-license / keywords-list / login-wall / share-button furniture
  1892	# (consolidated from run_honest_sweep_r3._CLAIM_HEADER_CHROME_RE). "Close-Share" and CC-license
  1893	# are explicitly in the I-wire-012 category list. PRECISION: this predicate can DROP composer text,
  1894	# so the bare ``\bkeywords\b`` of the header-only version is TIGHTENED to the ``Keywords:`` list
  1895	# LABEL — a real sentence ("the keywords were extracted from ...") is never matched.
  1896	_SHARED_CLAIM_HEADER_CHROME_RE = re.compile(
  1897	    r"creative commons|licensed under a |\bkeywords\s*:|premium access|must have premium|"
  1898	    r"share icon|close\s*-\s*share|all rights reserved",
  1899	    re.IGNORECASE,
  1900	)
  1901	# Numbered table-of-contents entry, SECTION-NAME-anchored only ("1 Introduction", "3 Methods").
  1902	# PRECISION: the loose decimal "N.N Capitalized" form (kept header-only in run_honest_sweep, where
  1903	# an over-match merely swaps to subject+predicate) is DELIBERATELY EXCLUDED here — it would drop a
  1904	# real magnitude claim ("$3.2 Billion") from a composer. Only the unambiguous section-name ToC shape
  1905	# (which a real finding sentence never IS) screens droppable text.
  1906	_SHARED_TOC_RE = re.compile(
  1907	    r"^\s*\d+\s+(?:Introduction|Background|Materials?|Methods?|Results?|Discussion|"
  1908	    r"References|Conclusion|Abstract)\s*$",
  1909	    re.IGNORECASE,
  1910	)
  1911	# A WHOLE-UNIT scraped document label standing alone as a "claim" ("Abstract",
  1912	# "AI Summary", "Author summary", "Graphical abstract"). Whole-unit anchored
  1913	# (``fullmatch``-style ``^...$``) so it NEVER catches POLARIS's own ``## Abstract``
  1914	# section header (that carries the ``## `` prefix + body) or a real sentence that
  1915	# merely contains the word "abstract".
  1916	_DOC_LABEL_RE = re.compile(
  1917	    r"^(?:abstract|ai\s+summary|ai\s+overview|graphical\s+abstract|author\s+summary|"
  1918	    r"plain\s+language\s+summary|highlights|table\s+of\s+contents)\s*[:.]?\s*$",
  1919	    re.IGNORECASE,
  1920	)
  1921	# An ORCID identifier in a "claim" => an author/affiliation masthead list, never a
  1922	# finding (a real clinical/economics sentence never carries a 0000-0000-0000-0000
  1923	# ORCID id). High precision by construction.
  1924	_ORCID_RE = re.compile(r"\b\d{4}-\d{4}-\d{4}-\d{3}[\dxX]\b")
  1925	# A bare DOI / identifier row standing alone as a "claim" (no assertional prose).
  1926	_DOI_ONLY_RE = re.compile(
  1927	    r"^\s*(?:doi\s*:?\s*|https?://(?:dx\.)?doi\.org/)?10\.\d{4,9}/[-._;()/:A-Za-z0-9]+\s*$",
  1928	    re.IGNORECASE,
  1929	)
  1930	# Trailing ``[N]`` / ``[#ev:...]`` citation markers (stripped before the sentence-form
  1931	# completeness test so "…claim.[12]" is judged on the "." not the marker).
  1932	_SHARED_TRAILING_CITE_RE = re.compile(r"(?:\s*\[(?:\d+|#ev:[^\]]*)\])+\s*$")
  1933	
  1934	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  1935	# I-wire-013 (#1327) iter-3a — CONTAINMENT forensic chrome rules (the UNBLINDING).
  1936	#
  1937	# The legacy chrome categories above are WHOLE-UNIT junk classifiers (anchored ^…$ / standalone-
  1938	# label / bare-DOI shapes): they return False the moment a unit ALSO carries real prose, so glued
  1939	# page-furniture survived ("…over the recent past.[1] 1 Introduction 1.1 Research background 1.2
  1940	# Resea.[14]", a masthead glued mid-Abstract, a "## Dennis Zami …" author header glued onto a
  1941	# section title). These rules — ported from the independent detector
  1942	# scripts/iwire013_sec11_forensic_audit.py (which catches 55 chrome / 20 truncation on the banked
  1943	# render where the production predicate reported ~0) — flag a unit that CONTAINS chrome, not only a
  1944	# unit that IS chrome.
  1945	#
  1946	# PRECISION OVER RECALL (drop-path law — "over-strip deletes a real finding, worse than a leak"):
  1947	# the detector's loose bare ``\d+ TitleCase`` ToC token and any-run non-Latin rule were tightened
  1948	# for this DROP path (they over-flagged real economics prose with year/figure number pairs and an
  1949	# English finding quoting a short CJK term). The kept rules are structure-anchored and validated to
  1950	# flag ZERO of a clean-finding probe set while catching the real glued chrome (≈47/55 of the banked
  1951	# render; the residual are detector false-positives we deliberately KEEP, or niche chrome the canary
  1952	# backstops). Every numeric threshold is a named constant (LAW VI / §9.4).
  1953	
  1954	# A glued/inline markdown header INSIDE a unit body (a SECOND "## …" header welded onto the title /
  1955	# into prose) — NOT a clean leading header (the caller passes a header's TITLE, post-``#`` strip).
  1956	_INLINE_HEADER_RE = re.compile(r"(?:^|[^\n#])#{1,6}\s+[A-Za-z]")
  1957	# Author-with-superscript-affiliation list: "Kanbach1,2 · Louisa Heiduk1 · …" (middot separators).
  1958	_AFFIL_MIDDOT_RE = re.compile(r"[A-Za-z]{2,}\d{1,2}(?:,\d)?\s*[·•]")
  1959	# A run of non-Latin script (Arabic / CJK) — the report is English-only, so a PREDOMINANTLY
  1960	# non-Latin unit is a foreign-page scrape. A SHORT inline foreign term inside English prose is NOT
  1961	# flagged (§-1.3 multilingual preservation): the run must be long AND outweigh the Latin letters.
  1962	_NONLATIN_CHAR_RE = re.compile(r"[؀-ۿݐ-ݿ一-鿿぀-ヿ가-힯]")
  1963	_NONLATIN_RUN_RE = re.compile(r"[؀-ۿݐ-ݿ一-鿿぀-ヿ가-힯]{4,}")
  1964	_MIN_NONLATIN_RUN_CHARS = 4  # a shorter run is an inline foreign term, kept
  1965	# A DOTTED section-number token glued into a unit ("1.1 Research", "5.2 AI"); the TitleCase word is
  1966	# excluded when it is a magnitude/measure unit so a real "3.2 Million / 4.5 Billion" pair never
  1967	# reads as a two-token ToC. A unit needs ``_MIN_DOTTED_TOC_HITS`` dotted tokens to flag as glued ToC.
  1968	_DOTTED_SECTION_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"(?:^|\s)\d+\.\d+(?:\.\d+){0,2}\s+([A-Z][a-z]+)")
  1969	_MIN_DOTTED_TOC_HITS = 2
  1970	_MAGNITUDE_UNIT_WORDS = frozenset({
  1971	    "million", "billion", "trillion", "thousand", "hundred", "percent", "percentage",
  1972	    "times", "average", "points", "point",
  1973	})
  1974	# A STANDALONE numbered-heading LINE/unit: a unit that OPENS with a dotted section number + a
  1975	# TitleCase word ("3.3 Recommender Systems", "1.1 Research background to the study"). Anchored at the
  1976	# unit start so a mid-sentence "see section 3.3 for details" never matches; the opener word is
  1977	# magnitude-excluded so "3.2 Billion outcomes …" never matches.
  1978	_STANDALONE_DOTTED_HEADING_RE = re.compile(r"^\s*\d+\.\d+(?:\.\d+){0,2}\s+([A-Z][a-z][\w]*)")
  1979	# A STANDALONE numbered SECTION-NAME heading ("1 Introduction", "3 Methods") — anchored at the unit
  1980	# start with a closed section-name vocabulary so a prose "Figure 1 Results" / "Table 2 Methods"
  1981	# (which does NOT open with a bare number) is never matched.
  1982	_STANDALONE_SECTION_NAME_RE = re.compile(
  1983	    r"^\s*\d+(?:\.\d+){0,3}\s+(?:Introduction|Background|Materials?|Methods?|Methodology|"
  1984	    r"Results?|Discussion|References?|Conclusion|Abstract|Literature|Overview)\b",
  1985	    re.IGNORECASE,
  1986	)
  1987	# Journal / submission MASTHEAD furniture welded into a unit ("44 Pages Posted: 9 Jan 2018",
  1988	# "Vol: 30 Issue: 1", "Date Issued April 2020", "Policy Research Working Paper 11057").
  1989	_MASTHEAD_CHROME_RE = re.compile(
  1990	    r"\bpages?\s+posted\s*:|\bposted\s*:\s*\d|\blast revised\s*:|\bdate issued\b|"
  1991	    r"\bworking paper\s+\d{2,}|\bvol\.?\s*:?\s*\d+\s*(?:,|issue|no\.?)|"
  1992	    r"there are \d+ versions of this paper|\bpolicy research working paper\b|"
  1993	    r"cite this paper as|number of pages",
  1994	    re.IGNORECASE,
  1995	)
  1996	# Author / submission-metadata block ("Received: 31 May 2023 / Accepted: …", "Published online").
  1997	_SUBMISSION_META_RE = re.compile(
  1998	    r"received:\s*\d|accepted:\s*\d|published online|\brevised:\s*\d", re.IGNORECASE,
  1999	)
  2000	# Browser / UI / nav / social-share junk welded into a unit.
  2001	_NAV_CHROME_RE = re.compile(
  2002	    r"share\s+facebook|facebook\s+twitter|twitter\s+linkedin|download associated records|"
  2003	    r"clear your browser cache|refresh the page or clear|accessing this content requir|"
  2004	    r"this content is only available as a pdf|i need some assistance|most recent answer|"
  2005	    r"requires a membership|please log into",
  2006	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2007	)
  2008	# Open-access / license / copyright furniture.
  2009	_LICENSE_CHROME_RE = re.compile(
  2010	    r"creative commons|creativecommons\.org/licenses|open access article distributed under|"
  2011	    r"this is an open access article|©\s*\d{4}\s+the\b|©\s*the author|copyright\s+©",
  2012	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2013	)
  2014	# HARD bibliographic / portal markers (a LONE URL is NOT chrome; these are unambiguous).
  2015	_BIBLIO_CHROME_RE = re.compile(
  2016	    r"\bdoi:\s*10\.\d|crossref reports the following articles citing|"
  2017	    r"volume title publisher|name:\s*\S+\.txt\b|file type:\s*text/",
  2018	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2019	)  # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-A: the bare ISSN alternative moved to the gated ``_is_issn_masthead_chrome``
  2020	#    (ISSNe/ISSNp-aware + over-fire-safe); it is invoked in ``_contains_forensic_chrome`` below.
  2021	_URL_RE = re.compile(r"https?://", re.IGNORECASE)
  2022	_DOI_URL_RE = re.compile(r"https?://(?:dx\.)?doi\.org/", re.IGNORECASE)
  2023	_MIN_URLS_FOR_CHROME = 3       # >=3 bare URLs in one unit => a link list / portal blob
  2024	_MIN_DOI_URLS_FOR_CHROME = 2   # >=2 doi.org URLs => a reference blob
  2025	# A statistics / regression TABLE welded into a unit: a dense run of parenthesised std-errors
  2026	# "(0.018) (0.016) (0.011)" or starred coefficients "0.034* 0.030* 0.027**". A real finding cites
  2027	# one coefficient, never a 3+/2+ run.
  2028	_STATS_TABLE_RE = re.compile(
  2029	    r"(?:\(\s*[-−]?\d+\.\d+\s*\)\s*){3,}|(?:\d+\.\d+\s*\*{1,3}\s*){3,}"
  2030	)
  2031	
  2032	# I-deepfix-002 (#1363) FIX-1 — cookie/consent banner, DOI-registry error page, mixed-script
  2033	# masthead. drb_72 smoke leaked these into cited claims (cookie-wall [10][23][24], DOI-Not-Found
  2034	# error page [25], Russian journal masthead [5][11]); they self-entail strict_verify (text == its
  2035	# own span) so the faithfulness engine cannot catch them — they are page furniture / dead-fetch
  2036	# shells, never a corroborating source. SUPPRESS-only (FLAG-not-drop); engine UNCHANGED.
  2037	_COOKIE_CONSENT_RE = re.compile(
  2038	    r"utiliz\w*\s+technologies\s+such\s+as\s+cookies"
  2039	    r"|we\s+use\s+cookies\s+to\s+enhance\s+your\s+browsing"
  2040	    r"|we\s+value\s+your\s+privacy"
  2041	    r"|analytics,?\s+personali[sz]ation,?\s+and\s+targeted\s+advertising"
  2042	    r"|necessary\s+cookies\s+are\s+required"
  2043	    r"|the\s+technical\s+storage\s+or\s+access\s+(?:is|that\s+is)\s+(?:strictly\s+necessary|used\s+exclusively)"
  2044	    r"|opens\s+(?:in\s+a\s+new\s+window|an\s+external\s+website)"
  2045	    r"|store\s+and/or\s+access\s+information\s+on\s+your\s+device"
  2046	    r"|error\s*[-–—]\s*cookies\s+turned\s+off"
  2047	    r"|cookieabsent"
  2048	    r"|press\s+alt\+1\s+for\s+screen-reader\s+mode"
  2049	    r"|strictly\s+necessary\s+for\s+the\s+legitimate\s+purpose"
  2050	    r"|accept\s+all\s+cookies", re.IGNORECASE)
  2051	_DOI_ERROR_RE = re.compile(
  2052	    r"DOI\s+Not\s+Found"
  2053	    r"|this\s+DOI\s+cannot\s+be\s+found\s+in\s+the\s+DOI\s+System"
  2054	    r"|report\s+this\s+error\s+to\s+the\s+responsible\s+DOI\s+Registration\s+Agency"
  2055	    r"|the\s+DOI\s+has\s+not\s+been\s+activated\s+yet"
  2056	    r"|search\s+again\s+from\s+DOI\.ORG", re.IGNORECASE)
  2057	# A 4+ char non-Latin run (Cyrillic U+0400–052F added — the legacy _NONLATIN_CHAR_RE omitted it)
  2058	# AND a Vol/Issue/№/Том token = a foreign-language journal masthead, not English prose quoting a
  2059	# short foreign term.
  2060	_NONLATIN_MASTHEAD_RUN_RE = re.compile(r"[Ѐ-ԯ؀-ۿ一-鿿぀-ヿ가-힣]{4,}")
  2061	_MASTHEAD_VOL_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"\b(?:Vol\.?|Volume|Issue|No\.)\b|№|Том\b", re.IGNORECASE)
  2062	
  2063	
  2064	def _is_foreign_journal_masthead(text: str) -> bool:
  2065	    return bool(_NONLATIN_MASTHEAD_RUN_RE.search(text) and _MASTHEAD_VOL_TOKEN_RE.search(text))
  2066
