  2068	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  2069	# I-deepfix-001 (#1344) DEFER-4 — residual WHOLE-UNIT page-furniture the FIX-1 (cookie/DOI/foreign-
  2070	# masthead/byline) and legacy categories miss. drb_72 smoke leaked these as cited claims:
  2071	#   A14 publisher PAYWALL call-to-action ("Get full access to this article / View all access and
  2072	#       purchase options for this article." [20]) — the legacy chrome_furniture_screen._PAYWALL_RE
  2073	#       covers Member-only/Feature-Story but not this Sage/Atypon access-wall string.
  2074	#   A15 working-paper COVER masthead + author-opinion DISCLAIMER ("DISCUSSION PAPER SERIES IZA DP
  2075	#       No. 14409 ... Any opinions expressed in this paper are those of the author(s) ..." [19]).
  2076	#   A16 PDF FOOTNOTE / citation-apparatus run ("See OECD (2020), Table 3.3. 14Tate and Yang (2016)
  2077	#       analyze ... 7 Post-merger restructuring." [19]).
  2078	#
  2079	# PRECISION + OVER-STRIP SAFETY (operator-locked drop-path law "over-strip deletes a real finding,
  2080	# worse than a leak"): each rule fires ONLY on a unit that is DOMINANTLY page furniture — a paywall
  2081	# CTA, a series-cover masthead, a footnote/reference run with NO finding clause. A real economics /
  2082	# labor finding never carries these anchors. Units that are a REAL finding welded to a SMALL artifact
  2083	# (A17 "…eliminated.1 1 This number assumes…", A18 "Box 3.1 … In collaboration with Indeed …",
  2084	# A19 "(See Exhibit 1.)", E1 truncated "…not only access to.") are DELIBERATELY NOT matched here —
  2085	# dropping their whole unit would delete the real finding inside, so they are left to the render-seam
  2086	# REPAIR / truncation legs. A20 ("eloundou_gpts_are_gpts") is a SUPPORT sub-bullet source-locator
  2087	# (keep-only surface), not a claim unit, so it is out of this predicate's lane too. FLAG-not-drop:
  2088	# the source row stays in evidence_pool + the credibility disclosure; the faithfulness engine
  2089	# (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role / span-grounding) is UNCHANGED.
  2090	
  2091	# A14 — publisher paywall / "get full access" CTA furniture. Multi-word, access-wall-specific.
  2092	_PAYWALL_ACCESS_RE = re.compile(
  2093	    r"\bget\s+full\s+access\s+to\s+this\s+article\b"
  2094	    r"|\bview\s+all\s+access\s+and\s+purchase\s+options\b"
  2095	    r"|\bpurchase\s+options\s+for\s+this\s+article\b",
  2096	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2097	)
  2098	# A15 — working-paper / discussion-paper COVER masthead + author-opinion DISCLAIMER. Both phrases are
  2099	# series-cover boilerplate a real finding never contains (the working-paper-NUMBER masthead form
  2100	# "Policy Research Working Paper 11057" is already covered by _MASTHEAD_CHROME_RE; this adds the
  2101	# "DISCUSSION PAPER SERIES" series header and the "Any opinions expressed in this paper are those of
  2102	# the author(s)" disclaimer that the IZA cover carries).
  2103	_WORKING_PAPER_COVER_RE = re.compile(
  2104	    r"\bdiscussion\s+paper\s+series\b"
  2105	    r"|\bany\s+opinions?\s+expressed\s+in\s+this\s+paper\s+are\s+those\s+of\s+the\b",
  2106	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2107	)
  2108	# A16 — PDF footnote / citation-apparatus run: a 1-2 digit footnote number GLUED directly to a
  2109	# Capitalized surname ("14Tate and Yang (2016)") or a "See <REF> (year), Table N" cross-reference
  2110	# opener. A real sentence writes "Tate and Yang (2016)" (space, no glue) and never opens "See OECD
  2111	# (2020), Table 3.3.". The glue rule's ``[A-Z][a-z]{2,}`` excludes all-caps tokens (so "4IR", "23
  2112	# OECD") and lowercase (so "165million") — only a footnote-digit welded to a Mixed-case surname.
  2113	_FOOTNOTE_GLUE_RE = re.compile(
  2114	    r"\b\d{1,2}[A-Z][a-z]{2,}\s+(?:and|et\s+al\.?|\(\d{4}\))"
  2115	    r"|\bSee\s+[A-Z][A-Za-z]+(?:\s+(?:and|&)\s+[A-Z][A-Za-z]+)?\s*\(\d{4}\)\s*,?\s+Table\s+\d",
  2116	)
  2117	
  2118	
  2119	def _is_residual_chrome_furniture(text: str) -> bool:
  2120	    """I-deepfix-001 (#1344) DEFER-4: True iff ``text`` is a residual furniture-DOMINATED unit
  2121	    (publisher paywall CTA, working-paper cover masthead/disclaimer, PDF footnote/citation run).
  2122	    High-precision whole-unit screen; a real finding welded to a small artifact is NOT matched."""
  2123	    return bool(
  2124	        _PAYWALL_ACCESS_RE.search(text)
  2125	        or _WORKING_PAPER_COVER_RE.search(text)
  2126	        or _FOOTNOTE_GLUE_RE.search(text)
  2127	    )
  2128	
  2129	
  2130	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  2131	# I-deepfix-001 (#1344) chrome_canary_unblind — three chrome CLASSES the containment predicate was
  2132	# BLIND to (the canary passed 0/226 while the report was saturated with chrome). Each rule is a
  2133	# high-precision CONTAINMENT signal (fires even when the class is welded INTO otherwise-real prose),
  2134	# structure/dual-signal-anchored so it can NEVER flag clean clinical prose:
  2135	#   (a) AUTHOR-AFFILIATION / EMAIL block — an email address CO-OCCURRING with an institution keyword
  2136	#       (a corresponding-author byline: "…, Department of Cardiology, Harvard University. Email:
  2137	#       jsmith@harvard.edu"). A real clinical/research finding never carries a raw email address, and
  2138	#       the email+institution DUAL signal never co-occurs in substantive prose (precision-first per
  2139	#       §-1.3: recall is secondary, over-strip is worse). The email alone is NOT enough (a finding
  2140	#       could conceivably quote one); both signals are required.
  2141	#   (b) TABLE-OF-CONTENTS DOT-LEADERS — a run of 4+ leader dots (a normal ellipsis is exactly 3)
  2142	#       followed by a page number ("Introduction ......... 12"). Consecutive-dot runs with a trailing
  2143	#       page number are ToC furniture; a decimal table ("0.034 0.030") has digits BETWEEN the dots so
  2144	#       it never matches.
  2145	#   (c) COOKIE / CONSENT banner — the "By clicking/continuing … you accept/agree/consent" consent-CTA
  2146	#       phrasing the legacy ``_COOKIE_CONSENT_RE`` alternation missed. Bounded gap (no ``.``/newline)
  2147	#       between the two anchors keeps it from spanning unrelated sentences.
  2148	# FLAG-not-drop / detector-only: a flagged unit is withheld from the rendered rollup and KEPT in
  2149	# evidence; the faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role / provenance / span-grounding) is
  2150	# UNCHANGED. Gated by the caller under ``render_chrome_screen_enabled()`` (default ON).
  2151	_AFFIL_EMAIL_ADDRESS_RE = re.compile(
  2152	    r"[A-Za-z0-9._%+\-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.\-]+\.[A-Za-z]{2,}"
  2153	)
  2154	_AFFIL_INSTITUTION_KEYWORD_RE = re.compile(
  2155	    r"\b(?:Universit(?:y|ies|[àáäé]|e)|Universidad|Universit[àé]|Department|Departamento|"
  2156	    r"Institut(?:e|o|ion)?|College|Hospital|Clinic|Laborator(?:y|ies)|Faculty|Facultad|"
  2157	    r"Escuela|Polytechnic|Academy|Ministry)\b",
  2158	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2159	)
  2160	_TOC_DOTLEADER_RE = re.compile(r"(?:\.[ \t]*){4,}\d{1,4}\b")
  2161	_COOKIE_BY_CLICKING_RE = re.compile(
  2162	    r"\bby\s+(?:clicking|continuing|using|browsing)\b[^.\n]{0,80}?"
  2163	    r"\byou\s+(?:accept|agree|consent)\b",
  2164	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2165	)
  2166	
  2167	
  2168	def _contains_missed_chrome_class(text: str) -> bool:
  2169	    """I-deepfix-001 (#1344) chrome_canary_unblind: True iff ``text`` CONTAINS one of the three
  2170	    high-precision chrome classes the legacy containment predicate was blind to — an author-
  2171	    affiliation/email byline, a ToC dot-leader run, or a "By clicking … you accept" consent banner.
  2172	    Detector-only (FLAG-not-drop); the faithfulness engine is UNCHANGED."""
  2173	    if _AFFIL_EMAIL_ADDRESS_RE.search(text) and _AFFIL_INSTITUTION_KEYWORD_RE.search(text):
  2174	        return True
  2175	    if _TOC_DOTLEADER_RE.search(text):
  2176	        return True
  2177	    return bool(_COOKIE_BY_CLICKING_RE.search(text))
  2178	
  2179	
  2180	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  2181	# I-wire-016 (#1338) gap-fill — precision-safe furniture rules the legacy categories miss (the OSS
  2182	# survey confirmed no fetch-time HTML extractor fits the render seam; extend the deterministic
  2183	# predicate). Codex iter-1/2/3 removed every rule whose surface form overlaps a real finding (biblio
  2184	# date+page, bibliometric stats, "Name<digit>, <digit>" superscript), leaving the unambiguous
  2185	# affiliation-glued / title+affiliation / author-attribution-phrase rules. VALIDATED precision-first:
  2186	# ZERO of the 398 curated-clean real-content units are flagged; every Codex adversarial real-finding
  2187	# case is KEPT. Under-removal is the safe direction (recall secondary per §-1.3); the chrome-as-claim
  2188	# canary backstops the rarer residual classes. FLAG-not-drop: a flagged unit is withheld from the
  2189	# rendered rollup, KEPT in evidence; the faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role / span) is UNCHANGED.
  2190	#
  2191	# gap 1 — a digit GLUED to an institution keyword ANCHORED to its affiliation preposition (Department
  2192	# OF, Laboratory OF/FOR/AT, Institute OF/FOR, …) so an adjective ("2Laboratory-confirmed cases",
  2193	# "1Institutional review boards") never matches (Codex iter-1 P1). Real prose spells "a/one/the department";
  2194	# only an author-block superscript glues a digit directly to "Department of"/"Institute of"/etc.
  2195	_AFFIL_GLUED_RE = re.compile(
  2196	    r"\b\d{1,2}(?:Department\s+(?:of|for)\b|Departamento\s+de\b|Faculty\s+of\b|School\s+of\b|"
  2197	    r"Institute\s+(?:of|for)\b|University\s+of\b|Universidad\s+de\b|Facultad\s+de\b|Escuela\s+de\b|"
  2198	    r"Laborator(?:y|ies)\s+(?:of|for|at)\b|Centre\s+for\b|Center\s+for\b)",
  2199	)
  2200	# gap 4 — title+affiliation composite: a dash + digit + institution ("A Survey of … - 1 Department of …").
  2201	_TITLE_AFFIL_RE = re.compile(
  2202	    r"[-–—]\s*\d{1,2}\s+(?:Department\s+of|Institute\s+(?:of|for)|Faculty\s+of|School\s+of|"
  2203	    r"University\s+of|Laborator(?:y|ies)\s+(?:of|for|at)|Centre\s+for|Center\s+for)\b",
  2204	)
  2205	# gap 1 — author-attribution MASTHEAD block: the authorship phrase ("X is listed as an author",
  2206	# "… are among the listed authors") AND a co-occurring article-portal MASTHEAD signal (the
  2207	# "article has received N accesses/citations/altmetric" engagement-stats furniture). Codex iter-4 P1:
  2208	# the phrase ALONE flags a real research-integrity finding ("X is listed as an author on the retracted
  2209	# paper"); requiring BOTH the phrase AND the portal-stats co-signal anchors it to the masthead block
  2210	# ("Gazdag is listed as an author. The article has received 3258 accesses, 16 citations…") — a real
  2211	# integrity/COI finding never co-reports portal engagement stats. Both signals required (precision-first).
  2212	_AUTHOR_ATTRIB_PHRASE_RE = re.compile(
  2213	    r"\bis listed as an?\s+(?:author|co-author)\b|\bare among the listed authors\b|"
  2214	    r"\blisted as (?:the\s+)?(?:author|co-author)s?\b",
  2215	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2216	)
  2217	_MASTHEAD_PORTAL_STATS_RE = re.compile(
  2218	    # Codex iter-5 P1: the co-signal must be a TRUE portal-only metric (a number directly followed by
  2219	    # "accesses" or "altmetric") — masthead engagement counts a research finding never reports. Bare
  2220	    # "N citations" and unconstrained "article has received" are REMOVED: a real integrity/bibliometrics
  2221	    # finding legitimately says "received 18 citations before correction", so they are not portal-unique.
  2222	    r"\b\d[\d,]*\s+(?:accesses|altmetric)\b",
  2223	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2224	)
  2225	# DROPPED (Codex iter-1/2/3, not precision-safe — surface form overlaps real findings):
  2226	#  - gap 2 biblio date+page ("…, July 12, p. 36" vs "The July 12, p. 36 article reported…").
  2227	#  - gap 3 bibliometric stats ("3,258 accesses, 16 citations, 7 altmetric" vs real bibliometrics findings;
  2228	#    "vascular accesses"). The author-attribution phrase above catches the masthead blocks these appeared in.
  2229	#  - gap 1 "Name<digit>, <digit>" author-superscript (titlecase mouse-gene notation "Smad1, 5 and Smad2, 3").
  2230	# These rare residual classes are left to the chrome-as-claim canary (enforce, floor 0.05) per §-1.3
  2231	# (precision over recall — never risk dropping a real finding).
  2232	
  2233	
  2234	def _contains_iwire016_gap_furniture(s: str) -> bool:
  2235	    """I-wire-016 #1338: precision-safe gap-class furniture rules (validated 0 content false-positives;
  2236	    Codex iter-1/2/3 removed every rule whose surface form overlaps a real finding). Catches the
  2237	    affiliation/author-attribution masthead blocks; rarer stats/biblio/superscript classes are left to
  2238	    the chrome-as-claim canary. FLAG-not-drop: withheld from rollup, kept in evidence; faithfulness UNCHANGED."""
  2239	    if _AFFIL_GLUED_RE.search(s) or _TITLE_AFFIL_RE.search(s):
  2240	        return True
  2241	    # author-attribution masthead: the authorship phrase AND a portal-stats co-signal (both required —
  2242	    # Codex iter-4 P1: the phrase alone flags a real integrity/COI finding).
  2243	    return bool(_AUTHOR_ATTRIB_PHRASE_RE.search(s) and _MASTHEAD_PORTAL_STATS_RE.search(s))
  2244	
  2245	
  2246	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  2247	# I-deepfix-001 (#1344) drb72_apparatus_unblind — three chrome CLASSES that leaked into cited
  2248	# CLAIMS (and into the Abstract + Conclusion sandwich) of the drb_72 report because no enumerated
  2249	# rule covered them and chrome self-entails strict_verify (text == its own span) so the faithfulness
  2250	# engine is structurally blind to furniture. All are high-precision CONTAINMENT / structure signals,
  2251	# dual-signal / structure-anchored so they can NEVER flag a real economics / labor / clinical finding
  2252	# (precision-first per §-1.3: fail-OPEN on ambiguity — over-strip is worse than a leak). FLAG-not-drop
  2253	# / detector-only: a flagged unit is WITHHELD from the rendered rollup and from the abstract/conclusion
  2254	# harvest, KEPT in evidence + the credibility disclosure; the faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI /
  2255	# 4-role / provenance / span-grounding) is UNCHANGED. Gated by the caller under
  2256	# ``render_chrome_screen_enabled()`` (default ON).
  2257	#
  2258	#   (1) CITATION-COUNTER / CITEDBY-PATH API blob — a scraped citation-metrics API response
  2259	#       ("… includes the values 54719037, 1074, and 1837 … references path …"). The furniture
  2260	#       markers are an API field/path token (``citedby`` / ``references path`` / a crossref-openalex
  2261	#       API host). ``citedby`` and the API host are furniture on their own (a real finding never
  2262	#       writes them). ``references path`` is dual-signal-guarded — it must co-occur with a BARE 5+
  2263	#       digit integer (an unformatted entity/citation id like ``54719037``; a real finding writes a
  2264	#       grouped number ``54,719,037`` or ``$54 million``, never a bare 8-digit id) within the clause.
  2265	#   (2) VERSION-HEADER cover block — the SSRN / working-paper cover version furniture
  2266	#       ("This version: March 18, 2026  First version: August 16, 2025  Please click here for the
  2267	#       latest version."). ``This/First version:`` is dual-signal-guarded (must be followed by a
  2268	#       month name or a digit — a DATE, not the prose "in this version, we …"); the "please click …
  2269	#       for the latest version" CTA is unambiguous furniture on its own.
  2270	#   (3) FIGURE-CAPTION / AXIS apparatus — CAPTION/AXIS-ONLY (Codex #1344 P1 tighten). The prior
  2271	#       rule matched "Figure A2 replicates … Figure 12" / "for each quintile is as follows" ANYWHERE,
  2272	#       so a hit ate real result prose and dropped its citation unit. The rule now matches ONLY a span
  2273	#       whose WHOLE sentence is pure figure/axis furniture: a bare figure-to-figure caption cross-
  2274	#       reference ("Figure A2 replicates the prior analysis in Figure 12.") or a table axis lead-in
  2275	#       that ENDS at the descriptor colon with no data row ("… for each quintile is as follows:"). It
  2276	#       is anchored ^…$ over a SINGLE sentence (``[^.]*`` never crosses a period), so a welded methods
  2277	#       sentence that merely describes what a figure does is NOT eaten. A KEEP guard adds a second
  2278	#       fail-open safety: if the span ALSO carries a result verb/qualifier (shows/finds/reports/remains/
  2279	#       increase/decrease/negative/positive/significant/…) OR a numeric RESULT (a decimal, a percent, a
  2280	#       p-value, a dollar/grouped magnitude — a bare figure id like "A2"/"12"/"[22]" is NOT a result
  2281	#       number), the span is real finding prose and is KEPT. A real finding that merely CITES a figure
  2282	#       ("As shown in Figure 12, employment rose across each quintile") carries neither anchor.
  2283	_CITEDBY_API_RE = re.compile(
  2284	    r"\bcitedby\b"
  2285	    r"|\b(?:api\.crossref\.org|api\.openalex\.org)\b",
  2286	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2287	)
  2288	_REFERENCES_PATH_RE = re.compile(r"\breferences[\s\-]?path\b", re.IGNORECASE)
  2289	_BARE_ENTITY_ID_RE = re.compile(r"(?<![\d.])\d{5,}(?![\d.])")
  2290	_VERSION_HEADER_RE = re.compile(
  2291	    r"\b(?:this|first|current|previous|earlier)\s+version\s*:\s*"
  2292	    r"(?:jan(?:uary)?|feb(?:ruary)?|mar(?:ch)?|apr(?:il)?|may|jun(?:e)?|jul(?:y)?|"
  2293	    r"aug(?:ust)?|sep(?:tember)?|oct(?:ober)?|nov(?:ember)?|dec(?:ember)?|\d)"
  2294	    r"|\bplease\s+click\s+here\s+for\s+the\s+(?:latest|most\s+recent)\s+version\b",
  2295	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2296	)
  2297	# CAPTION/AXIS-ONLY figure apparatus (Codex #1344 P1 tighten): anchored ^…$ over a SINGLE
  2298	# sentence so ONLY a pure caption/axis stub matches; ``[^.]*`` never crosses a sentence period,
  2299	# so a welded methods sentence is structurally excluded.
  2300	_FIGURE_APPARATUS_RE = re.compile(
  2301	    # a bare figure-to-figure caption cross-reference stub (the whole sentence is the cross-ref)
  2302	    # I-deepfix-001 c-fix (iter3): the second Figure ref must be effectively sentence-final —
  2303	    # only whitespace / period / trailing cite may follow it. This fails OPEN on any substantive
  2304	    # trailing result prose ("...and confirms the relationship is robust..."), which is real
  2305	    # finding text, not caption furniture.
  2306	    r"^\W*Figure\s+[A-Z]?\d+\s+replicates\b[^.]*?\bFigure\s+[A-Z]?\d+\b\s*\.?\s*(?:\[\d+\])?\s*$"
  2307	    # a table axis lead-in that ENDS at the descriptor colon (no data row follows)
  2308	    r"|^\W*[^.]*?\bfor\s+each\s+quintile\s+is\s+as\s+follows\s*:\s*(?:\[\d+\])?\s*$",
  2309	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2310	)
  2311	# KEEP guard (fail-open, §-1.3): a result verb/qualifier marks real finding prose — never furniture.
  2312	_FIGURE_RESULT_VERB_RE = re.compile(
  2313	    r"\b(?:shows?|showed|finds?|found|reports?|reported|reveal(?:s|ed)?|remains?|remained|"
  2314	    # I-deepfix-001 c-fix (iter3): result verbs Codex flagged as missing — a welded result
  2315	    # sentence using any of these is KEPT (fail-open), never dropped as furniture.
  2316	    r"confirms?|confirmed|demonstrat\w+|indicat\w+|establish\w+|suggest\w+|imply|implies|implied|"
  2317	    r"robust|consistent|"
  2318	    r"increas(?:e|es|ed|ing)|decreas(?:e|es|ed|ing)|rose|rise[sn]?|risen|fell|fall(?:s|en|ing)?|"
  2319	    r"declin\w+|grew|grow(?:s|ing)?|widen\w+|narrow\w+|"
  2320	    r"negative|positive|significant(?:ly)?|associat\w+|correlat\w+|"
  2321	    r"higher|lower|greater|elevat\w+|reduc\w+|gradient|elasticity|coefficient)\b",
  2322	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2323	)
  2324	# KEEP guard (fail-open, §-1.3): a numeric RESULT (decimal / percent / p-value / grouped or dollar
  2325	# magnitude). A bare figure/table id ("A2", "12", "[22]") is NOT a result number.
  2326	_FIGURE_RESULT_NUMBER_RE = re.compile(
  2327	    r"\d\.\d"                                         # a decimal value (4.2, 0.05)
  2328	    r"|\d\s?%|\bpercent\b|\bpercentage\s+points?\b"   # a percentage
  2329	    r"|\bp\s?[<>=]\s?0?\.\d"                          # a p-value
  2330	    r"|\$\s?\d"                                       # a dollar amount
  2331	    r"|\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})+",                           # a grouped thousands magnitude
  2332	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2333	)
  2334	
  2335	
  2336	def _figure_apparatus_is_pure_furniture(text: str) -> bool:
  2337	    """I-deepfix-001 (#1344): True iff ``text`` is a CAPTION/AXIS-ONLY figure-apparatus stub with no
  2338	    real result content. Fail-open (§-1.3): a span that ALSO carries a result verb/qualifier or a
  2339	    numeric result is real finding prose and is KEPT (returns False), never withheld — this is the
  2340	    Codex-#1344-P1 tighten that stops the rule eating result prose and dropping its citation unit."""
  2341	    if not _FIGURE_APPARATUS_RE.search(text):
  2342	        return False
  2343	    if _FIGURE_RESULT_VERB_RE.search(text) or _FIGURE_RESULT_NUMBER_RE.search(text):
  2344	        return False  # KEEP: a real finding welded with a figure/axis reference
  2345	    return True
  2346	
  2347	
  2348	def _contains_drb72_apparatus_chrome(text: str) -> bool:
  2349	    """I-deepfix-001 (#1344): True iff ``text`` CONTAINS one of the three drb_72 apparatus chrome
  2350	    classes the enumerated denylist was blind to — a citation-counter/citedby-path API blob, an
  2351	    SSRN/working-paper version-header cover block, or a CAPTION/AXIS-ONLY figure-apparatus stub.
  2352	    High-precision / dual-signal-anchored (never flags a real finding). Detector-only
  2353	    (FLAG-not-drop); the faithfulness engine is UNCHANGED."""
  2354	    if _CITEDBY_API_RE.search(text):
  2355	        return True
  2356	    if _REFERENCES_PATH_RE.search(text) and _BARE_ENTITY_ID_RE.search(text):
  2357	        return True
  2358	    if _VERSION_HEADER_RE.search(text):
  2359	        return True
  2360	    return _figure_apparatus_is_pure_furniture(text)
  2361	
  2362	
  2363	def _dotted_toc_hits(text: str) -> int:
  2364	    """Count dotted section-number tokens whose TitleCase word is NOT a magnitude unit (so a
  2365	    "3.2 Million / 4.5 Billion" magnitude pair contributes ZERO ToC hits)."""
  2366	    return sum(
  2367	        1 for word in _DOTTED_SECTION_TOKEN_RE.findall(text)
  2368	        if word.lower() not in _MAGNITUDE_UNIT_WORDS
  2369	    )
  2370	
  2371	
  2372	def _is_predominantly_nonlatin(text: str) -> bool:
  2373	    """True iff ``text`` carries a long non-Latin run AND its non-Latin characters outnumber its
  2374	    Latin letters — a foreign-page scrape, not an English finding quoting a short foreign term."""
  2375	    if not _NONLATIN_RUN_RE.search(text):
  2376	        return False
  2377	    nonlatin = len(_NONLATIN_CHAR_RE.findall(text))
  2378	    latin = len(re.findall(r"[A-Za-z]", text))
  2379	    return nonlatin >= _MIN_NONLATIN_RUN_CHARS and nonlatin >= latin
  2380	
  2381	
  2382	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  2383	# A1+A2 (I-wire Wave-A) — the render-seam chrome classes the drb_72 audit found the containment
  2384	# predicate STILL blind to. At iter-3b the set is TWO high-precision / structure-anchored rules: a
  2385	# title-page / monograph MASTHEAD and a BIBLIOGRAPHY-fragment. (A pure TABLE/FIGURE CAPTION-stub rule
  2386	# was tried and REMOVED — a present-tense captioned finding could not be separated from a bare
  2387	# caption without over-stripping; see the note where the class used to live below.) Each rule is
  2388	# FLAG-not-drop (a flagged unit is withheld from the rendered rollup and KEPT in evidence_pool +
  2389	# the disclosure); the faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role / provenance) is UNCHANGED.
  2390	#
  2391	# (1) TITLE-PAGE / MONOGRAPH MASTHEAD — an ALL-CAPS "<MONTH> <YEAR> <DOC-TYPE>" cover header
  2392	#     ("JUNE 2011 RESEARCH", "MARCH 2020 WORKING PAPER"). It fires ONLY on a PURE all-caps line: the
  2393	#     trailing guard ``(?![^\n]*[a-z])`` requires NO lowercase letter anywhere after the doc type, so
  2394	#     any running-prose sentence — which ALWAYS carries a lowercase letter, whether the continuation
  2395	#     is lowercase ("… RESEARCH: employment rose …") OR title-case ("… RESEARCH: Employment rose …")
  2396	#     — can NEVER match. ``(?m)^`` + an optional bounded leading ALL-CAPS institute/series run
  2397	#     ("CENTRE FOR ECONOMIC POLICY JUNE 2011 …") anchor the genuine cover-header form. A masthead that
  2398	#     carries "No. 8452" is LEAKED (its "o" trips the guard): the safe direction, since over-strip of
  2399	#     a real finding is worse than a leaked masthead (§-1.3 drop-path law).
  2400	_TITLE_PAGE_MASTHEAD_RE = re.compile(
  2401	    r"(?m)^\W{0,4}"
  2402	    r"(?:[A-Z][A-Z&.'/-]*\s+){0,6}"
  2403	    r"\b(?:JANUARY|FEBRUARY|MARCH|APRIL|MAY|JUNE|JULY|AUGUST|SEPTEMBER|OCTOBER|NOVEMBER|DECEMBER)"
  2404	    r"\s+(?:19|20)\d{2}\s+"
  2405	    r"(?:RESEARCH|REPORT|WORKING\s+PAPER|DISCUSSION\s+PAPER|WHITE\s+PAPER|POLICY\s+BRIEF|"
  2406	    r"BRIEFING|BULLETIN|MONOGRAPH|PREPRINT)\b"
  2407	    # Codex P1 (Wave-A iter-3b): fire ONLY on a pure ALL-CAPS masthead line. A real sentence ALWAYS
  2408	    # carries a lowercase letter somewhere after the doc type — whether the continuation is lowercase
  2409	    # ("JUNE 2011 RESEARCH: employment rose …") OR title-case ("… RESEARCH: Employment rose …") — so
  2410	    # requiring NO lowercase letter to end-of-line rejects every running-prose sentence. A masthead
  2411	    # that legitimately carries "No. 8452" is LEAKED (its "o" trips the guard), which is the safe
  2412	    # direction: over-strip of a real finding is worse than a leaked masthead (§-1.3 drop-path law).
  2413	    r"(?![^\n]*[a-z])"
  2414	)
  2415	# (2) BIBLIOGRAPHY fragment — a reference-list locator a real finding sentence never contains: a
  2416	#     "pp. 45-67" page range, a "Retrieved from http…" / "Accessed <date>" retrieval line, or an
  2417	#     "In: <Editor> (Ed(s).)" book-chapter opener. DELIBERATELY OMITTED: a bare "12(3): 45-67"
  2418	#     volume(issue):pages locator — it collides with real clinical prose ("in arm 2 (3): 45-60
  2419	#     patients responded"), and over-strip of a real finding is worse than a leak (§-1.3). An
  2420	#     author-block-glued-to-"Abstract" byline is ALSO deliberately not screened here: it cannot be
  2421	#     separated from real academic/clinical prose ("Patients at Massachusetts General Hospital showed
  2422	#     improved Abstract Reasoning scores") without over-stripping — genuine title pages carry an
  2423	#     ORCID / email / superscript-affiliation signal already caught by ``_contains_missed_chrome_class``
  2424	#     and ``_contains_iwire016_gap_furniture``.
  2425	_BIBLIOGRAPHY_FRAGMENT_RE = re.compile(
  2426	    r"\bpp\.\s*\d+\s*[-–—]\s*\d+\b"
  2427	    r"|\bRetrieved\s+from\s+https?://"
  2428	    r"|\bAccessed\s+(?:on\s+)?\d{1,2}\s+[A-Za-z]+\s+\d{4}\b"
  2429	    r"|\bIn:\s+[A-Z][A-Za-z.\s,&]+?\(Eds?\.\)",
  2430	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2431	)
  2432	# (3) PURE TABLE / FIGURE CAPTION stub — REMOVED at Wave-A iter-3b (Codex P1). A caption-opening unit
  2433	#     carries a real PRESENT-TENSE finding whose verb no finite whitelist can enumerate and which has
  2434	#     no -ed/-ing morphology ("Table 1. Patients receive standard care after randomization.[1]",
  2435	#     "Figure 2: The low-dose arms lack measurable benefit.[1]"), so any caption-stub screen
  2436	#     over-withholds real findings. Per §-1.3 (over-strip is worse than a leak) the table/figure
  2437	#     caption class is DEFERRED — it cannot be separated from real captioned findings without a real
  2438	#     clause parser. Masthead + bibliography-fragment (high-precision, structure-anchored) remain.
  2439	
  2440	
  2441	def _contains_missed_titlepage_biblio_caption(text: str) -> bool:
  2442	    """A1+A2 (I-wire Wave-A): True iff ``text`` CONTAINS a still-missing render-seam chrome class — an
  2443	    ALL-CAPS title-page/monograph masthead OR an unambiguous bibliography-fragment locator. (The
  2444	    table/figure caption class was removed at iter-3b — it could not be separated from real captioned
  2445	    findings without over-stripping.) High-precision / detector-only (FLAG-not-drop); the faithfulness
  2446	    engine is UNCHANGED."""
  2447	    if _TITLE_PAGE_MASTHEAD_RE.search(text):
  2448	        return True
  2449	    return bool(_BIBLIOGRAPHY_FRAGMENT_RE.search(text))
  2450	
  2451	
  2452	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  2453	# I-deepfix-001 P1_chrome_gate (#1344) — the SEVEN box1 render-seam chrome CLASSES the containment
  2454	# predicate was empirically proven blind to (all 8 shipped box1 chrome strings returned False; all
  2455	# three nets that route through ``_contains_forensic_chrome`` — the render-seam sanitize pass, the
  2456	# chrome canary, and the verified-compose K-span junk screen — failed together). Each rule is a
  2457	# high-precision, label/structure-anchored CONTAINMENT signal (fires even when the class is welded
  2458	# INTO otherwise-real prose) that can NEVER flag a real economics / labor / clinical finding
  2459	# (precision-first per §-1.3: over-strip of a real finding is worse than a leaked furniture unit).
  2460	# FLAG-not-drop / suppress-only: a flagged unit is WITHHELD from the rendered rollup and KEPT in
  2461	# evidence_pool + the disclosure; the faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role / provenance
  2462	# / span-grounding) is UNCHANGED. Gated by the caller under ``render_chrome_screen_enabled()``.
  2463	# Frontier basis: trafilatura 2.1 / jusText stopword-density boilerplate SIGNALS ported as a
  2464	# text-level predicate (the tools need raw HTML the render seam no longer has).
  2465	#
  2466	#   (1) PUBLISHER PAYWALL / PURCHASE CTA — "Add to cart", "Purchase this article", "Subscribe for
  2467	#       unlimited", "Rent this article", "printable version". Distinct from the legacy
  2468	#       ``_PAYWALL_ACCESS_RE`` (Sage/Atypon "get full access to this article") — this covers the
  2469	#       cart/subscription CTA form. Multi-word, CTA-specific; a finding never carries these.
  2470	#   (2) MULTILINGUAL LICENSE / REPOSITORY furniture — German repository boilerplate
  2471	#       ("Standard-Nutzungsbedingungen", "EconStor", "Die Dokumente auf …", "zu eigenen
  2472	#       wissenschaftlichen Zwecken"). Distinctive repository tokens a real English finding never
  2473	#       contains. ("Terms of Use" alone is deliberately NOT screened — too generic.)
  2474	#   (3) GLUED AUTHOR-STATS-TABLE — either a Stata summary-table header run ("Variable Obs Mean
  2475	#       Std. Dev. Min Max") OR >=2 glued "Surname<digit>" author-superscript tokens
  2476	#       ("Kanbach1 Heiduk2 Kraus3"). The surname-digit rule is the RISKY one (a clinical
  2477	#       "Group1 … Group2" could collide), so it is GUARDED by ``_stopword_density`` < the floor:
  2478	#       a pure author list has near-zero stopwords while real prose does not.
  2479	#   (4) ASTERISKED-AUTHOR STREET + ZIP affiliation block — a US "City, ST 02142" postal block
  2480	#       (unambiguous), or a corresponding-author marker co-occurring with a street address. A real
  2481	#       finding never carries a full postal address.
  2482	#   (5) EXEC / PROMO BIO — a job-title ("Chief Executive Officer", "CEO", "Founder", "Managing
  2483	#       Director") WELDED to a promo predicate ("visionary", "thought leader", "award-winning",
  2484	#       "driving digital transformation"). DUAL-signal: a real finding that merely names a CEO
  2485	#       ("the CEO announced layoffs") carries no promo predicate and is KEPT.
  2486	#   (6) STITCHED METADATA-RECITAL citation — a reference recital ("… journal article, volume 42,
  2487	#       article 7, authored by …"). The "journal article" + "volume N" + ("article N" | "authored
  2488	#       by") co-occurrence is a stitched biblio recital a finding never writes.
  2489	#   (7) SHORT NAV / TOPIC-LIST item — the RISKY short-nav rule, guarded on FOUR ANDed conditions:
  2490	#       word-count <= 6 AND ends with a bare ordinal ("Labor Market Trends 3.2") AND no finite verb
  2491	#       AND ``_stopword_density`` < the floor. All four together isolate a scraped ToC/nav entry
  2492	#       from a real short sentence (which carries a verb and stopwords).
  2493	_PAYWALL_CTA_BOX1_RE = re.compile(
  2494	    r"\badd\s+to\s+cart\b"
  2495	    r"|\bpurchase\s+(?:this\s+)?(?:article|pdf|access|subscription)\b"
  2496	    r"|\brent\s+(?:this\s+)?article\b"
  2497	    r"|\bbuy\s+(?:now|this\s+article|the\s+pdf)\b"
  2498	    r"|\bsubscribe\s+(?:for|to\s+get)\s+(?:unlimited|full|instant)\b"
  2499	    r"|\bstart\s+your\s+free\s+trial\b"
  2500	    r"|\bprintable\s+version\b",
  2501	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2502	)
  2503	_REPO_LICENSE_FURNITURE_RE = re.compile(
  2504	    r"\bStandard-?Nutzungsbedingungen\b"
  2505	    r"|\bNutzungsbedingungen\b"
  2506	    r"|\bEconStor\b"
  2507	    r"|\bLeibniz[- ]Informationszentrum\b"
  2508	    r"|\bzu\s+eigenen\s+wissenschaftlichen\s+Zwecken\b"
  2509	    r"|\bDie\s+Dokumente\s+auf\b",
  2510	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2511	)
  2512	_STATS_SUMMARY_HEADER_RE = re.compile(
  2513	    r"\bObs\.?\s+Mean\b"
  2514	    r"|\bMean\s+Std\.?\s*Dev\.?\b"
  2515	    r"|\bVariable\s+Obs\b"
  2516	    r"|\bStd\.?\s*Dev\.?\s+Min\s+Max\b",
  2517	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2518	)
  2519	# A glued author-superscript token: a name-like stem (>=3 letters, any case, so an OCR-mangled
  2520	# "bALACHANDER2" byline surname counts while "Q1" does not) welded — OR joined by ONE space — to a
  2521	# 1-2 digit affiliation superscript that is NOT part of a decimal / percent / longer number
  2522	# (``(?![\w.%])``). The finite finding-label allowlist (Group / Stage / Type / ...) is DROPPED: it was
  2523	# open-ended and could never enumerate every real TWO-CATEGORY label ("High School1 Low College2",
  2524	# "Blue Collar1 White Collar2" — School / College / Collar are not authorable in any finite list), so
  2525	# it still over-stripped real labor / economic findings (Codex blocker). Instead rule 3b is anchored to
  2526	# the STRONGER author-LIST structure a real finding never carries: >=3 such surname-digit pairs, OR
  2527	# exactly 2 pairs PLUS an author/affiliation CO-SIGNAL in the same unit (see ``_AUTHOR_COSIGNAL_RE``).
  2528	# Two bare category-labels (exactly 2 pairs, no co-signal) therefore NEVER trip it, while a genuine
  2529	# glued byline (5 welded names, or a spaced "Surname 2, Surname 1, First Last 2" OCR list, or 2 names +
  2530	# an affiliation) still fires. Precision-first per §-1.3: over-stripping a real finding is the harm.
  2531	_SURNAME_DIGIT_PAIR_RE = re.compile(r"\b([A-Za-z]{3,})[ ]?(\d{1,2})(?![\w.%])")
  2532	# An author/affiliation co-signal that upgrades EXACTLY 2 surname-digit pairs to an author byline: an
  2533	# affiliation keyword (University / Institute / College / Department as a WHOLE word — "\bCollege\b"
  2534	# never matches the welded "College2" in a labelled finding), an "et al." marker, or an email address.
  2535	# A finite, high-precision set; still ANDed under the stopword-density guard so real prose that merely
  2536	# names an institution ("Researchers at Stanford University found Group1 and Group2 differed" — density
  2537	# above the floor) is NOT upgraded. Precision-first per §-1.3.
  2538	#
  2539	# The superscript author ASTERISK is deliberately NOT an author co-signal at ALL — not even the
  2540	# ">=2 starred pairs" form the iter-1 fix used. A "*" welded to a "Surname<digit>" token is byte-
  2541	# identical whether it is an author corresponding-author marker ("Jane Smith1* John Doe2*") OR a
  2542	# statistical / footnote SIGNIFICANCE STAR on a category label ("High School1* Low College2*
  2543	# earnings differed" — TWO starred category labels, no independent author signal). The iter-1
  2544	# ">=2 starred pairs" heuristic could not tell these apart and over-stripped the real two-category /
  2545	# table finding (Codex iter-2 P1 blocker). So the asterisk path now requires an INDEPENDENT author
  2546	# signal (``_AUTHOR_COSIGNAL_RE``): the exactly-2-pair upgrade fires ONLY on an affiliation keyword /
  2547	# "et al." / email. Precision-first per §-1.3: a genuine bare-stars-only two-author byline that
  2548	# carries no affiliation/email/et-al ("Jane Smith1* John Doe2*") is now an ACCEPTED LEAK (leaked page
  2549	# furniture is far lower harm than deleting a real clinical / labor / economic finding); the >=3-pair
  2550	# path still catches any real glued author LIST, and 2 names + a real affiliation still fires.
  2551	_AUTHOR_COSIGNAL_RE = re.compile(
  2552	    r"\b(?:University|Institute|College|Department)\b"
  2553	    r"|\bet\s+al\b"
  2554	    r"|[\w.+-]+@[\w-]+\.[A-Za-z]{2,}",
  2555	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2556	)
  2557	
  2558	
  2559	def _surname_digit_pair_count(text: str) -> int:
  2560	    """Count "Surname<digit>" author-superscript pairs (welded ``Kanbach1`` or single-space ``Archbold
  2561	    2``), with NO finding-label allowlist — the pair COUNT plus an author/affiliation co-signal (not a
  2562	    per-word allowlist) is what separates a genuine glued byline from a real two-category finding. See
  2563	    ``_SURNAME_DIGIT_PAIR_RE`` and the rule-3b call site for the >=3 / 2+co-signal structure."""
  2564	    return len(_SURNAME_DIGIT_PAIR_RE.findall(text))
  2565	# A US "City, ST 02142" postal block. On its OWN this over-strips a real finding that merely cites a
  2566	# place (Codex P1 iter 1); it is chrome ONLY with an affiliation CO-SIGNAL (a street address or a
  2567	# corresponding-author marker), so rule 4 ANDs it below.
  2568	_US_CITY_STATE_ZIP_RE = re.compile(r"\b[A-Z][A-Za-z.\-]+,\s+[A-Z]{2}\s+\d{5}(?:-\d{4})?\b")
  2569	_CORRESP_AUTHOR_RE = re.compile(
  2570	    r"\*\s*correspond|\bcorrespond(?:ing|ence)\s+(?:author|to)\b", re.IGNORECASE
  2571	)
  2572	_STREET_ADDRESS_RE = re.compile(
  2573	    r"\b\d{1,5}\s+(?:[A-Z][a-z]+\s+){1,4}"
  2574	    r"(?:Street|St\.|Avenue|Ave\.?|Road|Rd\.?|Drive|Dr\.?|Boulevard|Blvd\.?|Lane|Ln\.?|"
  2575	    r"Way|Square|Sq\.?|Court|Ct\.?)\b"
  2576	)
  2577	_EXEC_TITLE_RE = re.compile(
  2578	    r"\bchief\s+\w+\s+officer\b|\bC[EFOT]O\b|\b(?:co-)?founder\b|\bmanaging\s+director\b|"
  2579	    r"\bpresident\s+and\s+ceo\b|\bvice\s+president\b|\bexecutive\s+director\b|\bpartner\s+at\b",
  2580	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2581	)
  2582	_PROMO_PREDICATE_RE = re.compile(
  2583	    r"\bvisionary\b|\bthought\s+leader(?:ship)?\b|\bpassionate\s+about\b|\baward[- ]winning\b|"
  2584	    r"\bworld[- ]class\b|\bleading\s+expert\b|\bdriving\s+(?:digital\s+)?transformation\b|"
  2585	    r"\brenowned\b|\bseasoned\s+(?:leader|executive|professional)\b|\btrusted\s+advisor\b|"
  2586	    r"\bproven\s+track\s+record\b|\bindustry\s+veteran\b",
  2587	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2588	)
  2589	_METADATA_RECITAL_RE = re.compile(
  2590	    r"\bjournal\s+article\b[^.]{0,80}\bvolume\s+\d+\b[^.]{0,60}\b(?:article\s+\d+|authored\s+by)\b"
  2591	    r"|\bvolume\s+\d+\b[^.]{0,30}\bissue\s+\d+\b[^.]{0,30}\bauthored\s+by\b",
  2592	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2593	)
  2594	# Rule 7 helpers: a trailing bare ordinal (a standalone 1-3 digit / dotted section number at the
  2595	# very end, e.g. "3.2" / "5"; a trailing "0.42%" carries a % so it never matches), and the small
  2596	# finite-verb / copula lexicon whose ABSENCE (with the other three guards) marks a nav/topic stub.
  2597	_TRAILING_CITE_STRIP_RE = re.compile(r"(?:\s*\[\d+\])+\s*$")
  2598	_ENDS_WITH_BARE_ORDINAL_RE = re.compile(r"(?:^|\s)\d{1,3}(?:\.\d{1,2})?\s*$")
  2599	_CHROME_STOPWORD_DENSITY_FLOOR = 0.10
  2600	_NAV_ITEM_MAX_WORDS = 6
  2601	_CHROME_STOPWORDS = frozenset({
  2602	    "the", "a", "an", "and", "or", "but", "of", "to", "in", "on", "at", "for", "with", "by",
  2603	    "from", "as", "is", "are", "was", "were", "be", "been", "being", "am", "that", "this",
  2604	    "these", "those", "it", "its", "their", "his", "her", "they", "we", "our", "you", "your",
  2605	    "which", "who", "whom", "whose", "than", "then", "into", "over", "under", "about", "between",
  2606	    "among", "per", "via", "not", "no", "nor", "so", "if", "while", "during", "after", "before",
  2607	    "above", "below", "up", "down", "out", "off", "how", "when", "where", "what", "why", "all",
  2608	    "each", "more", "most", "some", "such", "also", "may", "can", "will", "would", "should",
  2609	    "could", "has", "have", "had", "do", "does", "did", "versus", "vs", "both", "either",
  2610	})
  2611	def _stopword_density(text: str) -> float:
  2612	    """The fraction of ALPHABETIC tokens in ``text`` that are common English stopwords (PURE). A
  2613	    scraped author list / ToC-nav stub has near-zero stopword density; real running prose does not.
  2614	    The precision guard for the risky surname-digit (rule 3b) and short-nav (rule 7) chrome rules."""
  2615	    words = re.findall(r"[A-Za-z]+", text.lower())
  2616	    if not words:
  2617	        return 0.0
  2618	    return sum(1 for w in words if w in _CHROME_STOPWORDS) / len(words)
  2619	
  2620	
  2621	def _is_titlecase_heading(text: str) -> bool:
  2622	    """True iff EVERY content word (>=3 letters and not a stopword) starts uppercase — the Title-Case
  2623	    shape of a scraped ToC / nav / section heading ("Labor Market Trends 3.2"). This REPLACES the old
  2624	    finite-verb-absence heuristic (Codex P1 iter 1: a small verb lexicon mislabels real short claims
  2625	    whose verb is outside it — "doubled", "worsened", "adopted", "differed" — as nav stubs). A real
  2626	    short sentence carries at least one LOWERCASE content word (its verb / object), so it is not
  2627	    Title-Case and is kept. Requires >=2 content words so a one-word label is not a "heading"."""
  2628	    content_words = [
  2629	        w for w in re.findall(r"[A-Za-z]+", text)
  2630	        if len(w) >= 3 and w.lower() not in _CHROME_STOPWORDS
  2631	    ]
  2632	    if len(content_words) < 2:
  2633	        return False
  2634	    return all(w[0].isupper() for w in content_words)
  2635	
  2636	
  2637	def _is_short_nav_topic_item(text: str) -> bool:
  2638	    """Rule 7 (the risky short-nav rule): True iff ``text`` is a scraped ToC / nav / topic-list stub
  2639	    under ALL FOUR guards — <= 6 words AND ends with a bare ordinal AND stopword-density below the
  2640	    floor AND Title-Case heading shape (every content word capitalized). Any one guard failing keeps
  2641	    a real short sentence (precision-first per §-1.3)."""
  2642	    core = _TRAILING_CITE_STRIP_RE.sub("", text.strip()).strip()
  2643	    words = core.split()
  2644	    if not (1 <= len(words) <= _NAV_ITEM_MAX_WORDS):
  2645	        return False
  2646	    if not _ENDS_WITH_BARE_ORDINAL_RE.search(core):
  2647	        return False
  2648	    if _stopword_density(core) >= _CHROME_STOPWORD_DENSITY_FLOOR:
  2649	        return False
  2650	    return _is_titlecase_heading(core)
  2651	
  2652	
  2653	def _contains_p1_box1_chrome(text: str) -> bool:
  2654	    """I-deepfix-001 P1_chrome_gate (#1344): True iff ``text`` CONTAINS one of the seven box1
  2655	    render-seam chrome CLASSES the containment predicate was blind to (paywall/purchase CTA;
  2656	    multilingual license/repository furniture; glued author-stats-table; asterisked-author
  2657	    street+ZIP affiliation; exec/promo bio; stitched metadata-recital citation; short nav/topic-list
  2658	    stub). High-precision / label-anchored; detector-only (FLAG-not-drop); the faithfulness engine
  2659	    is UNCHANGED."""
  2660	    s = text
  2661	    # (1) publisher paywall / purchase CTA
  2662	    if _PAYWALL_CTA_BOX1_RE.search(s):
  2663	        return True
  2664	    # (2) multilingual license / repository furniture
  2665	    if _REPO_LICENSE_FURNITURE_RE.search(s):
  2666	        return True
  2667	    # (3a) Stata summary-table header run
  2668	    if _STATS_SUMMARY_HEADER_RE.search(s):
  2669	        return True
  2670	    # (3b) glued author byline, anchored to author-LIST STRUCTURE (NOT a per-word label allowlist —
  2671	    #      that was open-ended and still over-stripped real TWO-CATEGORY findings like "High School1
  2672	    #      Low College2 earnings differed" / "Blue Collar1 White Collar2 wages diverged", Codex
  2673	    #      blocker). Fire ONLY on >=3 surname-digit pairs, OR exactly 2 pairs PLUS an INDEPENDENT
  2674	    #      author/affiliation co-signal in the SAME unit — all still under the stopword-density guard.
  2675	    #      The co-signal is an affiliation keyword (University|Institute|College|Department) / "et al."
  2676	    #      / email ONLY. The superscript author asterisk is NOT a co-signal (not even ">=2 starred
  2677	    #      pairs"): two starred CATEGORY labels ("High School1* Low College2* earnings differed") are
  2678	    #      byte-identical to a two-author starred byline, so the iter-1 starred-pair heuristic
  2679	    #      over-stripped that real finding (Codex iter-2 P1 blocker). A genuine bare-stars-only byline
  2680	    #      ("Jane Smith1* John Doe2*", no affiliation/email/et-al) is now an ACCEPTED LEAK — leaked
  2681	    #      furniture is far lower harm than deleting a real finding (§-1.3 precision-first).
  2682	    _pairs = _surname_digit_pair_count(s)
  2683	    _cosignal = bool(_AUTHOR_COSIGNAL_RE.search(s))
  2684	    if (
  2685	        (_pairs >= 3 or (_pairs == 2 and _cosignal))
  2686	        and _stopword_density(s) < _CHROME_STOPWORD_DENSITY_FLOOR
  2687	    ):
  2688	        return True
  2689	    # (4) asterisked-author street + ZIP affiliation block. A City,ST ZIP is chrome ONLY with an
  2690	    #     affiliation CO-SIGNAL (a street address or a corresponding-author marker); a bare City,ST
  2691	    #     ZIP in a real finding ("... in Cambridge, MA 02142 ...") is KEPT — Codex P1 iter 1.
  2692	    if _US_CITY_STATE_ZIP_RE.search(s) and (
  2693	        _STREET_ADDRESS_RE.search(s) or _CORRESP_AUTHOR_RE.search(s)
  2694	    ):
  2695	        return True
  2696	    if _CORRESP_AUTHOR_RE.search(s) and _STREET_ADDRESS_RE.search(s):
  2697	        return True
  2698	    # (5) exec / promo bio (dual-signal: job title WELDED to a promo predicate)
  2699	    if _EXEC_TITLE_RE.search(s) and _PROMO_PREDICATE_RE.search(s):
  2700	        return True
  2701	    # (6) stitched metadata-recital citation
  2702	    if _METADATA_RECITAL_RE.search(s):
  2703	        return True
  2704	    # (7) short nav / topic-list stub (four-guarded)
  2705	    return _is_short_nav_topic_item(s)
  2706	
  2707	
  2708	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  2709	# Box C QUALITY fix (workflow wioabua6u) — the render-seam chrome CLASSES the containment
  2710	# predicate above was STILL PROVEN BLIND to on the live Box A/C breadth section. Each rule is
  2711	# high-precision + STRUCTURE-ANCHORED to furniture a real finding never carries (constraint 2,
  2712	# precision-first): an author affiliation-byline / a date WELDED onto a section header, website
  2713	# nav-menu glyph furniture, a file-asset size inventory, a bibliographic recital, an IMF/ToC
  2714	# trailing-page heading, a heading glued to prose, a pipeline repetition marker, and a
  2715	# predominantly non-English (Vietnamese Latin-extended) heading. FLAG-not-drop / detector-only: a
  2716	# flagged UNIT is withheld from the rendered rollup, the SOURCE stays in evidence_pool + its
  2717	# credibility disclosure; the faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role D8 / provenance /
  2718	# span-grounding) is UNCHANGED. Gated by the caller under render_chrome_screen_enabled() (default ON).
  2719	
  2720	# author affiliation-byline furniture (bio line / masthead author block).
  2721	_BOXC_AFFIL_BYLINE_RE = re.compile(
  2722	    r"\bis\s+(?:a\s+)?(?:Non-?Resident\s+)?Senior\s+Fellow\b"
  2723	    r"|\bAuthors?\s+and\s+[Cc]ontributors\b"
  2724	    r"|\bAbout\s+(?:CSIS|Brookings|the\s+Author)\b"
  2725	    r"|\bEDITORS\b[\s\S]{0,80}?\bAUTHORS\b"
  2726	)
  2727	# a calendar date WELDED directly onto a section header word (author-date + "Abstract"/etc.).
  2728	_BOXC_DATE_WELDED_HEADER_RE = re.compile(
  2729	    r"\b\d{1,2}\s+(?:Jan|Feb|Mar|Apr|May|Jun|Jul|Aug|Sep|Oct|Nov|Dec)[a-z]*\s+\d{4}\s+"
  2730	    r"(?:Abstract|Introduction|Conclusion|Executive\s+Summary)\b"
  2731	)
  2732	# website nav-menu furniture -- glyphs / bracketed nav labels a real finding never carries, plus a
  2733	# markdown nav-link run ("](https://...) * [").
  2734	# Correction 6 (Codex+Fable gate): written with EXPLICIT \uXXXX unicode escapes so the SOURCE stays
  2735	# pure-ASCII and no file-encoding / mojibake ambiguity can silently break a glyph class. NON-raw
  2736	# string: \uXXXX expands to the literal char in the compiled pattern; \\ escapes the regex
  2737	# metacharacters. Glyphs: \u2794 = heavy rightwards arrow, \u2261 = triple-bar, \u2718 = ballot-X,
  2738	# \u00fc = u-umlaut, \u00b7 = middle-dot, \u2022 = bullet. Same classes as before.
  2739	_BOXC_NAV_MENU_RE = re.compile(
  2740	    "\u2794"                                             # heavy round-tipped rightwards arrow
  2741	    "|\u2261\\s*Menu"                                    # triple-bar [ws]* Menu
  2742	    "|\u2718"                                             # heavy ballot X
  2743	    "|\\[Zur(?:\u00fc|ue)ck\\]"                          # [Zurueck] with u-umlaut or ue
  2744	    "|\\[Startseite"                                     # [Startseite
  2745	    "|\\]\\(https?://[^)]+\\)\\s*[*\u00b7\u2022]\\s*\\["  # ](url) [ws]* {* mid-dot bullet} [ws]* [
  2746	)
  2747	# file-asset-metadata inventory — >=2 size tokens WELDED to a file-asset noun ("paper PDF of 6 MB",
  2748	# "text file of 213.59 KB", "study brief PDF of 1.08 MB"): a download-widget size inventory.
  2749	# Correction 1 (Codex+Fable gate): the prior ">=2 BARE size tokens" trigger over-dropped real
  2750	# quantitative claims that merely carry two data sizes — "grew from 570 GB in 2020 to 45 TB by 2023
  2751	# [7]" / "Each A100 card provides 80 GB ... consumer cards offer 24 GB [12]". Anchor the token to a
  2752	# preceding FILE-ASSET noun (PDF / file / download / attachment / document / text file / brief) so a
  2753	# bare data-magnitude claim is KEPT and only a file-download size inventory is flagged (precision-
  2754	# first, constraint 2). Still requires >=2 such WELDED matches (one incidental file size is fine).
  2755	_BOXC_FILE_SIZE_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(
  2756	    r"(?:PDF|file|download|attachment|document|text\s+file|brief)"
  2757	    r"\s+(?:of\s+)?\d+(?:\.\d+)?\s?(?:MB|KB|GB|TB)\b",
  2758	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2759	)
  2760	_BOXC_MIN_FILE_SIZE_TOKENS = 2
  2761	# bibliographic-recital-as-prose ("published volume 13, article 569", "with an ISSN date of").
  2762	_BOXC_BIBLIO_RECITAL_RE = re.compile(
  2763	    r"published\s+volume\s+\d+\s*,\s*article\s+\d+"
  2764	    r"|with\s+an\s+ISSN\s+date\s+of",
  2765	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2766	)
  2767	# IMF/ToC trailing-page heading — a Title-Case heading run ending in a bare page number with NO
  2768	# verb. The shape admits ONLY Capitalized words + a small connective allowlist + a trailing 1-3
  2769	# digit page number, so any lowercase content word (a real sentence's verb/object) breaks the match.
  2770	_BOXC_TOC_PAGE_RE = re.compile(
  2771	    r"^(?:(?:[A-Z][\w’'.&/-]*|and|of|the|for|to|in|on|at|a|an|with|from|by|[-–—&])[:,]?\s+)+"
  2772	    r"\d{1,3}$"
  2773	)
  2774	# heading-glued-to-prose — an ALL-CAPS multiword run of 5+ words embedded anywhere, and a leading
  2775	# standalone policy-brief heading token followed by unrelated prose.
  2776	_BOXC_ALLCAPS_RUN_RE = re.compile(r"\b(?:[A-Z][A-Z0-9]*[A-Z]\s+){4,}[A-Z][A-Z0-9]*[A-Z]\b")
  2777	_BOXC_HEADING_OPENER_RE = re.compile(
  2778	    r"^\s*(?:Elevator\s+pitch|Key\s+findings|One[- ]page\s+summary|Executive\s+summary)\b\s+[A-Z]"
  2779	)
  2780	# a pipeline-internal "(also mirrored)" duplicate/repetition annotation (never in a real finding).
  2781	_BOXC_REPETITION_MARKER_RE = re.compile(r"\(also\s+mirrored\)", re.IGNORECASE)
  2782	# predominantly non-English heading in an English-contract run — a run of Vietnamese Latin-extended
  2783	# tone-marked characters (Latin Extended Additional U+1E00–U+1EFF + the Vietnamese-specific
  2784	# precomposed letters Ă/ă/Đ/đ/Ơ/ơ/Ư/ư) a real English finding never carries at this density.
  2785	_BOXC_VIET_DIACRITIC_RE = re.compile(
  2786	    r"[Ḁ-ỿĂăĐđƠơƯư]"
  2787	)
  2788	_BOXC_MIN_VIET_DIACRITIC_CHARS = 3
  2789	# Correction 2 (Codex+Fable gate): any alphabetic (unicode) character, for the DENSITY denominator.
  2790	_BOXC_ALPHA_RE = re.compile(r"[^\W\d_]", re.UNICODE)
  2791	# tone-marked chars must be at least this SHARE of the alphabetic characters for the density leg to
  2792	# fire (a predominantly-Vietnamese heading; an English sentence naming a Vietnamese entity is well
  2793	# below it and is KEPT). ~18% chosen so the leaked full-Vietnamese title (~0.22) drops while the two
  2794	# entity-naming English claims (~0.06-0.07) are preserved.
  2795	_BOXC_VIET_DENSITY = 0.18
  2796	# OR the mostly-UPPERCASE heading shape: uppercase-dominant AND carrying the >=floor tone-mark run.
  2797	_BOXC_UPPER_HEADING_RATIO = 0.6
  2798	
  2799	
  2800	def _is_boxc_toc_trailing_page(text: str) -> bool:
  2801	    """True iff ``text`` is an IMF/ToC trailing-page heading — a multi-word Title-Case heading run
  2802	    ending in a bare 1-3 digit page number with no finite verb. High-precision: the shape admits only
  2803	    Capitalized words + a small connective allowlist, so any lowercase content word keeps a real
  2804	    sentence; requires >=4 tokens and >=2 Capitalized content words so a short "Table 3" stub is out
  2805	    of this rule's lane."""
  2806	    core = _TRAILING_CITE_STRIP_RE.sub("", text.strip()).strip()
  2807	    if not _BOXC_TOC_PAGE_RE.match(core):
  2808	        return False
  2809	    tokens = core.split()
  2810	    if len(tokens) < 4:
  2811	        return False
  2812	    caps = [t for t in tokens[:-1] if t[:1].isupper() and len(re.sub(r"[^A-Za-z]", "", t)) >= 2]
  2813	    return len(caps) >= 2
  2814	
  2815	
  2816	def _is_boxc_non_english(text: str) -> bool:
  2817	    """True iff ``text`` is a predominantly non-English (Vietnamese) heading in an English-contract run
  2818	    (e.g. "CACH MANG CONG NGHIEP 4.0 TAI VIET NAM ...").
  2819	
  2820	    Correction 2 (Codex+Fable gate): the prior ABSOLUTE ``count >= 3`` over-dropped real English claims
  2821	    that merely NAME one or two Vietnamese entities — "Vietnam Ministry of Labour (Bo Lao dong ...)
  2822	    projects 3 million displaced workers by 2030 [9]", "Prime Minister Pham Minh Chinh and Nguyen Thi
  2823	    Hong announced the strategy in 2024 [2]". This uses a DENSITY test instead: the tone-marked chars
  2824	    must be at least ``_BOXC_VIET_DENSITY`` of the ALPHABETIC characters (a SHARE, not an absolute
  2825	    count), OR the text must be the mostly-UPPERCASE heading shape carrying the tone-mark run. A
  2826	    one-or-two-proper-noun English sentence stays below both bars and is KEPT (§-1.3 multilingual
  2827	    preservation); the full-Vietnamese heading crosses either bar and is DROPPED. A small floor
  2828	    (``_BOXC_MIN_VIET_DIACRITIC_CHARS``) still gates out incidental 1-2 accented characters."""
  2829	    diac = len(_BOXC_VIET_DIACRITIC_RE.findall(text))
  2830	    if diac < _BOXC_MIN_VIET_DIACRITIC_CHARS:
  2831	        return False
  2832	    alpha = _BOXC_ALPHA_RE.findall(text)
  2833	    if not alpha:
  2834	        return False
  2835	    # DENSITY leg: tone-marked chars as a SHARE of alphabetic chars.
  2836	    if diac / len(alpha) >= _BOXC_VIET_DENSITY:
  2837	        return True
  2838	    # OR the mostly-UPPERCASE heading shape (uppercase-dominant AND >=floor tone marks, already true).
  2839	    upper = sum(1 for c in alpha if c.isupper())
  2840	    return (upper / len(alpha)) >= _BOXC_UPPER_HEADING_RATIO
  2841	
  2842	
  2843	# Correction 3 (Codex+Fable gate): the affiliation-byline class must flag ONLY a PURE masthead (names +
  2844	# affiliations, no attributed result). A real finding that MENTIONS an author's affiliation in passing —
  2845	# "Landry Signé, who is a Senior Fellow at Brookings, projects that AI will shift 30 percent of tasks
  2846	# [4]." — carries BOTH a bracketed [N] citation AND a finite finding/report verb, so it is KEPT.
  2847	_BOXC_BRACKET_CITE_RE = re.compile(r"\[\d{1,3}\]")
  2848	_BOXC_FINDING_VERB_RE = re.compile(
  2849	    r"\b(?:project(?:s|ed|ing)?|estimat(?:e|es|ed|ing)|forecast(?:s|ed|ing)?|predict(?:s|ed|ing)?|"
  2850	    r"find(?:s)?|found|report(?:s|ed|ing)?|show(?:s|ed|ing|n)?|suggest(?:s|ed|ing)?|"
  2851	    r"indicat(?:e|es|ed|ing)|warn(?:s|ed|ing)?|conclud(?:e|es|ed|ing)|reduc(?:e|es|ed|ing)|"
  2852	    r"increas(?:e|es|ed|ing)|shift(?:s|ed|ing)?|displac(?:e|es|ed|ing)|rais(?:e|es|ed|ing)|"
  2853	    r"grow(?:s|ing)?|grew|reach(?:es|ed|ing)?|account(?:s|ed|ing)?\s+for|will\s+\w+)\b",
  2854	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2855	)
  2856	
  2857	
  2858	def _has_attributed_cited_finding(text: str) -> bool:
  2859	    """True iff ``text`` carries BOTH a bracketed [N] citation AND a finite finding/report verb — a real
  2860	    attributed finding that merely names an author affiliation in passing (KEEP). The pure masthead
  2861	    byline class (names + affiliations, NO [N] citation, NO finding verb) has neither and stays FLAGGED.
  2862	    Precision-first (constraint 2): the guard only ever RELAXES a drop; it never adds one."""
  2863	    return bool(_BOXC_BRACKET_CITE_RE.search(text) and _BOXC_FINDING_VERB_RE.search(text))
  2864	
  2865	
  2866	def _contains_boxc_render_chrome(text: str) -> bool:
  2867	    """Box C QUALITY fix (workflow wioabua6u): True iff ``text`` CONTAINS one of the render-seam
  2868	    chrome CLASSES the containment predicate was still proven blind to on the live Box A/C breadth
  2869	    section (author/date-welded byline · nav-menu glyph furniture · file-asset size inventory ·
  2870	    bibliographic recital · ToC trailing-page heading · heading-glued-to-prose · repetition marker ·
  2871	    predominantly non-English heading). High-precision / structure-anchored; detector-only
  2872	    (FLAG-not-drop); the faithfulness engine is UNCHANGED."""
  2873	    s = text
  2874	    # date-welded section header always flags; the affiliation byline flags ONLY when the unit has NO
  2875	    # surviving attributed cited finding (correction 3 — keep "…Senior Fellow…, projects … [4]").
  2876	    if _BOXC_DATE_WELDED_HEADER_RE.search(s):
  2877	        return True
  2878	    if _BOXC_AFFIL_BYLINE_RE.search(s) and not _has_attributed_cited_finding(s):
  2879	        return True
  2880	    if _BOXC_NAV_MENU_RE.search(s):
  2881	        return True
  2882	    if len(_BOXC_FILE_SIZE_TOKEN_RE.findall(s)) >= _BOXC_MIN_FILE_SIZE_TOKENS:
  2883	        return True
  2884	    if _BOXC_BIBLIO_RECITAL_RE.search(s):
  2885	        return True
  2886	    if _is_boxc_toc_trailing_page(s):
  2887	        return True
  2888	    if _BOXC_ALLCAPS_RUN_RE.search(s) or _BOXC_HEADING_OPENER_RE.search(s):
  2889	        return True
  2890	    if _BOXC_REPETITION_MARKER_RE.search(s):
  2891	        return True
  2892	    return _is_boxc_non_english(s)
  2893

  2895	# I-deepfix-001 (#1344) FF1-CHROME v2: the FOUR NEW page-furniture vocabularies the enumerated
  2896	# containment denylist never enumerated (recurrence of the I-wire-013 blind-predicate class on
  2897	# unlisted surface vocabularies) — service/dead-fetch interstitial · OpenAlex/entity-portal record
  2898	# scaffold · "Name - Honorific" bare byline directory stub · "Publication date:"/bare NN:N masthead.
  2899	# High-precision / structure-anchored / cited-finding-guarded. Detector-only (FLAG-not-drop); the
  2900	# faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI / D8 / provenance / span-grounding) is UNCHANGED.
  2901	# v2 (Codex+Fable build-gate precision fix): the v1 RULE 1 used an UNANCHORED `_SERVICE_OFFLINE_RE.search`
  2902	# whose narrow `_has_attributed_cited_finding` guard (needs a [N] citation AND a finding VERB — the
  2903	# copula "is" is not one) could NOT rescue a substantive cited finding that merely CONTAINS an outage
  2904	# phrase, so real claims like "Public employment service is unavailable in 37 percent of rural districts
  2905	# [7]." were over-dropped (the P1). v2 WHOLE-UNIT anchors RULE 1 (^…$ over the cite-stripped core) and
  2906	# adds the same KEEP guard to RULE 4 (the P2 bare-NN:N collision), so a real cited finding is NEVER
  2907	# dropped — precision-first per the operator-locked drop-path law (§-1.3).
  2908	_SERVICE_OFFLINE_RE = re.compile(
  2909	    r"^(?:this\s+)?(?:journal|site|website|server|service|page|content|portal|database|repository|domain)"
  2910	    r"\s+is\s+(?:currently\s+|temporarily\s+)?(?:offline|unavailable|down|under\s+maintenance|not\s+available)\s*[.!?]*$"
  2911	    r"|^service\s+(?:temporarily\s+)?unavailable\s*[.!?]*$"
  2912	    r"|^this\s+site\s+can[’']?t\s+be\s+reached\s*[.!?]*$",
  2913	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2914	)
  2915	_PORTAL_RECORD_SCAFFOLD_RE = re.compile(
  2916	    r"DetailsLocations"
  2917	    r"|Year\s*:\s*(?:19|20)\d{2}\s+Type\s*:\s*\w+\s+Abstract\s*:"
  2918	    r"|Type\s*:\s*article\s+Abstract\s*:"
  2919	    r"|Cited\s+by\s+\d+\s+Related\s+works",
  2920	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2921	)
  2922	_BYLINE_HONORIFIC_RE = re.compile(
  2923	    r"^[A-Z][A-Za-z.'’-]+(?:\s+[A-Z][A-Za-z.'’-]+){0,3}\s+[-–—]\s+"
  2924	    r"(?:Mr|Mrs|Ms|Mx|Miss|Dr|Prof|Professor|Sir|Dame|Rev)\.?$"
  2925	)
  2926	_PUB_DATE_MASTHEAD_RE = re.compile(
  2927	    r"(?<!the\s)\bPublication\s+date\b\s*:?\s*"
  2928	    r"(?:(?:19|20)\d{2}|(?:Jan|Feb|Mar|Apr|May|Jun|Jul|Aug|Sep|Oct|Nov|Dec)[a-z]*\s+(?:19|20)\d{2})",
  2929	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2930	)
  2931	_MASTHEAD_COSIGNAL_RE = re.compile(
  2932	    r"(?<!\d)\d{1,3}\s*:\s*\d{1,3}(?!\d)|Document Version|Published in|\bDOI\s*10\.|\bISSN[a-z]?\b",
  2933	    re.IGNORECASE,
  2934	)
  2935	
  2936	
  2937	def _contains_portal_masthead_status_chrome(text: str) -> bool:
  2938	    """True iff ``text`` is one of the four NEW page-furniture vocabularies (FF1-CHROME) the
  2939	    enumerated containment denylist never enumerated: (1) a service/dead-fetch interstitial
  2940	    ("This journal is currently offline.") — WHOLE-UNIT anchored AND cited-finding-guarded; (2) an
  2941	    OpenAlex/entity-portal record scaffold ("…DetailsLocations Year: NNNN Type: article Abstract: …");
  2942	    (3) a bare "Name - Honorific" byline/directory stub; (4) a "Publication date: <Month YYYY>"
  2943	    masthead paired with a bare "NN:N" volume:issue (or DOI/ISSN/Document-Version) co-signal AND
  2944	    cited-finding-guarded. High-precision / structure-anchored — detector-only (FLAG-not-drop); it
  2945	    never strips a substantive finding. Precision-first per the operator-locked drop-path law (§-1.3).
  2946	    Reuses ``_TRAILING_CITE_STRIP_RE`` and the ``_has_attributed_cited_finding`` KEEP guard so a real
  2947	    cited finding is never dropped."""
  2948	    s = text
  2949	    # The cite-stripped, whitespace-trimmed unit — the whole-unit anchor surface for RULEs 1 and 3.
  2950	    core = _TRAILING_CITE_STRIP_RE.sub("", text.strip()).strip()
  2951	    # RULE 1 — service/dead-fetch interstitial. WHOLE-UNIT anchored (Codex+Fable P1 over-strip fix): the
  2952	    # interstitial must BE the entire unit (after stripping a trailing [N] + terminal punctuation), so a
  2953	    # substantive cited finding that merely CONTAINS an outage phrase ("Public employment service is
  2954	    # unavailable in 37 percent of rural districts [7].") is NEVER dropped. The narrow
  2955	    # `_has_attributed_cited_finding` guard is kept as a second KEEP layer (it only ever relaxes a drop).
  2956	    if _SERVICE_OFFLINE_RE.search(core) and not _has_attributed_cited_finding(s):
  2957	        return True
  2958	    # RULE 2 — OpenAlex/entity-portal record scaffold (glued UI-button token / Year:/Type:/Abstract:
  2959	    # field-ladder); no guard needed (no author writes these text-extraction artifacts).
  2960	    if _PORTAL_RECORD_SCAFFOLD_RE.search(s):
  2961	        return True
  2962	    # RULE 3 — bare "Name - Honorific" byline/directory stub; whole-unit ^…$ anchored with the
  2963	    # honorific as the TERMINAL token (keeps "Ms. Parikh testified that … [9]").
  2964	    if _BYLINE_HONORIFIC_RE.match(core):
  2965	        return True
  2966	    # RULE 4 — masthead "Publication date: <Month YYYY>" + a bare volume:issue / DOI / ISSN /
  2967	    # Document-Version co-signal (dual-signal). The (?<!the\s) lookbehind + required co-signal + the
  2968	    # `_has_attributed_cited_finding` KEEP guard (Codex+Fable P2 fix) keep a real cited claim that
  2969	    # recites a publication date ("Publication date: March 2021 the study found a 2:1 response ratio [5].").
  2970	    if (
  2971	        _PUB_DATE_MASTHEAD_RE.search(s)
  2972	        and _MASTHEAD_COSIGNAL_RE.search(s)
  2973	        and not _has_attributed_cited_finding(s)
  2974	    ):
  2975	        return True
  2976	    return False
  2977	
  2978	
  2979	def _contains_forensic_chrome(text: str) -> bool:
  2980	    """True iff ``text`` CONTAINS page-furniture chrome (not only IS chrome). The CONTAINMENT
  2981	    unblinding ported from scripts/iwire013_sec11_forensic_audit.py, tightened for this drop path
  2982	    (see the module comment above). High-precision / structure-anchored; never flags a clean
  2983	    finding. Gated by the caller under ``render_chrome_screen_enabled()``."""
  2984	    s = text
  2985	    low = s.lower()
  2986	    # browser/UI · license · author/submission metadata · bibliographic/portal · masthead
  2987	    if _NAV_CHROME_RE.search(s) or _LICENSE_CHROME_RE.search(s) or _BIBLIO_CHROME_RE.search(s):
  2988	        return True
  2989	    # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-A: ISSNe/ISSNp-aware, over-fire-safe ISSN masthead recital
  2990	    # (default-ON co-signal gate; OFF => byte-identical legacy bare ISSN).
  2991	    if _is_issn_masthead_chrome(s):
  2992	        return True
  2993	    # I-deepfix-002 (#1363) FIX-1: cookie/consent banner · DOI-registry error page · foreign masthead
  2994	    if _COOKIE_CONSENT_RE.search(s) or _DOI_ERROR_RE.search(s) or _is_foreign_journal_masthead(s):
  2995	        return True
  2996	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1344) DEFER-4: residual furniture-dominated units — publisher paywall CTA ·
  2997	    # working-paper cover masthead/disclaimer · PDF footnote/citation-apparatus run.
  2998	    if _is_residual_chrome_furniture(s):
  2999	        return True
  3000	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1344) chrome_canary_unblind: author-affiliation/email byline · ToC dot-leaders ·
  3001	    # "By clicking … you accept" consent banner (the three classes the canary was blind to).
  3002	    if _contains_missed_chrome_class(s):
  3003	        return True
  3004	    if _SUBMISSION_META_RE.search(s) or _MASTHEAD_CHROME_RE.search(s) or _STATS_TABLE_RE.search(s):
  3005	        return True
  3006	    if _ORCID_RE.search(s) or "orcid" in low or _AFFIL_MIDDOT_RE.search(s):
  3007	        return True
  3008	    if len(_URL_RE.findall(s)) >= _MIN_URLS_FOR_CHROME:
  3009	        return True
  3010	    if len(_DOI_URL_RE.findall(s)) >= _MIN_DOI_URLS_FOR_CHROME:
  3011	        return True
  3012	    # glued markdown header / ToC fragment
  3013	    if _INLINE_HEADER_RE.search(s) or _dotted_toc_hits(s) >= _MIN_DOTTED_TOC_HITS:
  3014	        return True
  3015	    if _STANDALONE_SECTION_NAME_RE.search(s):
  3016	        return True
  3017	    standalone_dotted = _STANDALONE_DOTTED_HEADING_RE.match(s)
  3018	    if standalone_dotted and standalone_dotted.group(1).lower() not in _MAGNITUDE_UNIT_WORDS:
  3019	        return True
  3020	    # I-wire-016 #1338 gap-fill (affiliation-glued / title+affiliation / author-attribution-phrase) —
  3021	    # the precision-safe masthead classes that leaked past the legacy categories.
  3022	    if _contains_iwire016_gap_furniture(s):
  3023	        return True
  3024	    # I-deepfix-001 #1344 drb72_apparatus_unblind: citation-counter/citedby-path API blob ·
  3025	    # SSRN/working-paper version-header cover · CAPTION/AXIS-ONLY figure apparatus (the classes that
  3026	    # leaked into cited claims + the Abstract/Conclusion sandwich; figure rule tightened per Codex P1).
  3027	    if _contains_drb72_apparatus_chrome(s):
  3028	        return True
  3029	    # A1+A2 (I-wire Wave-A): title-page/monograph masthead · author-block→Abstract byline ·
  3030	    # bibliography-fragment locator · pure table/figure caption stub (the classes the drb_72 audit
  3031	    # found the containment predicate STILL blind to). High-precision / fail-open on real prose.
  3032	    if _contains_missed_titlepage_biblio_caption(s):
  3033	        return True
  3034	    # I-deepfix-001 P1_chrome_gate (#1344): the SEVEN box1 render-seam chrome classes the containment
  3035	    # predicate was proven blind to (paywall/purchase CTA · multilingual license/repository furniture ·
  3036	    # glued author-stats-table · asterisked-author street+ZIP affiliation · exec/promo bio · stitched
  3037	    # metadata-recital citation · short nav/topic-list stub). High-precision / label-anchored.
  3038	    if _contains_p1_box1_chrome(s):
  3039	        return True
  3040	    # Box C QUALITY fix (workflow wioabua6u): the render-seam chrome classes proven STILL blind on
  3041	    # the live Box A/C breadth section — author/date-welded byline · nav-menu glyphs · file-asset
  3042	    # size inventory · bibliographic recital · ToC trailing-page heading · heading-glued-to-prose ·
  3043	    # repetition marker · predominantly non-English (Vietnamese) heading. High-precision / anchored.
  3044	    if _contains_boxc_render_chrome(s):
  3045	        return True
  3046	    # I-deepfix-001 #1344 FF1-CHROME v2: the four NEW furniture vocabularies the enumerated denylist
  3047	    # never enumerated — service/dead-fetch interstitial · OpenAlex/entity-portal record scaffold ·
  3048	    # "Name - Honorific" bare byline stub · "Publication date:"/bare NN:N masthead. WHOLE-UNIT anchored /
  3049	    # cited-finding-guarded (precision-first §-1.3); detector-only (FLAG-not-drop).
  3050	    if _contains_portal_masthead_status_chrome(s):
  3051	        return True
  3052	    # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-B: figure alt-text axis enumeration ("The chart has 1 X axis … Y axis …").
  3053	    if chart_alt_chrome_gate_enabled() and _CHART_ALT_TEXT_RE.search(s):
  3054	        global _CHART_ALT_ACTIVATION_LOGGED
  3055	        if not _CHART_ALT_ACTIVATION_LOGGED:
  3056	            _CHART_ALT_ACTIVATION_LOGGED = True
  3057	            logger.info("[activation] chart_alt_chrome: fired=1 (chart-alt-text gate ON)")
  3058	        return True
  3059	    # foreign-page scrape (predominantly non-Latin)
  3060	    return _is_predominantly_nonlatin(s)

  3063	def render_chrome_screen_enabled() -> bool:
  3064	    """Default ON (LAW VI kill-switch ``PG_RENDER_CHROME_SCREEN=0``). When OFF, the NEW
  3065	    I-wire-012 chrome categories are skipped and the predicate is byte-identical to the
  3066	    legacy base junk screen (boilerplate + sentence-form web-chrome + CAPTCHA)."""
  3067	    return os.environ.get(_RENDER_CHROME_SCREEN_ENV, "1").strip().lower() in (
  3068	        "1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled",
  3069	    )

  3072	def _base_junk(text: str) -> bool:
  3073	    """The PRE-I-wire-012 junk screen, byte-equivalent to the old ``_make_junk_screen``
  3074	    closure: production boilerplate OR sentence-form web-chrome OR CAPTCHA stub OR a
  3075	    unit that reduces to "" under ``strip_web_boilerplate``. Import-safe (access_bypass
  3076	    import failure falls back to the chrome + CAPTCHA screens, never fail-open to nothing)."""
  3077	    try:
  3078	        from src.tools.access_bypass import (  # noqa: PLC0415
  3079	            is_boilerplate_or_nonassertional as _boiler,
  3080	            strip_web_boilerplate as _strip_boiler,
  3081	        )
  3082	    except Exception:  # pragma: no cover - access_bypass import is stable in-tree
  3083	        return _is_web_chrome(text) or _is_captcha_stub(text)
  3084	    try:
  3085	        if bool(_boiler(text)) or _is_web_chrome(text) or _is_captcha_stub(text):
  3086	            return True
  3087	        return not (_strip_boiler(text) or "").strip()
  3088	    except Exception:  # pragma: no cover - boiler helpers are pure in-tree
  3089	        return _is_web_chrome(text) or _is_captcha_stub(text)

  3092	# I-deepfix-001 (#1369) FIX 4 — chrome TYPES the existing screens structurally cannot match (Fable,
  3093	# code-verified on box-2 report): (a) GENERATED document-navigation NARRATION ("...on page 46, presents
  3094	# Figure 4.1 on page 61, includes Figure 6.1 as a schematic") — span-grounded so strict_verify passes it,
  3095	# but it is document-structure furniture, not a research finding; (b) an author MASTHEAD carrying NO
  3096	# ORCID/ISSN (so _ORCID_RE + the ISSN masthead rule both miss it: "Alexandra Shajek 1. Institut für ...,
  3097	# GmbH, Berlin, Germany 2."). Default-ON kill-switch PG_RENDER_CHROME_NARRATION. Precision-first: the
  3098	# narration rule needs >=2 distinct structure references so a real claim mentioning ONE figure is safe.
  3099	_STRUCTURE_REF_RE = re.compile(
  3100	    r"\b(?:on\s+)?page\s+\d+\b|\bFig(?:ure|\.)?\s*\d+(?:\.\d+)?\b|\bTable\s+\d+(?:\.\d+)?\b"
  3101	    r"|\bas\s+a\s+schematic\b|\bchapter\s+\d+\b|\bsection\s+\d+(?:\.\d+)?\b",
  3102	    re.I,
  3103	)
  3104	_MASTHEAD_NO_ORCID_RE = re.compile(
  3105	    r"\b\d\s*\.?\s*(?:Institut|Institute|Universit|GmbH|Department|Laborator|Faculty|Ministry|Centre|Center)\b"
  3106	    r".{0,90}?\b(?:Germany|Deutschland|USA|United\s+States|France|Italy|Spain|Netherlands|Austria|"
  3107	    r"Switzerland|Sweden|Norway|Denmark|Finland|Belgium|Poland|Portugal|Greece|China|Japan|Korea|India|"
  3108	    r"Canada|Australia|Kingdom)\b",
  3109	    re.I,
  3110	)

  3113	def _render_chrome_narration_enabled() -> bool:
  3114	    """Kill-switch ``PG_RENDER_CHROME_NARRATION`` (default ON). Only an explicit 0/false/off/no
  3115	    disables; an EMPTY string stays ON."""
  3116	    return os.environ.get("PG_RENDER_CHROME_NARRATION", "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
