  3119	# I-deepfix-001 (#1369) iter2/iter3 (Codex + Fable P1, WEIGHT-NOT-FILTER / no-drop): a REAL finding that
  3120	# merely cites figure/table LOCATIONS is NOT chrome. TWO keep-signals, both computed on the residual after
  3121	# stripping the structure references, so "Figure 4.1"'s "4.1" / "page 61"'s "61" never read as findings:
  3122	#   (a) a finding metric survives — a %, "percent/pp", a decimal, OR a plain/comma integer of >=2 digits
  3123	#       ("job losses of 1,200 and 900 workers"); OR
  3124	#   (b) SUBSTANTIVE content dominates — the structure references are a MINORITY of the text (< 45% of chars),
  3125	#       so a qualitative finding ("Table 2 and Table 3 show automation displaces routine work") is KEPT.
  3126	# Only text that is BOTH metric-free AND dominated by document-navigation refs ("...page 46, presents
  3127	# Figure 4.1 on page 61, includes Figure 6.1 as a schematic") is flagged as chrome. Err toward KEEP (§-1.3).
  3128	_FINDING_METRIC_RE = re.compile(
  3129	    r"\d+(?:\.\d+)?\s*%|\bpercent(?:age\s+points?)?\b|\bpp\b|\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})+|\d+\.\d+|\b\d{2,}\b"
  3130	)
  3131	# Document-DESCRIPTION verb that DIRECTLY GOVERNS a structure noun — the writer narrating a document's own
  3132	# apparatus ("presents Figure 4.1", "includes Figure 6.1", "reproduces Table 2 as a schematic"). Codex iter-3
  3133	# P1: the verb ALONE is not enough — "present/illustrate/depict/include" are REAL finding verbs when they
  3134	# govern CONTENT ("present evidence that automation displaces work", "illustrate that ...", "depict a shift").
  3135	# So we require the description verb to be IMMEDIATELY followed by a structure noun (Figure/Table/Chart/...),
  3136	# OR the standalone "as a schematic" tail. This catches the box-2 navigation chrome without touching a real
  3137	# qualitative finding that merely uses "present/illustrate/depict".
  3138	# STRONG navigation signal: a description verb DIRECTLY governing a structure noun ("presents Figure 4.1").
  3139	# Each occurrence counts fully toward the narration chain.
  3140	_NAV_VERB_STRUCTURE_RE = re.compile(
  3141	    r"\b(?:outlines?|presents?|depicts?|illustrates?|includes?|reproduces?|shows?|contains?|summariz\w+)\s+"
  3142	    r"(?:the\s+|a\s+|an\s+)?(?:Fig(?:ure|\.)?|Table|Chart|Schematic|Diagram|Panel|Exhibit|Appendix|Chapter)\b",
  3143	    re.I,
  3144	)
  3145	# WEAK navigation signal: a bare "see Figure/Table/page" locator or an "as a schematic" tail. Codex iter-4 +
  3146	# Fable iter-5 P1 (no-drop): a REAL finding routinely carries such parentheticals — "(see Table 2) and
  3147	# manufacturing (see Figure 3)". So ALL of these together count AT MOST ONCE toward the chain.
  3148	_NAV_LOCATOR_RE = re.compile(
  3149	    r"\bas\s+a\s+schematic\b|\bsee\s+(?:figure|table|page)\b",
  3150	    re.I,
  3151	)
  3152	
  3153	
  3154	def _is_generated_narration_or_masthead(text: str) -> bool:
  3155	    """True iff ``text`` is generated document-navigation narration or an ORCID/ISSN-less author-
  3156	    affiliation masthead. NARRATION = >=2 structure refs AND no finding metric AND (a document-DESCRIPTION
  3157	    verb like outlines/presents/includes OR the structure refs DOMINATE the text). Weight-not-filter /
  3158	    no-drop (Codex+Fable P1): a real finding citing a table/figure location — quantitative ('3.2% ... Table 4
  3159	    on page 12.', 'job losses of 1,200 and 900 workers') OR qualitative ('Table 2 and Table 3 show automation
  3160	    displaces routine work') — is CONTENT and is NEVER dropped (it has a metric, or an outcome verb rather
  3161	    than a description verb, or low structure-share). PURE."""
  3162	    # Masthead: an affiliation block carrying a finding metric is a numbered-list FINDING, not a masthead.
  3163	    if _MASTHEAD_NO_ORCID_RE.search(text) and not _FINDING_METRIC_RE.search(text):
  3164	        return True
  3165	    refs = _STRUCTURE_REF_RE.findall(text)
  3166	    if len(refs) >= 2:
  3167	        residual = _STRUCTURE_REF_RE.sub(" ", text)
  3168	        if _FINDING_METRIC_RE.search(residual):
  3169	            return False  # a real finding metric survives the structure refs -> content, keep it
  3170	        ref_chars = sum(len(m) for m in refs)
  3171	        structure_dominates = ref_chars / (len(text.strip()) or 1) >= 0.45
  3172	        # Codex iter-3/4 + Fable iter-5 P1 (no-drop): pure document narration walks the reader through
  3173	        # MULTIPLE exhibits ("presents Figure 4.1 ... includes Figure 6.1 as a schematic"); a REAL finding
  3174	        # cites locations in passing ("...(see Table 2) and manufacturing (see Figure 3)", "present evidence
  3175	        # that ..."). So the chain = (every strong description-verb-governs-structure phrase) + (all the weak
  3176	        # bare "see X"/"as a schematic" locators counted AT MOST ONCE combined). Flag only when the chain
  3177	        # reaches 2 OR the structure refs outright dominate. A real finding never chains 2+ STRONG nav clauses.
  3178	        nav_chain = len(_NAV_VERB_STRUCTURE_RE.findall(text)) + min(1, len(_NAV_LOCATOR_RE.findall(text)))
  3179	        if nav_chain >= 2 or structure_dominates:
  3180	            return True   # metric-free + (multi-clause document-navigation OR structure-dominated) -> chrome
  3181	        return False      # metric-free finding with <=1 locator phrase and low structure-share -> keep it
  3182	    return False
  3183	
  3184	
  3185	def _is_new_chrome_category(text: str) -> bool:
  3186	    """The NEW I-wire-012 chrome categories (default-ON, high-precision) PLUS the I-wire-013 (#1327)
  3187	    CONTAINMENT forensic rules (a unit that CONTAINS glued page-furniture, not only IS junk)."""
  3188	    if _SHARED_RENDER_CHROME_RE.search(text):
  3189	        return True
  3190	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1369) FIX 4: generated page/figure narration + ORCID-less masthead (default-ON).
  3191	    if _render_chrome_narration_enabled() and _is_generated_narration_or_masthead(text):
  3192	        return True
  3193	    if _SHARED_CLAIM_HEADER_CHROME_RE.search(text):
  3194	        return True
  3195	    if _SHARED_TOC_RE.search(text):
  3196	        return True
  3197	    if _ORCID_RE.search(text):
  3198	        return True
  3199	    stripped = text.strip()
  3200	    if _DOC_LABEL_RE.match(stripped):
  3201	        return True
  3202	    if _DOI_ONLY_RE.match(stripped):
  3203	        return True
  3204	    # I-wire-014 (#1334): the benchmarked whole-unit-collapse furniture screen — a unit DOMINATED
  3205	    # by page furniture (journal metrics/cite/permissions/JEL/Associated-Records/member-only/
  3206	    # feature-story/cookie-geo/back-matter label runs) with no real clause surviving. Whole-unit
  3207	    # decision only (never an inline partial strip), so a real claim with a welded fragment is
  3208	    # preserved (validated content_preserved_rate = 1.0 on chrome_gold_augmented).
  3209	    try:
  3210	        from src.polaris_graph.generator.chrome_furniture_screen import (  # noqa: PLC0415
  3211	            is_furniture_dominant,
  3212	        )
  3213	        if is_furniture_dominant(text):
  3214	            return True
  3215	    except Exception:  # pragma: no cover - chrome_furniture_screen is stable in-tree
  3216	        pass
  3217	    # I-wire-013 (#1327): CONTAINMENT unblinding — glued ToC / masthead / author / license /
  3218	    # bibliographic / nav / stats-table / foreign-scrape welded into otherwise-real prose.
  3219	    return _contains_forensic_chrome(text)
  3220	
  3221	
  3222	def _is_unrenderable_sentence_form(text: str) -> bool:
  3223	    """``require_sentence_form`` extras for a unit that MUST be a standalone complete
  3224	    claim (a bullet / a lifted body sentence): a mid-word START cut (a lowercase opener
  3225	    is a span sliced mid-token — a real body sentence opens capital/quote/digit) or an
  3226	    INCOMPLETE sentence (no sentence-terminal punctuation after stripping a trailing
  3227	    ``[N]`` marker). NOT applied to verified-compose / enrichment clauses (which a
  3228	    composer may legitimately lowercase / leave mid-clause) — only to bullet/header
  3229	    surfaces, so a lowercased verbatim clause is never over-dropped."""
  3230	    core = text.strip()
  3231	    if not core:
  3232	        return True
  3233	    first = core[:1]
  3234	    if first.islower():
  3235	        return True
  3236	    no_cite = _SHARED_TRAILING_CITE_RE.sub("", core).rstrip()
  3237	    if no_cite and no_cite[-1] not in ".!?\"')]":
  3238	        return True
  3239	    return False
  3240	
  3241	
  3242	# I-deepfix-001 P0 (box2 chrome infestation): furniture-chrome vocabulary the I-wire-013 containment
  3243	# port never enumerated (BLS wage-in-table, PDF object dict, tel:/mailto, >=2 inline md-links, scraped
  3244	# masthead byline). SUPPRESS-ONLY, faithfulness-neutral. Kill-switch PG_SOURCE_FURNITURE_CHROME (default ON).
  3245	_FURN_WAGE_RE = re.compile(r"\$\s?[\d,]+(?:\.\d+)?\s*(?:per\s+(?:year|hour)|/\s*(?:year|hour|hr))", re.IGNORECASE)
  3246	_FURN_PDF_OBJ_RE = re.compile(r"(?:%PDF|\bendobj\b|\bendstream\b|\bxref\b|/ID\s*\[<|\bIndex\[\d+\s+\d+\]|\b\d+\s+\d+\s+obj\b|/(?:Root|Prev|Length|BBox)\b)")
  3247	_FURN_CONTACT_RE = re.compile(r"\b(?:tel:|mailto:)\S", re.IGNORECASE)
  3248	_FURN_MDLINK_RE = re.compile(r"\]\(\s*https?://")
  3249	_FURN_TBWIDGET_RE = re.compile(r"#TB_inline|&inlineId=|&width=\d+", re.IGNORECASE)
  3250	# Codex P1: the author-byline rule was DROPPED — "[David Autor](url) is a professor at MIT who finds that
  3251	# one more robot ... reduces wages by 0.42%" matched it and suppressed a REAL finding. Box2's actual masthead
  3252	# byline chrome is always glued to a wage table (caught by _FURN_WAGE_RE) so no coverage is lost. Over-drop-safe.
  3253	
  3254	# I-deepfix-001 wave-2 (#1370): the furniture-chrome vocabulary the box2 §-1.1 line-by-line read exposed the
  3255	# wave-1 set still missed — a dashboard chart-legend dump (a RUN of >=3 bare "+NN%" tokens, no sentence
  3256	# structure), a bare international CONTACT phone number, a nav CTA ("view details" / "Learn more about the"),
  3257	# a document-TITLE recital ("The document is titled ..."), and CC-license / publisher boilerplate. SUPPRESS-ONLY,
  3258	# faithfulness-neutral. Each pattern was verified NON-matching against the box2 MUST-KEEP real findings (the
  3259	# Acemoglu robot -0.42% wage stat, the Eloundou 1.8% exposure stat, the GDP 1.5%/3%/3.7% projection, the SMEs
  3260	# 83% stat, the Accenture 26.08% stat) — a genuine finding's percents are ALWAYS separated by prose words, so
  3261	# the consecutive-"%"-run signature never fires on them (over-drop-safe, the Codex-P1 byline lesson applied).
  3262	_FURN_CHARTDUMP_RE = re.compile(r"(?:[+\-]?\d+(?:\.\d+)?\s?%\s+){2,}[+\-]?\d+(?:\.\d+)?\s?%")
  3263	_FURN_PHONE_RE = re.compile(r"\+\d{1,3}[\s\-]\d{2,4}[\s\-]\d{2,4}(?:[\s\-]\d{2,4})?")
  3264	# Fable gate (wave-2): "learn more about the" / "read more" substring-match REAL synthesis prose
  3265	# ("workers learn more about the mechanism of task substitution") — DROPPED (byline-trap). Only the
  3266	# unambiguous nav CTAs remain; neither ever appears inside a genuine finding.
  3267	_FURN_NAVCTA_RE = re.compile(r"\bview details\b|\bclick here\b", re.IGNORECASE)
  3268	# Fable gate (wave-2): the bare "is titled" leg substring-matched a REAL cited finding ("the study,
  3269	# which is titled 'Generative AI at Work,' found +14%"). Tightened to the RECITAL form only — a doc-noun
  3270	# IMMEDIATELY followed by "(is )titled" ("The document is titled …", "A work titled …") — so a mid-prose
  3271	# ", which is titled" (comma breaks the doc-noun adjacency) is never matched. Over-drop-safe.
  3272	_FURN_DOCTITLE_RE = re.compile(
  3273	    r"\b(?:a|an|the)\s+(?:document|work|study|report|book|guide|paper|article|publication|chapter)\s+(?:is\s+)?titled\b",
  3274	    re.IGNORECASE,
  3275	)
  3276	_FURN_PUBLISHER_RE = re.compile(
  3277	    r"books in this series are published|some rights are reserved|users can reuse,\s*share,?\s*adapt|authors alliance",
  3278	    re.IGNORECASE,
  3279	)
  3280	
  3281	# I-deepfix-001 F2 (#1371, box2 §-1.1 line-by-line): the furniture-chrome FORM classes the wave-1/2
  3282	# vocabulary still missed — grant/acknowledgment back-matter, a cookie-consent notice, media-player
  3283	# reader furniture, a paywall unlock-code token, a Crossref citation-count widget, the US-gov site
  3284	# banner, and the "Split View" reader control.
  3285	#
  3286	# Codex F2 gate iter-1 (HC-2): these 7 legs are consulted ONLY by the F2 body/ledger PLACEMENT path
  3287	# (``_contains_f2_placement_furniture`` below) — they are deliberately NOT added to the shared
  3288	# ``_contains_source_furniture_chrome`` / ``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` predicate, because that
  3289	# shared predicate ALSO feeds pre-existing DROP seams OUTSIDE this fix (retrieval fetch-furniture
  3290	# screen, verified_compose sentence screen, key_findings, run_honest_sweep). Keeping the F2 vocab out
  3291	# of the shared predicate leaves those drop seams BYTE-IDENTICAL, so no new vocabulary can WIDEN a drop
  3292	# of a real source. §-1.3: a match here can only MOVE a unit below the appendix boundary into the
  3293	# labelled ledger (PLACEMENT), never a drop / cap / thin. SUPPRESS-nothing, faithfulness-neutral.
  3294	#
  3295	# The four broad legs are narrowed (Codex F2 iter-1 P1) to the unambiguous furniture FORM so they never
  3296	# route a genuine topical finding — even for placement — in a media/streaming/HCI, grants/bibliometrics,
  3297	# privacy/cookies, or product-UI report:
  3298	#   • media-player: the specific reader control "playback rate" ONLY (the broad "live stream" is dropped
  3299	#     — a plausible real finding in media economics / streaming commerce);
  3300	#   • grant back-matter: "under Grant <digit>" (an acknowledgment number, not prose) OR the byline form
  3301	#     "Corresponding author:" WITH a colon (a masthead field, not "corresponding authorship" prose);
  3302	#   • cookie-consent: the "cookie" noun co-occurring with a consent-notice signature ("cookie called …"
  3303	#     or "does not store any identifiable data") — the broad bare "duration" context is dropped;
  3304	#   • "Split View": only when glued to a section label by a "-"/":" separator (the scrape form), never a
  3305	#     sentence-initial product-feature mention.
  3306	# Verified NON-matching against the box2 MUST-KEEP real findings (the robot -0.42% wage stat, the
  3307	# Eloundou 1.8%->46% exposure stat, the 5,172-agent Brynjolfsson design sentence, the 0.5-0.9pp GDP
  3308	# productivity projection, the Frey-Osborne 702-occupation methodology).
  3309	_FURN_GRANT_RE = re.compile(r"\bunder\s+Grant\s+\d|\bCorresponding\s+author\s*:", re.IGNORECASE)
  3310	# Cookie-consent fires ONLY when the "cookie" noun co-occurs with a consent-notice signature token —
  3311	# never on a bare mention, and never on generic "duration" prose — so a substantive cookie/privacy
  3312	# finding (e.g. "third-party cookies persist for a long duration enabling tracking") is never furniture.
  3313	_FURN_COOKIE_RE = re.compile(r"\bcookies?\b", re.IGNORECASE)
  3314	_FURN_COOKIE_CTX_RE = re.compile(r"does not store any identifiable data|\bcookie\s+called\b", re.IGNORECASE)
  3315	_FURN_MEDIAPLAYER_RE = re.compile(r"\bplayback rate\b", re.IGNORECASE)
  3316	_FURN_PAYWALL_RE = re.compile(r"\bunlocked article code\b", re.IGNORECASE)
  3317	_FURN_CROSSREF_RE = re.compile(r"\bCrossref\s+\d")
  3318	_FURN_GOVSITE_RE = re.compile(r"An official website of the United States government", re.IGNORECASE)
  3319	# "Split View" is a title-cased reader-pane control that scrapes glued to a section label ("Design: -
  3320	# Split View"). Require the label-glue separator ("-"/":") so a sentence-initial product-feature mention
  3321	# ("Split View lets users …") is never matched.
  3322	_FURN_SPLITVIEW_RE = re.compile(r"[:\-]\s*Split View\b")
  3323	# Codex gate (wave-2) P1: a unit carrying a genuine finding SIGNAL — a decimal, a percentage, or a
  3324	# finding VERB — must NEVER be dropped by the SOFT furniture legs (doc-title recital, >=2 md-links),
  3325	# because a real finding legitimately mentions a title ("A study titled X FOUND +14%") or carries a
  3326	# linked author + linked paper. Only a pure recital / link-farm with NO finding is chrome. The HARD
  3327	# legs (PDF-object dict, chart-legend dump, publisher boilerplate, contact-phone) are unambiguous and
  3328	# fire regardless. Over-drop-safe (verified vs the box2 MUST-KEEP findings + the Codex adversarial cases).
  3329	_FINDING_SIGNAL_RE = re.compile(
  3330	    r"\d\.\d|\b\d+(?:\.\d+)?\s?%|\b(?:found|finds|estimat\w+|report\w+|show\w+|showed|conclud\w+|"
  3331	    r"observ\w+|demonstrat\w+|reveal\w+|reduc\w+|increas\w+|associated with|correlat\w+|"
  3332	    r"percentage points?)\b",
  3333	    re.IGNORECASE,
  3334	)
  3335	# Codex gate (wave-2) P1: the phone leg fires ONLY with a contact CONTEXT word, so a signed statistical
  3336	# estimate ("+0.123 (0.045)") — digits/dots/parens/spaces, no contact context — is never dropped.
  3337	_FURN_CONTACT_CTX_RE = re.compile(
  3338	    r"\b(?:phone|telephone|fax|hotline|dial|call\s*back)\b",
  3339	    re.IGNORECASE,
  3340	)
  3341	
  3342	
  3343	def _source_furniture_chrome_enabled() -> bool:
  3344	    return os.getenv("PG_SOURCE_FURNITURE_CHROME", "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
  3345	
  3346	
  3347	def _contains_source_furniture_chrome(text: str) -> bool:
  3348	    """True iff ``text`` carries page/source FURNITURE chrome the enumerated categories miss: a PDF
  3349	    object-dictionary recital, a tel:/mailto: contact line, a wage figure inside a nav/pipe table or a
  3350	    table-widget id (BLS OOH), >=2 inline markdown links (nav link-furniture), or a scraped author
  3351	    masthead byline glued to a profile link. SUPPRESS-ONLY, faithfulness-neutral."""
  3352	    if not _source_furniture_chrome_enabled():
  3353	        return False
  3354	    s = str(text or "")
  3355	    if not s.strip():
  3356	        return False
  3357	    if _FURN_PDF_OBJ_RE.search(s):
  3358	        return True
  3359	    if _FURN_CONTACT_RE.search(s):
  3360	        return True
  3361	    if _FURN_WAGE_RE.search(s) and ("|" in s or _FURN_TBWIDGET_RE.search(s)):
  3362	        return True
  3363	    # I-deepfix-001 wave-2 (#1370): the box2 §-1.1 furniture classes wave-1 missed.
  3364	    # HARD legs (unambiguous furniture — fire regardless of finding-signal):
  3365	    if _FURN_CHARTDUMP_RE.search(s):  # a run of >=3 whitespace-separated bare %-tokens (chart legend)
  3366	        return True
  3367	    if _FURN_PUBLISHER_RE.search(s):  # CC-license / publisher boilerplate
  3368	        return True
  3369	    if _FURN_NAVCTA_RE.search(s):  # "view details" / "click here" (never inside a finding)
  3370	        return True
  3371	    # I-deepfix-001 F2 (#1371) — the 7 F2 furniture legs (grant/cookie/media-player/paywall/Crossref/
  3372	    # gov-banner/Split-View) are NOT screened here: they feed ONLY the F2 PLACEMENT path
  3373	    # (``_contains_f2_placement_furniture``), never this shared predicate. Codex F2 gate iter-1 (HC-2):
  3374	    # this predicate ALSO feeds pre-existing DROP seams, so adding vocabulary here would WIDEN a drop of
  3375	    # a real source. §-1.3 keeps furniture a placement (move to the ledger), never a drop.
  3376	    # SOFT legs (Codex P1/P1-cont: guarded — a unit with a real finding SIGNAL is never dropped here.
  3377	    # Phone is under the guard AND format-tight AND context-gated so a signed statistic like
  3378	    # "Recruitment increased employment by +0.123 (0.045)" is triple-safe from a false drop):
  3379	    if not _FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(s):
  3380	        if _FURN_PHONE_RE.search(s) and _FURN_CONTACT_CTX_RE.search(s):  # a contact phone, not a statistic
  3381	            return True
  3382	        if _FURN_DOCTITLE_RE.search(s):  # a pure doc-title RECITAL ("The document is titled …")
  3383	            return True
  3384	        if len(_FURN_MDLINK_RE.findall(s)) >= 2:  # a link-farm / nav block, not a linked finding
  3385	            return True
  3386	    return False
  3387

  3389	def is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(
  3390	    text: str,
  3391	    *,
  3392	    require_sentence_form: bool = False,
  3393	    known_words: "set[str] | frozenset[str] | None" = None,
  3394	) -> bool:
  3395	    """THE ONE shared render-side chrome+truncation predicate (I-wire-012 #1326; I-wire-013 #1327).
  3396	
  3397	    True iff ``text`` is page-furniture chrome, a CAPTCHA/boilerplate stub, a numbered
  3398	    ToC / CC-license / masthead / login-wall fragment, a standalone scraped doc label
  3399	    ("Abstract"/"AI Summary"), an author-ORCID/affiliation list, a bare DOI row, glued
  3400	    page-furniture welded INTO real prose (I-wire-013 CONTAINMENT), or a mid-word/cut-span
  3401	    TRUNCATION. With ``require_sentence_form=True`` it ALSO rejects a mid-word-START fragment
  3402	    and an incomplete sentence (bullet/header surfaces only).
  3403	
  3404	    ``known_words`` (I-wire-013 #1327): when a caller supplies the run's corpus-vocabulary
  3405	    allowlist, the truncation leg ALSO catches a CORPUS-GROUNDED span cut at a ``[N]`` boundary
  3406	    (a non-inflectional prefix/suffix of a longer corpus word — "… 1.2 Resea.[14]"). It defaults
  3407	    to ``None`` so every existing caller (including the canary) is unchanged: no corpus → the
  3408	    boundary-cut leg is skipped → no new false positive.
  3409	
  3410	    SUPPRESS-ONLY: never promotes a unit, never alters a faithfulness VERDICT. The base
  3411	    screen (boilerplate/web-chrome/CAPTCHA) ALWAYS runs (preserving the pre-I-wire-012
  3412	    behaviour of every existing consumer); the NEW categories + truncation are gated on
  3413	    ``render_chrome_screen_enabled()`` (default ON) so a ``PG_RENDER_CHROME_SCREEN=0``
  3414	    run is byte-identical to the legacy base screen."""
  3415	    if not text or not str(text).strip():
  3416	        return True  # an empty unit is non-assertional by definition
  3417	    s = str(text)
  3418	    if _base_junk(s):
  3419	        return True
  3420	    if not render_chrome_screen_enabled():
  3421	        return False  # NEW categories OFF -> byte-identical to the legacy base screen
  3422	    if _is_new_chrome_category(s):
  3423	        return True
  3424	    # I-deepfix-001 P0 (box2 chrome infestation): the missing-vocabulary furniture classes. SUPPRESS-ONLY,
  3425	    # faithfulness-neutral; inside the render_chrome_screen_enabled() gate so PG_RENDER_CHROME_SCREEN=0 stays
  3426	    # byte-identical. Auto-fixes _screen_render_chrome_prose + _compose_junk_screen + the render seam at once.
  3427	    if _contains_source_furniture_chrome(s):
  3428	        return True
  3429	    try:
  3430	        from src.polaris_graph.generator.key_findings import (  # noqa: PLC0415
  3431	            is_truncated_fragment,
  3432	        )
  3433	        # When a corpus allowlist is supplied, treat the unit as eligible at BOTH boundaries so the
  3434	        # corpus-grounded span-cut leg fires on a cut at the unit's leading/trailing ``[N]`` edge
  3435	        # (the chokepoint splits the report into per-citation units before calling this). With no
  3436	        # corpus (known_words=None) the boundary flags are inert and only the marker leg runs.
  3437	        _eligible = known_words is not None
  3438	        if is_truncated_fragment(
  3439	            s,
  3440	            known_words,
  3441	            ends_before_marker=_eligible,
  3442	            starts_after_marker=_eligible,
  3443	        ):
  3444	            return True
  3445	    except Exception:  # pragma: no cover - key_findings is stable in-tree
  3446	        pass
  3447	    if require_sentence_form and _is_unrenderable_sentence_form(s):
  3448	        return True
  3449	    return False
  3450	
  3451	
  3452	def _contains_f2_placement_furniture(text: Any) -> bool:
  3453	    """The F2 (#1371) PLACEMENT-ONLY furniture vocabulary — the 7 legs (grant/ack back-matter,
  3454	    cookie-consent notice, media-player reader control, paywall unlock-code token, Crossref widget,
  3455	    US-gov site banner, glued "Split View" control) that the F2 fix added.
  3456	
  3457	    Codex F2 gate iter-1 (HC-2): these legs are consulted EXCLUSIVELY by the F2 body/ledger PLACEMENT
  3458	    path (``is_offtopic_or_chrome_for_placement`` / ``_row_routes_to_ledger``) — deliberately NOT by the
  3459	    shared ``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` predicate, because that shared predicate ALSO feeds
  3460	    pre-existing DROP seams (retrieval fetch-furniture screen, verified_compose, key_findings,
  3461	    run_honest_sweep). Keeping the F2 vocab out of the shared predicate means a match here can ONLY MOVE
  3462	    a unit below the appendix boundary into the ledger (§-1.3 PLACEMENT), never a drop / cap / thin. The
  3463	    faithfulness engine is untouched. Gated by ``render_chrome_screen_enabled()`` so a
  3464	    ``PG_RENDER_CHROME_SCREEN=0`` run is inert (the F2 furniture legs disappear) — matching the base
  3465	    screen's own kill-switch. PURE."""
  3466	    if not render_chrome_screen_enabled():
  3467	        return False
  3468	    s = str(text or "")
  3469	    if not s.strip():
  3470	        return False
  3471	    if _FURN_GRANT_RE.search(s):  # grant/ack back-matter ("under Grant 435-…", "Corresponding author:")
  3472	        return True
  3473	    if _FURN_COOKIE_RE.search(s) and _FURN_COOKIE_CTX_RE.search(s):  # cookie-consent notice (noun + signature)
  3474	        return True
  3475	    if _FURN_MEDIAPLAYER_RE.search(s):  # media-player reader control ("… playback rate …")
  3476	        return True
  3477	    if _FURN_PAYWALL_RE.search(s):  # paywall unlock-code token ("unlocked article code of …")
  3478	        return True
  3479	    if _FURN_CROSSREF_RE.search(s):  # Crossref citation-count widget ("Crossref 0 Crossref 0")
  3480	        return True
  3481	    if _FURN_GOVSITE_RE.search(s):  # US-gov site banner
  3482	        return True
  3483	    if _FURN_SPLITVIEW_RE.search(s):  # glued "Split View" reader-pane control ("Design: - Split View")
  3484	        return True
  3485	    return False
  3486	
  3487	
  3488	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  3489	# I-deepfix-006 A/B (#1376) — INLINE furniture strip (SPAN-LEVEL, suppress-only, source NEVER deleted).
  3490	#
  3491	# THE GAP (Fable A/B root cause): the furniture predicates above route a WHOLE unit to the ledger or
  3492	# drop it, but a fixed boilerplate FRAGMENT welded INSIDE an otherwise-real clause survives — e.g.
  3493	# "An official website of the United States government The unemployment rate fell 0.4%", a "Crossref 0"
  3494	# citation-count widget glued to a finding, a "5 Minute Read Time" reader token, a "02-10-2025" date
  3495	# stamp, or IMF working-paper front-matter ("© 2025 International Monetary Fund", "WP/25/123",
  3496	# "Prepared by …", "Authorized for distribution by …", "The authors would like to thank …") lifted into
  3497	# the same extraction blob as a real sentence. This EXCISES the boilerplate fragment while KEEPING the
  3498	# surrounding clause. It never touches the evidence pool, the bibliography, or a faithfulness verdict —
  3499	# removing furniture text can only SHORTEN a rendered unit, never fabricate a number/word (all numeric
  3500	# comparison stays with the frozen strict_verify). §-1.3.1 span-level carve-out.
  3501	#
  3502	# FAITHFULNESS SAFETY: fixed-token furniture (gov banner / Crossref widget / reading-time / WP number /
  3503	# date stamp) never carries a finding, so it is excised unconditionally. The clause-form front-matter
  3504	# (IMF copyright / "Prepared by" / "Authorized for distribution by" / acknowledgements) is excised ONLY
  3505	# when the matched clause carries NO finding signal (``_FINDING_SIGNAL_RE``) — so a real attribution
  3506	# such as "prepared by the OECD, which found unemployment rose 2%" is KEPT (fail-open). Default-ON;
  3507	# ``PG_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP=0`` restores byte-identical legacy text.
  3508	_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP_ENV = "PG_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP"
  3509	
  3510	# Fixed-token furniture — excised unconditionally (never carries a finding).
  3511	_INLINE_GOVBANNER_RE = re.compile(
  3512	    r"An official website of the United States government\.?", re.IGNORECASE
  3513	)
  3514	_INLINE_CROSSREF_RE = re.compile(r"\bCrossref\s+\d+")
  3515	_INLINE_READTIME_RE = re.compile(r"\b\d+\s+Minute\s+Read\s+Time\b", re.IGNORECASE)
  3516	_INLINE_WP_NUMBER_RE = re.compile(r"\bWP/\d+/\d+\b")
  3517	# A standalone dd-mm-yyyy / mm-dd-yyyy date stamp (scrape furniture). A real finding never renders a
  3518	# figure in this hyphenated calendar-stamp form, so removing it never drops a finding number.
  3519	_INLINE_DATESTAMP_RE = re.compile(r"\b\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}\b")
  3520	
  3521	# Clause-form front-matter — excised ONLY when the matched clause carries no finding signal (fail-open).
  3522	_INLINE_IMF_COPYRIGHT_RE = re.compile(
  3523	    r"©\s*\d{0,4}\s*International Monetary Fund", re.IGNORECASE
  3524	)
  3525	_INLINE_PREPARED_RE = re.compile(r"\bPrepared by\b[^.!?\n]*[.!?]?", re.IGNORECASE)
  3526	_INLINE_AUTHORIZED_RE = re.compile(
  3527	    r"\bAuthorized for distribution by\b[^.!?\n]*[.!?]?", re.IGNORECASE
  3528	)
  3529	_INLINE_ACK_RE = re.compile(
  3530	    r"(?:\b(?:the\s+authors?|we|i)\s+)?would\s+like\s+to\s+thank\b[^.!?\n]*[.!?]?",
  3531	    re.IGNORECASE,
  3532	)
  3533	_INLINE_ORPHAN_LEAD_RE = re.compile(r"^[\s,;:.\-–—]+")
  3534	_INLINE_WS_RUN_RE = re.compile(r"[ \t]{2,}")
  3535	
  3536	
  3537	def _inline_furniture_strip_enabled() -> bool:
  3538	    """Kill-switch PG_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP (default ON). OFF / empty => the inline strip never runs =>
  3539	    byte-identical legacy text. Mirrors the ``_snap_span_enabled`` off-token convention."""
  3540	    return os.getenv(_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
  3541	
  3542	
  3543	def _strip_clause_if_no_finding(rx: "re.Pattern[str]", text: str) -> str:
  3544	    """Remove every match of ``rx`` from ``text`` UNLESS the matched clause itself carries a finding
  3545	    signal (a decimal / percentage / finding verb) — in which case the clause is a real attribution and
  3546	    is KEPT untouched (fail-open). Pure."""
  3547	    def _repl(m: "re.Match[str]") -> str:
  3548	        frag = m.group(0)
  3549	        if _FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(frag):
  3550	            return frag  # a real finding is welded to the phrase — keep it whole
  3551	        return " "
  3552	    return rx.sub(_repl, text)
  3553	
  3554	
  3555	def strip_inline_furniture(text: Any) -> str:
  3556	    """Excise fixed boilerplate FRAGMENTS from inside a kept unit while keeping the surrounding clause
  3557	    (I-deepfix-006 A/B). SUPPRESS-only, faithfulness-neutral: it can only remove furniture text, never
  3558	    fabricate. Byte-identical to the input when the kill-switch is OFF or nothing matches. Pure."""
  3559	    if not _inline_furniture_strip_enabled():
  3560	        return str(text or "")
  3561	    s = str(text or "")
  3562	    if not s.strip():
  3563	        return s
  3564	    # Fixed-token furniture: excised unconditionally (never a finding).
  3565	    for rx in (
  3566	        _INLINE_GOVBANNER_RE,
  3567	        _INLINE_CROSSREF_RE,
  3568	        _INLINE_READTIME_RE,
  3569	        _INLINE_WP_NUMBER_RE,
  3570	        _INLINE_DATESTAMP_RE,
  3571	    ):
  3572	        s = rx.sub(" ", s)
  3573	    # Clause-form front-matter: excised only when the clause carries no finding signal (fail-open).
  3574	    for rx in (
  3575	        _INLINE_IMF_COPYRIGHT_RE,
  3576	        _INLINE_PREPARED_RE,
  3577	        _INLINE_AUTHORIZED_RE,
  3578	        _INLINE_ACK_RE,
  3579	    ):
  3580	        s = _strip_clause_if_no_finding(rx, s)
  3581	    # Tidy whitespace + orphan leading punctuation left by a removed prefix fragment.
  3582	    s = _INLINE_WS_RUN_RE.sub(" ", s)
  3583	    s = _INLINE_ORPHAN_LEAD_RE.sub("", s)
  3584	    return s.strip()
  3585	
  3586	
  3587	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  3588	# I-deepfix-006 C (#1376) — INLINE markup strip (SPAN-LEVEL, suppress-only). Removes raw render markup a
  3589	# strict_verify-passing unit can carry: a "](http…)" markdown-link remnant, a bare URL, a bare URL-path
  3590	# fragment with a query string ("/search/researchers?query=*&page=1"), an orphan markdown heading
  3591	# ("## 2"), and a stray emphasis marker ("_**"). Over-stripping markup is faithfulness-safe — a URL /
  3592	# heading marker / emphasis token is never a finding number or word. Default-ON; PG_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP=0
  3593	# restores byte-identical legacy text.
  3594	_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP_ENV = "PG_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP"
  3595	_INLINE_MDLINK_REMNANT_RE = re.compile(r"\]\(https?://[^)]*\)")
  3596	_INLINE_BARE_URL_RE = re.compile(r"https?://\S+")
  3597	# A bare URL-PATH query fragment ("/search/researchers?institution=41ILO_INST&query=*&page=1"): a "/"
  3598	# path carrying a "?...=" query param. Requiring the "=" avoids matching real prose like "what/why?".
  3599	_INLINE_URL_PATH_QUERY_RE = re.compile(r"(?<![\w])/[^\s)\]]*\?[^\s)\]]*=[^\s)\]]*")
  3600	# An orphan markdown heading welded MID-line ("… adoption grew. ## 2 firms invested") — the leading
  3601	# ``(?<=\S)`` guard means a REAL numbered header at line start ("## 2 Results") is NEVER matched.
  3602	_INLINE_ORPHAN_HEADING_RE = re.compile(r"(?<=\S)\s+#{1,6}\s+\d+(?=\s|$)")
  3603	_INLINE_STRAY_EMPHASIS_RE = re.compile(r"_\*\*|\*\*_")
  3604	
  3605	
  3606	def _inline_markup_strip_enabled() -> bool:
  3607	    """Kill-switch PG_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP (default ON). OFF / empty => byte-identical legacy text."""
  3608	    return os.getenv(_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
  3609	
  3610	
  3611	def strip_inline_markup(text: Any) -> str:
  3612	    """Excise raw render-markup fragments (markdown-link remnants, bare URLs / URL-path query fragments,
  3613	    orphan markdown headings, stray emphasis markers) while keeping the surrounding prose. SUPPRESS-only,
  3614	    faithfulness-neutral. Byte-identical when the kill-switch is OFF or nothing matches. Pure."""
  3615	    if not _inline_markup_strip_enabled():
  3616	        return str(text or "")
  3617	    s = str(text or "")
  3618	    if not s.strip():
  3619	        return s
  3620	    s = _INLINE_MDLINK_REMNANT_RE.sub(" ", s)
  3621	    s = _INLINE_BARE_URL_RE.sub(" ", s)
  3622	    s = _INLINE_URL_PATH_QUERY_RE.sub(" ", s)
  3623	    s = _INLINE_ORPHAN_HEADING_RE.sub(" ", s)
  3624	    s = _INLINE_STRAY_EMPHASIS_RE.sub(" ", s)
  3625	    s = _INLINE_WS_RUN_RE.sub(" ", s)
  3626	    s = _INLINE_ORPHAN_LEAD_RE.sub("", s)
  3627	    return s.strip()
  3628	
  3629	
  3630	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  3631	# I-deepfix-006 D (#1376) — SHELL-SOURCE input screen (held out of the generator's drafting INPUT; the
  3632	# source STAYS in the pool + bibliography + disclosure — never deleted). A "shell" source is one whose
  3633	# direct_quote is DOMINATED by bracketed empty-anchor markdown links ("[](…)") and/or search-query URLs
  3634	# with NO finding sentence (ev_716 = a pure nav/search link-farm). Its honest meta-description
  3635	# ("The span consists of a repository collection link …") self-entails its own span and PASSES
  3636	# strict_verify, so it must be screened at the drafting INPUT. A per-unit narration-detector belt also
  3637	# withholds a shell-narration sentence lifted into an otherwise-real source. Default-ON;
  3638	# PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN=0 restores byte-identical legacy behaviour.
  3639	_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN_ENV = "PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN"
  3640	_SHELL_EMPTY_ANCHOR_RE = re.compile(r"\[\]\(")
  3641	_SHELL_SEARCH_URL_RE = re.compile(
  3642	    r"/search\b|[?&](?:query|q|page|institution|search)=|query=\*", re.IGNORECASE
  3643	)
  3644	_SHELL_NARRATION_RE = re.compile(
  3645	    r"the\s+span\s+consists\s+of|repository\s+collection\s+link|"
  3646	    r"search\s+query\s+for\s+all\s+results",
  3647	    re.IGNORECASE,
  3648	)
  3649	# Once the bracketed empty-anchor links and URLs are removed, a shell has very little real prose left.
  3650	_SHELL_RESIDUAL_PROSE_MIN_CHARS = 40
  3651	
  3652	
  3653	def _shell_source_input_screen_enabled() -> bool:
  3654	    """Kill-switch PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN (default ON). OFF / empty => byte-identical legacy."""
  3655	    return os.getenv(_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
  3656	
  3657	
  3658	def _is_shell_narration(text: Any) -> bool:
  3659	    """True iff a unit is SHELL NARRATION — a meta-description of a nav/search link-farm ("The span
  3660	    consists of …", "repository collection link", "search query for all results"). Pure."""
  3661	    return bool(_SHELL_NARRATION_RE.search(str(text or "")))
  3662	
  3663	
  3664	def is_shell_source_quote(direct_quote: Any) -> bool:
  3665	    """True iff a source's whole ``direct_quote`` is a nav/search SHELL — dominated by bracketed
  3666	    empty-anchor markdown links and/or search-query URLs, carrying NO finding sentence and almost no
  3667	    real prose once the link/URL scaffolding is removed. FAIL-CLOSED to KEEP (return False) on anything
  3668	    ambiguous: a quote carrying a finding signal, or one with substantial residual prose, is NEVER a
  3669	    shell. Pure — the source is only held out of drafting INPUT, never dropped from the pool."""
  3670	    if not _shell_source_input_screen_enabled():
  3671	        return False
  3672	    s = str(direct_quote or "")
  3673	    if not s.strip():
  3674	        return False
  3675	    # A real finding sentence anywhere => never a shell (fail-open to KEEP).
  3676	    if _FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(s):
  3677	        return False
  3678	    empty_anchors = len(_SHELL_EMPTY_ANCHOR_RE.findall(s))
  3679	    has_search_url = bool(_SHELL_SEARCH_URL_RE.search(s))
  3680	    if empty_anchors < 1 and not has_search_url and not _SHELL_NARRATION_RE.search(s):
  3681	        return False  # no link-farm / search / narration signature at all => not a shell
  3682	    # Measure residual prose after stripping the link/URL scaffolding: a shell has almost none.
  3683	    residual = _SHELL_EMPTY_ANCHOR_RE.sub(" ", s)
  3684	    residual = _INLINE_MDLINK_REMNANT_RE.sub(" ", residual)
  3685	    residual = _INLINE_BARE_URL_RE.sub(" ", residual)
  3686	    residual = _INLINE_URL_PATH_QUERY_RE.sub(" ", residual)
  3687	    residual = _SHELL_NARRATION_RE.sub(" ", residual)
  3688	    residual_alpha = "".join(ch for ch in residual if ch.isalpha() or ch.isspace()).strip()
  3689	    # Dominated by link/URL scaffolding + shell narration, with little real prose left => a shell.
  3690	    if (empty_anchors >= 2) or (empty_anchors >= 1 and has_search_url) or _SHELL_NARRATION_RE.search(s):
  3691	        return len(residual_alpha) < _SHELL_RESIDUAL_PROSE_MIN_CHARS
  3692	    return False
  3693	
  3694	
  3695	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  3696	# I-deepfix-006 E (#1376) — EVIDENCE-BASE finding-signal PREFERENCE (a §-1.3 WEIGHT/PLACEMENT: DEMOTE
  3697	# to the low-relevance ledger, NEVER a drop). An on-topic marketing PREAMBLE with no finding signal
  3698	# (Thompson Rivers "top 10 predictions for 2025", AACSB "is leading the way in business education")
  3699	# self-entails its own span and passes strict_verify, polluting the "Evidence base" body. Because such a
  3700	# source is credible + on-topic (§-1.3: never deleted, only weighted), E DEMOTES it BELOW the appendix
  3701	# boundary into the "Low-relevance evidence (kept at weight)" ledger — it STAYS in the pool, bibliography,
  3702	# and disclosure. The demotion is a LAST-RESORT leg in ``_row_routes_to_ledger``: it fires ONLY for an
  3703	# UNJUDGED source (no positive judged relevance label, no numeric selection_relevance) whose representative
  3704	# text carries no finding signal — a real judge that SAW the content (rules 1/4) always wins. Default-ON;
  3705	# PG_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE=0 removes the leg => byte-identical legacy routing.
  3706	_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE_ENV = "PG_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE"
  3707	
  3708	
  3709	def _evidence_base_finding_preference_enabled() -> bool:
  3710	    """Kill-switch PG_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE (default ON). OFF / empty => the ledger-routing
  3711	    leg never fires => byte-identical legacy body/ledger partition."""
  3712	    return os.getenv(_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in (
  3713	        "0", "false", "off", "no",
  3714	    )
  3715	
  3716	
  3717	def _row_is_marketing_only_preamble(text: Any) -> bool:
  3718	    """True iff ``text`` is a marketing PREAMBLE with no finding signal (no decimal / percentage /
  3719	    finding verb) — the TRU/AACSB shape. A demotion signal for an UNJUDGED row only; NEVER a drop.
  3720	    FAIL-OPEN to KEEP (False) on empty text or when the kill-switch is OFF. Pure."""
  3721	    if not _evidence_base_finding_preference_enabled():
  3722	        return False
  3723	    s = str(text or "").strip()
  3724	    if not s:
  3725	        return False
  3726	    return not bool(_FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(s))
  3727	
  3728	
  3729	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  3730	# I-deepfix-001 F2 (#1371) — UNIFIED BODY-PLACEMENT SCREEN + Low-relevance ledger partition.
  3731	#
  3732	# THE BUG (Fable F2 root cause): a grammatical sentence ABOUT junk (page furniture that renders as a
  3733	# coherent line, or an on-topic-looking sentence that is actually off the research question's topic)
  3734	# self-entails its own verbatim span, so it PASSES the frozen strict_verify gate and survives into the
  3735	# raw carry-up surfaces (Verified Findings / Abstract / Key Findings / Conclusion / Evidence base /
  3736	# CWF facet sections). Those surfaces have a FORM-chrome screen (``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable``)
  3737	# but NO topicality screen. Meanwhile the pipeline ALREADY computes per-row judged relevance
  3738	# (``selection_relevance`` + the W2 ``content_relevance_label``) that these seams ignore.
  3739	#
  3740	# THE FIX — §-1.3 WEIGHT / PLACEMENT, NEVER DELETE: make body PLACEMENT respect the weight already
  3741	# computed. A unit that is FURNITURE or confidently OFF-topic is MOVED BELOW the appendix boundary into
  3742	# a clearly-labelled "Low-relevance evidence (kept at weight)" ledger — it STAYS in the evidence pool,
  3743	# the bibliography, and the disclosure; nothing is dropped, capped, or thinned. The frozen faithfulness
  3744	# engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role D8 / provenance / span-grounding) is UNTOUCHED. The topicality
  3745	# leg reuses the EXISTING grounding tokenizer (``provenance_generator._content_words``) — no new model.
  3746	#
  3747	# SHIPPED SCOPE (F2 gate iter-3, resolving the dual-gate scope-wiring finding): the ledger PLACEMENT is
  3748	# wired into the two EV-ID-ordered raw carry-up surfaces — the "Evidence base" breadth section AND the
  3749	# weighted-enrichment "Corroborated Weighted Findings" (CWF) facet/flat sections — via the SINGLE
  3750	# order-preserving production entry ``partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger`` (both surfaces consume
  3751	# its BODY partition; the ledger rows render once below the appendix; see multi_section_generator.py at
  3752	# the CWF plan-build seam + assembly). The Verified Findings / Abstract / Key Findings / Conclusion
  3753	# surfaces are SYNTHESIZED PROSE, not ev-id lists, and stay covered by the pre-existing FORM-chrome +
  3754	# strict_verify screen; F2 does NOT retrofit a topicality screen onto synthesized prose in this ship.
  3755	# ``is_offtopic_or_chrome_for_placement`` (the unified TEXT predicate) and
  3756	# ``partition_body_and_low_relevance_ledger`` (the row-list form) are the general/reusable forms the
  3757	# unit tests exercise directly; they share the SAME ``_row_routes_to_ledger`` / furniture / topicality
  3758	# core that ships to production through ``partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger``.
  3759	_OFFTOPIC_PLACEMENT_MIN_WORDS = 6  # a zero-overlap unit this long is confidently off-topic; below it,
  3760	#                                    only a unit ALSO carrying no finding signal is demoted (fail-open).
  3761	
  3762	# Report-INSTRUCTION scaffolding words (deliverable-format vocabulary, NOT topic). A verbose benchmark
  3763	# question ("write a COMPREHENSIVE research REPORT drawing on credible SOURCES … with COLUMNS …") is
  3764	# laden with these; if they stay in the topical reference an off-topic intruder that merely says
  3765	# "publication"/"comprehensive"/"analysis" escapes the topicality demotion. Stripping them from the
  3766	# PLACEMENT reference ONLY (never from the production ``_question_topic_terms`` the ordering/promotion/
  3767	# span gates use) sharpens the lexical FALLBACK without touching any live ordering. Domain-agnostic
  3768	# (these describe the deliverable, not any field), fail-open (an over-strip keeps a source in body,
  3769	# never a drop — §-1.3). The clearly-topical words (impact, employment, occupation, industry, risk,
  3770	# …) are deliberately NOT here.
  3771	#
  3772	# Codex F2 gate iter-1 (HC-5 P2): the plausibly-TOPICAL words are pruned OUT of this set so they stay
  3773	# as live topic terms — ``evidence``, ``literature``, ``application(s)``, ``area(s)``, ``case(s)``,
  3774	# ``country/countries``, ``region(s)``, ``view(s)``, ``example(s)``, ``detail(s)``. In a grants /
  3775	# bibliometrics / geography / privacy report those ARE the topic, so stripping them could have
  3776	# over-routed a real on-topic source to the ledger when one of them was its only shared term. They are
  3777	# NOT deliverable-only words. Only the unambiguous deliverable-FORMAT vocabulary remains below.
  3778	_REPORT_SCAFFOLDING_TERMS = frozenset({
  3779	    "publication", "comprehensive", "analysis", "report", "reports", "research", "researching",
  3780	    "source", "sources", "provide", "provides", "summary", "summarizing", "table", "tables",
  3781	    "column", "columns", "section", "sections", "structure", "specific", "specifically",
  3782	    "key", "main", "detailing", "drawing", "please", "write", "written", "available", "credible",
  3783	    "relevant", "restriction", "date", "dates", "type", "types", "aspect", "aspects",
  3784	    "particular", "regarding", "limitation", "limitations", "support",
  3785	    "supporting", "end", "separate",
  3786	})
  3787	
  3788	
  3789	def _placement_topic_terms(research_question: str) -> frozenset[str]:
  3790	    """The PLACEMENT topical reference: ``_question_topic_terms`` minus the report-instruction
  3791	    scaffolding words. Used ONLY by the F2 body-placement predicate + ledger routing so the noisy
  3792	    lexical FALLBACK is sharpened; the production ordering/promotion/span gates keep the full
  3793	    ``_question_topic_terms`` (byte-identical). Empty question => empty set => fail-open (keep-all)."""
  3794	    return frozenset(_question_topic_terms(research_question)) - _REPORT_SCAFFOLDING_TERMS
  3795	
  3796	
  3797	def _is_offtopic_for_placement(text: Any, question_terms: "frozenset[str] | set[str]") -> bool:
  3798	    """True iff a grammatical unit is confidently OFF the research question's topic — a PLACEMENT
  3799	    demotion signal, NEVER a drop. FAIL-OPEN (return False => keep in body) whenever: there are no
  3800	    question terms (empty/blank research question => every legacy caller is byte-identical), the unit
  3801	    carries no content words, or the unit shares ANY content word with the question. A unit with ZERO
  3802	    question overlap is off-topic only when it is long enough to judge (``>= _OFFTOPIC_PLACEMENT_MIN_
  3803	    WORDS`` content words) OR — for a terse unit — it ALSO carries no finding signal (a real terse
  3804	    finding carries a percentage / decimal / finding verb, so it is never demoted here). PURE."""
  3805	    if not question_terms:
  3806	        return False
  3807	    try:
  3808	        from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (  # noqa: PLC0415
  3809	            _content_words,
  3810	        )
  3811	        unit_terms = _content_words(str(text or ""))
  3812	    except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — fail-safe: a tokenizer/import failure must never DEMOTE a real
  3813	        return False  #                    source to the ledger (§-1.3 fail-open, mirrors _ledger_relevance_floor)
  3814	    if not unit_terms:
  3815	        return False
  3816	    if unit_terms & set(question_terms):
  3817	        return False  # any shared topic term => on-topic, KEEP in body
  3818	    if len(unit_terms) >= _OFFTOPIC_PLACEMENT_MIN_WORDS:
  3819	        return True   # long, zero-overlap => confidently foreign to the question
  3820	    # terse + zero-overlap: demote only when it also lacks a finding signal (guard a real terse finding)
  3821	    return not bool(_FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(str(text or "")))
  3822	
  3823	
  3824	def is_offtopic_or_chrome_for_placement(text: Any, *, research_question: str = "") -> bool:
  3825	    """The unified F2 BODY-PLACEMENT screen. True iff a grammatical, strict_verify-passable unit is
  3826	    page/source FURNITURE (``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` — the FORM screen, honouring its
  3827	    ``render_chrome_screen_enabled()`` kill-switch) OR confidently OFF the research question's topic
  3828	    (``_is_offtopic_for_placement`` — the topicality screen this seam previously lacked).
  3829	
  3830	    A True verdict routes the unit BELOW the appendix boundary into the labelled "Low-relevance
  3831	    evidence (kept at weight)" ledger — a §-1.3 PLACEMENT demotion, NEVER a drop / cap / thin. The
  3832	    source stays in the pool, the bibliography, and the disclosure. The faithfulness engine is
  3833	    untouched. FAIL-OPEN for the topicality leg on an empty research question (byte-identical legacy).
  3834	
  3835	    The FORM leg is the shared ``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` predicate PLUS the F2 placement-only
  3836	    furniture vocabulary (``_contains_f2_placement_furniture``) — the F2 vocab lives on the PLACEMENT
  3837	    path only, never on the shared drop predicate (Codex F2 iter-1 HC-2).
  3838	
  3839	    SCOPE (F2 gate iter-3): this unified TEXT predicate is the general/reusable form the unit tests
  3840	    exercise directly. The SHIPPED production placement is the order-preserving, judged-relevance-aware
  3841	    ``partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger`` (wired into both ev-id carry-up surfaces: Evidence base +
  3842	    CWF), which shares this predicate's furniture + topicality legs via ``_row_routes_to_ledger``."""
  3843	    if is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(text) or _contains_f2_placement_furniture(text):
  3844	        return True
  3845	    return _is_offtopic_for_placement(text, _placement_topic_terms(research_question))
  3846	
  3847	
  3848	# ── Low-relevance ledger: the labelled below-the-appendix partition (§-1.3 PLACEMENT, never a drop) ──
  3849	_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER_TITLE = "Low-relevance evidence (kept at weight)"
  3850	_ENV_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER = "PG_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER"  # default ON
  3851	
  3852	
  3853	def low_relevance_ledger_enabled() -> bool:
  3854	    """Kill-switch ``PG_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER`` (default ON). OFF => the ledger partition never fires
  3855	    => every row stays in the body order => byte-identical to the legacy single-surface render."""
  3856	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER, "1").strip().lower() not in (
  3857	        "0", "false", "no", "off",
  3858	    )
  3859	
  3860	
  3861	def _ledger_relevance_floor() -> float:
  3862	    """The judged-relevance floor for the body/ledger split — the SAME ``PG_RELEVANCE_FLOOR`` the
  3863	    retrieval + enrichment gates use (default 0.30), with its fail-loud (0.0, 1.0] validation. A row
  3864	    whose JUDGED ``selection_relevance`` sits below this is routed to the ledger (placement, not a
  3865	    drop). Lazy import keeps this module import-time independent of the retrieval side."""
  3866	    try:
  3867	        from src.polaris_graph.retrieval.evidence_selector import (  # noqa: PLC0415
  3868	            parse_relevance_floor,
  3869	        )
  3870	        return parse_relevance_floor(os.environ.get("PG_RELEVANCE_FLOOR"))
  3871	    except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — fail-safe default; a broken import must never crash placement
  3872	        return 0.30
  3873	
  3874	
  3875	def _ledger_row_text(row: Any) -> str:
  3876	    """The render text a placement screen should judge: the member's direct quote / statement, else a
  3877	    join of the standard topic text fields. PURE read; never a faithfulness touch."""
  3878	    if not isinstance(row, dict):
  3879	        return ""
  3880	    quote = _member_quote(row)
  3881	    if quote:
  3882	        return quote
  3883	    return " ".join(str(row.get(f) or "") for f in _TOPIC_TEXT_FIELDS).strip()
  3884	
  3885	
  3886	def _ledger_weight_relevance_key(row: Any) -> "tuple[float, float]":
  3887	    """The ``(weight, relevance)`` ordering key (both DESC when negated by the caller). Reads the
  3888	    row's basket ``weight_mass`` (else ``credibility_weight``/``weight``) and its judged
  3889	    ``selection_relevance`` (missing => the keep-neutral sentinel). Ordering only — never a filter."""
  3890	    weight = 0.0
  3891	    for field in ("weight_mass", "credibility_weight", "weight"):
  3892	        raw = row.get(field) if isinstance(row, dict) else None
  3893	        if raw is not None:
  3894	            try:
  3895	                weight = float(raw)
  3896	                break
  3897	            except (TypeError, ValueError):
  3898	                continue
  3899	    rel = _row_relevance(row)
  3900	    return (weight, _relevance_sort_key(rel))
  3901	
  3902	
  3903	def _row_routes_to_ledger(
  3904	    row: Any, question_terms: "frozenset[str] | set[str]", relevance_floor: float
  3905	) -> bool:
  3906	    """Per-row body-vs-ledger verdict. POSITIVE judged relevance FIRST, then furniture, then the rest
  3907	    (Codex F2 gate iter-1 P1: positive-relevance-first ordering):
  3908	      1. A POSITIVE judged ``content_relevance_label`` (relevant / escalated_relevant) => BODY. A real
  3909	         upstream judge that SAW the content wins over every heuristic leg (§-1.3 WEIGHT-not-FILTER), so
  3910	         a judged-relevant row whose text incidentally trips a broad furniture regex is NOT demoted.
  3911	      2. FURNITURE (``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` OR the F2 placement-only vocab
  3912	         ``_contains_f2_placement_furniture``) => ledger. The F2 vocab lives on the PLACEMENT path only,
  3913	         never on the shared drop predicate (HC-2); a match is a placement (move to the ledger), never a
  3914	         drop — the source stays in the pool + bibliography + disclosure.
  3915	      3. A confirmed-OFF judged label (``topic_offtopic_demoted`` True or a demoted/escalated_demoted
  3916	         ``content_relevance_label``) => ledger.
  3917	      4. A JUDGED numeric ``selection_relevance`` below the floor => ledger (placement, not a drop).
  3918	      5. NO judgment => fall back to lexical question-term overlap (``_is_offtopic_for_placement``).
  3919	    PURE read of already-computed state; the faithfulness engine is untouched."""
  3920	    label = ""
  3921	    if isinstance(row, dict):
  3922	        label = str(row.get("content_relevance_label", "") or "").strip().lower()
  3923	    if label in _POSITIVE_RELEVANCE_LABELS:
  3924	        return False  # judged relevant => ALWAYS body (positive-relevance-first; never buried)
  3925	    text = _ledger_row_text(row)
  3926	    if is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(text) or _contains_f2_placement_furniture(text):
  3927	        return True  # furniture => ledger (placement, never a drop; F2 vocab never feeds a drop seam)
  3928	    if not isinstance(row, dict):
  3929	        return False
  3930	    if row.get("topic_offtopic_demoted") is True or label in _CONFIRMED_OFFTOPIC_LABELS:
  3931	        return True
  3932	    rel = _row_relevance(row)
  3933	    if rel is not None:
  3934	        return rel < relevance_floor  # judged below-floor => ledger (placement)
  3935	    # Unjudged: lexical off-topic => ledger.
  3936	    if _is_offtopic_for_placement(text, question_terms):
  3937	        return True
  3938	    # I-deepfix-006 E (#1376): an UNJUDGED marketing-only preamble (no finding signal — TRU/AACSB) is
  3939	    # DEMOTED to the ledger (kept at weight, never a drop). A real judge (rules 1/4) always wins first.
  3940	    if _row_is_marketing_only_preamble(text):
  3941	        return True
  3942	    return False
  3943	
  3944	
  3945	def partition_body_and_low_relevance_ledger(
  3946	    rows: Any, *, research_question: str = ""
  3947	) -> "tuple[list[Any], list[Any]]":
  3948	    """Split ordered ``rows`` into ``(body, ledger)`` by JUDGED weight/relevance then FURNITURE/off-
  3949	    topic, ordering EACH partition by ``weight * relevance`` DESC. §-1.3 PLACEMENT, NEVER a drop:
  3950	
  3951	      * ``body``   — rows kept in the report's carry-up prose (on-topic, at/above judged floor).
  3952	      * ``ledger`` — rows MOVED BELOW the appendix boundary into the "Low-relevance evidence (kept at
  3953	        weight)" section: furniture, confirmed-off-topic, judged-below-floor, or (unjudged) lexically
  3954	        off-topic. STILL present in the pool, bibliography, and disclosure — nothing is dropped.
  3955	
  3956	    CONSERVATION (asserted by the caller's test): ``body`` and ``ledger`` are disjoint and their union
  3957	    equals ``rows`` (deduped by identity of order) — no row vanishes, none is duplicated. When the
  3958	    kill-switch is OFF, every row stays in ``body`` (byte-identical). PURE; no faithfulness touch.
  3959	
  3960	    SCOPE (F2 gate iter-3): this row-list form is the general/reusable variant the unit tests exercise.
  3961	    The pipeline's raw carry-up surfaces are all ev-id ORDERED (weight order the render relies on), so
  3962	    the SHIPPED production entry is the order-preserving ``partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger`` —
  3963	    which shares the SAME per-row ``_row_routes_to_ledger`` verdict as this function."""
  3964	    row_list = list(rows or [])
  3965	    if not low_relevance_ledger_enabled() or not row_list:
  3966	        return row_list, []
  3967	    q_terms = _placement_topic_terms(research_question)
  3968	    floor = _ledger_relevance_floor()
  3969	    body: list[Any] = []
  3970	    ledger: list[Any] = []
  3971	    for row in row_list:
  3972	        (ledger if _row_routes_to_ledger(row, q_terms, floor) else body).append(row)
  3973	
  3974	    def _order(partition: list[Any]) -> list[Any]:
  3975	        # Stable weight*relevance DESC (a demotion order, never a filter). Index tiebreak preserves the
  3976	        # caller's incoming order within an equal-key group so the sort is deterministic.
  3977	        indexed = list(enumerate(partition))
  3978	        indexed.sort(
  3979	            key=lambda pair: (
  3980	                -(lambda wr: wr[0] * wr[1])(_ledger_weight_relevance_key(pair[1])),
  3981	                pair[0],
  3982	            )
  3983	        )
  3984	        return [row for _, row in indexed]
  3985	
  3986	    return _order(body), _order(ledger)
  3987	
  3988	
  3989	def partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger(
  3990	    ev_ids: Any, evidence_pool: Any, *, research_question: str = ""
  3991	) -> "tuple[list[str], list[str]]":
  3992	    """Order-PRESERVING split of the ordered Evidence-base ``ev_ids`` into ``(body, ledger)`` using the
  3993	    same per-row body/ledger verdict as ``partition_body_and_low_relevance_ledger``.
  3994	
  3995	    The incoming order (already weight*relevance from ``select_unbound_supports_by_weight``) is
  3996	    PRESERVED within each partition — the render (``build_evidence_base_section``) relies on that
  3997	    order, so this NEVER re-sorts. A ledger id is FURNITURE / confirmed-off-topic / judged-below-floor
  3998	    / (unjudged) lexically off-topic — it is MOVED BELOW the appendix boundary into the labelled
  3999	    "Low-relevance evidence (kept at weight)" section, and STAYS in the pool + bibliography + disclosure
  4000	    (§-1.3 PLACEMENT, never a drop). A pool-absent id stays in ``body`` (the render skips it exactly as
  4001	    before — no placement change for a non-resolvable id). Conservation: ``body`` + ``ledger`` equals
  4002	    the de-duplicated non-empty input. OFF (``PG_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER=0``) => ``(list(ev_ids), [])``."""
  4003	    # HC-7 (Codex F2 iter-1 P2): the OFF check is FIRST, before any dedup / empty-strip, so a
  4004	    # PG_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER=0 run feeds the body section the ORIGINAL ids untouched — strictly
  4005	    # byte-identical to legacy even when duplicate / empty ids are present in the input.
  4006	    #
  4007	    # F2 gate iter-6 (Codex NOVEL P0 — decoupled-flag placement-becomes-DROP): the ledger partition is
  4008	    # RENDERED only through ``build_evidence_base_section`` — BOTH the Evidence base body AND the ledger
  4009	    # section are gated internally by ``PG_BREADTH_EVIDENCE_BASE_SECTION``. If that flag is OFF the ledger
  4010	    # section CANNOT render, so routing rows into it while the CWF body-feed (multi_section_generator)
  4011	    # consumes only the body partition would make those rows vanish from the report prose AND the
  4012	    # bibliography — a §-1.3 DROP. COUPLE the split to the render gate: when the Evidence base surface
  4013	    # cannot render, the split returns ``(full-surface, [])`` so every row stays in the body order (fed
  4014	    # to CWF), the ledger is empty, and PG_BREADTH_EVIDENCE_BASE_SECTION=0 stays byte-identical to legacy
  4015	    # (its documented kill-switch contract). The move-half NEVER fires without the place-half.
  4016	    if not low_relevance_ledger_enabled() or not evidence_base_section_enabled():
  4017	        return list(ev_ids or []), []
  4018	    ids: list[str] = []
  4019	    seen: set[str] = set()
  4020	    for e in (ev_ids or []):
  4021	        e = str(e or "")
  4022	        if e and e not in seen:
  4023	            seen.add(e)
  4024	            ids.append(e)
  4025	    if not ids:
  4026	        return list(ev_ids or []), []
  4027	    pool = evidence_pool or {}
  4028	    q_terms = _placement_topic_terms(research_question)
  4029	    floor = _ledger_relevance_floor()
  4030	    body: list[str] = []
  4031	    ledger: list[str] = []
  4032	    for eid in ids:
  4033	        row = pool.get(eid)
  4034	        if not isinstance(row, dict):
  4035	            body.append(eid)  # pool-absent => leave in body; the render skips it as before (no change)
  4036	            continue
  4037	        (ledger if _row_routes_to_ledger(row, q_terms, floor) else body).append(eid)
  4038	    return body, ledger
  4039	
  4040	
  4041	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  4042	# I-wire-012 (#1326) — FAIL-LOUD chrome-as-claim CANARY on the SHIPPED report.
  4043	#
  4044	# A render-integrity tripwire: it measures what FRACTION of the report's CLAIM bullets
  4045	# are chrome (page furniture that rendered as a finding) and, in ``enforce`` mode above
  4046	# a floor, REFUSES to ship — so a chrome regression can NOT ship as
  4047	# ``released_with_disclosed_gaps``. It NEVER promotes a unit and NEVER touches a
  4048	# faithfulness verdict. Modes (LAW VI, default-safe):
  4049	#   off     — explicit opt-out: no telemetry, no enforce.
  4050	#   warn    — emit telemetry to the manifest; never fails the run.
  4051	#   enforce — DEFAULT (I-wire-013 #1327): emit telemetry AND fail the run (status flip) when rate > floor.
  4052	_RENDER_CANARY_MODE_ENV = "PG_RENDER_CHROME_CANARY"
  4053	_RENDER_CANARY_FLOOR_ENV = "PG_RENDER_CHROME_CANARY_FLOOR"
  4054	_DEFAULT_RENDER_CANARY_FLOOR = 0.05
  4055	_RENDER_CANARY_MODES = ("off", "warn", "enforce")
  4056	_DEFAULT_RENDER_CANARY_MODE = "enforce"
  4057	
  4058	# A TOP-LEVEL report bullet (no leading indent) = a claim surface (Key-Findings, the
  4059	# per-claim corroboration header, a finding bullet). Indented ``  - SUPPORT:`` /
  4060	# ``  - GROUNDED-BUT-WEAK`` sub-bullets (source URLs, not claims) and numbered
  4061	# bibliography lines ("1. Title") are deliberately EXCLUDED so the rate measures
  4062	# chrome-as-CLAIM, not chrome-as-source-locator.
  4063	_TOP_LEVEL_BULLET_RE = re.compile(r"^-\s+(.*\S)\s*$")
  4064	_BOLD_MARKER_RE = re.compile(r"\*\*")
  4065	
  4066	
  4067	def render_chrome_canary_mode() -> str:
  4068	    """Canary mode from ``PG_RENDER_CHROME_CANARY`` (off|warn|enforce); default ``enforce``
  4069	    (I-wire-013 #1327 — the tripwire enforces by default, not telemetry-only). Fail-loud on an
  4070	    UNRECOGNIZED value (LAW II — no silent guessed fallback), mirroring ``render_chrome_canary_floor``.
  4071	    ``off`` is the explicit opt-out (telemetry suppressed by the caller; verdict never trips)."""
  4072	    raw = os.environ.get(_RENDER_CANARY_MODE_ENV)
  4073	    if raw is None or not raw.strip():
  4074	        return _DEFAULT_RENDER_CANARY_MODE
  4075	    mode = raw.strip().lower()
  4076	    if mode not in _RENDER_CANARY_MODES:
  4077	        raise ValueError(
  4078	            f"{_RENDER_CANARY_MODE_ENV}={raw!r} is not a valid chrome-canary mode "
  4079	            f"(expected one of {_RENDER_CANARY_MODES})"
  4080	        )
  4081	    return mode
  4082	
  4083	
  4084	def render_chrome_canary_floor() -> float:
  4085	    """Chrome-as-claim rate floor from ``PG_RENDER_CHROME_CANARY_FLOOR`` (default 0.05).
  4086	    Fail-loud on a non-float (LAW II — no silent guessed fallback); clamped to [0, 1]."""
  4087	    raw = os.environ.get(_RENDER_CANARY_FLOOR_ENV)
  4088	    if raw is None or not raw.strip():
  4089	        return _DEFAULT_RENDER_CANARY_FLOOR
  4090	    try:
  4091	        val = float(raw.strip())
  4092	    except (TypeError, ValueError) as exc:
  4093	        raise ValueError(
  4094	            f"{_RENDER_CANARY_FLOOR_ENV}={raw!r} is not a float (chrome-as-claim rate floor)"
  4095	        ) from exc
  4096	    return min(1.0, max(0.0, val))
  4097	
  4098	
  4099	def _report_claim_bullets(report_text: str) -> list[str]:
  4100	    """The report's TOP-LEVEL claim bullets, bold markers stripped (PURE)."""
  4101	    out: list[str] = []
  4102	    for line in (report_text or "").split("\n"):
  4103	        m = _TOP_LEVEL_BULLET_RE.match(line)
  4104	        if not m:
  4105	            continue
  4106	        out.append(_BOLD_MARKER_RE.sub("", m.group(1)).strip())
  4107	    return out
  4108	
  4109	
  4110	# I-deepfix-001 WS-7 (D3): the chrome canary was BLIND to prose — it scored only top-level claim BULLETS
  4111	# (_report_claim_bullets), so an in-prose chrome leak (a leading bare section-header word, an in-text
  4112	# "(1, 2)" ref marker, a truncated "(2017)" subject) shipped without tripping the canary (drb_72: 0/33
  4113	# bullets flagged while prose leaked). This adds the report's claim-bearing PROSE units to the canary
  4114	# DENOMINATOR, screened with the SAME shared predicate, so a prose leak now trips the canary fail-closed.
  4115	# MEASUREMENT ONLY — the canary computes a rate/verdict; it NEVER drops or edits a rendered unit (that is
  4116	# the render seam's job). Default-ON PG_RENDER_CHROME_CANARY_PROSE; OFF => bullets-only => byte-identical.
  4117	_RENDER_CANARY_PROSE_ENV = "PG_RENDER_CHROME_CANARY_PROSE"
  4118	_PROSE_UNIT_MIN_CHARS = 40
  4119	
  4120	
  4121	def _render_canary_prose_enabled() -> bool:
  4122	    return os.environ.get(_RENDER_CANARY_PROSE_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "no", "off")
  4123	
  4124	
  4125	def _report_prose_units(report_text: str) -> list[str]:
  4126	    """The report's claim-bearing PROSE units (substantial non-bullet, non-header paragraph lines),
  4127	    EXCLUDING scaffolding sections (Bibliography / Methods / disclosures / Source corroboration / the H1
  4128	    question echo) whose legitimate DOIs/URLs are not chrome. PURE. These are the units the chrome canary
  4129	    was blind to (it scored only top-level bullets)."""
  4130	    out: list[str] = []
  4131	    in_scaffold = False
  4132	    for line in (report_text or "").split("\n"):
  4133	        s = line.strip()
  4134	        if not s:
  4135	            continue
  4136	        hdr = _SECTION_HEADER_RE.match(line)
  4137	        if hdr:
  4138	            title = hdr.group(2).strip().lower()
  4139	            in_scaffold = any(title.startswith(t) for t in _SCAFFOLDING_SECTION_TITLES)
  4140	            continue
  4141	        if in_scaffold:
  4142	            continue
  4143	        if _TOP_LEVEL_BULLET_RE.match(line) or _LEADING_BULLET_RE.match(line):
  4144	            continue  # bullets are already scored by _report_claim_bullets
  4145	        if len(s) >= _PROSE_UNIT_MIN_CHARS:
  4146	            out.append(_BOLD_MARKER_RE.sub("", s).strip())
  4147	    return out
  4148	
  4149	
  4150	def evaluate_render_chrome_canary(report_text: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
  4151	    """Compute the chrome-as-claim rate over the SHIPPED report's claim bullets AND prose units, and the
  4152	    canary verdict. PURE (no I/O). ``verdict='fail'`` ONLY in ``enforce`` mode when the rate exceeds the
  4153	    floor and there is at least one claim unit — so the caller can flip the run status. In ``warn``/``off``
  4154	    the verdict is always ``pass`` (telemetry only). Each chrome unit is screened with the SAME shared
  4155	    predicate every composer uses (chrome + truncation), so the canary and the screens can never disagree.
  4156	    WS-7 (D3): prose units are added to the denominator (default-ON PG_RENDER_CHROME_CANARY_PROSE) so an
  4157	    in-prose chrome leak trips the canary — MEASUREMENT ONLY, no rendered unit is dropped or edited."""
  4158	    bullets = _report_claim_bullets(report_text)
  4159	    units = list(bullets)
  4160	    prose_units = 0
  4161	    if _render_canary_prose_enabled():
  4162	        prose = _report_prose_units(report_text)
  4163	        prose_units = len(prose)
  4164	        units = units + prose
  4165	    chrome = [b for b in units if is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(b)]
  4166	    total = len(units)
  4167	    n_chrome = len(chrome)
  4168	    rate = (n_chrome / total) if total else 0.0
  4169	    floor = render_chrome_canary_floor()
  4170	    mode = render_chrome_canary_mode()
  4171	    tripped = bool(total and mode == "enforce" and rate > floor)
  4172	    return {
  4173	        "mode": mode,
  4174	        "floor": floor,
  4175	        # WS-7 (D3): denominator now = bullets + prose units. total_claim_bullets kept for back-compat
  4176	        # consumers (= total scored units); total_claim_units + prose_units_scored are the explicit names.
  4177	        "total_claim_bullets": total,
  4178	        "total_claim_units": total,
  4179	        "prose_units_scored": prose_units,
  4180	        "chrome_claim_bullets": n_chrome,
  4181	        "chrome_as_claim_rate": round(rate, 4),
  4182	        "verdict": "fail" if tripped else "pass",
  4183	        "examples": [b[:120] for b in chrome[:5]],
  4184	    }
  4185	
  4186	
  4187	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  4188	# I-wire-013 (#1327) iter-3a — RENDER-SEAM CHOKEPOINT.
  4189	#
  4190	# ONE sanitization pass over EVERY claim-bearing unit of the FINAL assembled report (Abstract,
  4191	# Key-Findings bullets, every ``###`` section body INCLUDING multi_section_generator output, the
  4192	# Corroborated Weighted Findings citation-split blob, the Conclusion), dropping/repairing chrome +
  4193	# truncated units with the now-unblinded predicate. This is the single seam that screens the
  4194	# currently-unscreened multi_section_generator output (0 screen calls today). It runs AFTER every
  4195	# composer + the header-sanity screen and BEFORE the chrome canary, so the canary reads the cleaned
  4196	# artifact and a residual leak still trips it fail-closed.
  4197	#
  4198	# FAITHFULNESS (FROZEN engine): RENDER hygiene only — it SUPPRESSES a page-furniture / truncated
  4199	# unit, NEVER promotes one and NEVER touches a strict_verify / NLI / 4-role / span-grounding verdict.
  4200	# Page furniture is not a corroborating source, so suppressing it STRENGTHENS faithfulness.
  4201	#
  4202	# OVER-STRIP SAFE (the drop-path law "over-strip deletes a real finding, worse than a leak"):
  4203	#   * Per-``[N]``-unit granularity — a flagged citation unit is dropped WITH its own trailing marker
  4204	#     (marker-paired, so a kept finding never loses its citation and a dropped chrome unit never
  4205	#     orphans a marker). The 4005-char Corroborated-Weighted-Findings blob keeps every real finding;
  4206	#     only its chrome sub-units drop.
  4207	#   * Scaffolding sections (Bibliography / Methods / disclosures / Reliability / Source corroboration
  4208	#     / the H1 question echo) are EXCLUDED — their legitimate DOIs/URLs are not chrome.
  4209	#   * A unit carrying SUBSTANTIAL real prose plus a glued inline ``#`` header is REPAIRED (cut at the
  4210	#     header, prefix kept) — the remainder is dropped only when it independently re-tests as chrome,
  4211	#     so a real "Limitations: … most extreme.## Analytical synthesis …" paragraph is never lost.
  4212	
  4213	# LAW VI: env-overridable, default ON (kill-switch ``PG_RENDER_SEAM_SANITIZE=0`` => no-op pass-through).
  4214	_RENDER_SEAM_SANITIZE_ENV = "PG_RENDER_SEAM_SANITIZE"
  4215	# I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-D: drop a bullet that carries NO claim text — only the list marker and/or
  4216	# orphan citation markers ("- ", "- [12]"). Such a bullet renders as an empty dash or a bare "[12]".
  4217	# Default-ON (``PG_CWF_EMPTY_BULLET_DROP``); OFF => byte-identical pass-through. SUPPRESS-ONLY: the
  4218	# cited evidence is untouched (it still appears wherever a real claim carries it).
  4219	_ENV_EMPTY_BULLET_DROP = "PG_CWF_EMPTY_BULLET_DROP"  # default ON
  4220	_EMPTY_BULLET_RE = re.compile(r"^\s*[-*]\s*(?:\[[^\]]+\]\s*)*$")
  4221	
  4222	
  4223	def empty_bullet_drop_enabled() -> bool:
  4224	    """Kill-switch ``PG_CWF_EMPTY_BULLET_DROP`` (default ON). OFF => an empty / marker-only bullet is
  4225	    left byte-identical (no drop)."""
  4226	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1369) FIX 4 — default-ON semantics: UNSET and EMPTY-STRING
  4227	    # are both ON; disabled ONLY by an explicit OFF token (see issn_chrome_gate).
  4228	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_EMPTY_BULLET_DROP, "1").strip().lower() not in (
  4229	        "0", "false", "no", "off",
  4230	    )
  4231	# LAW VI: the corpus known-word floor (a word must occur >= this many times across the run's fetched
  4232	# source text to count as "known" for the truncation allowlist). Mirrors the detector default.
  4233	_RENDER_SEAM_KNOWN_WORD_FLOOR_ENV = "PG_RENDER_SEAM_KNOWN_WORD_FLOOR"
  4234	_DEFAULT_KNOWN_WORD_FLOOR = 5
  4235	# A unit needs at least this many real-prose characters before a glued inline header in it is
  4236	# REPAIRED (prefix kept) rather than the whole unit dropped — below it the unit is treated as junk.
  4237	_MIN_REPAIR_PREFIX_CHARS = 40
  4238	# Section headers that are pipeline SCAFFOLDING, not carried-up source prose (no body units are
  4239	# screened under them; their legitimate DOIs/URLs must not be chrome-flagged). Matched against the
  4240	# header TITLE's leading text. Mirrors the detector's _SCAFFOLDING_TITLES.
  4241	_SCAFFOLDING_SECTION_TITLES = (
  4242	    "reliability header", "methods", "capability disclosures", "contradiction disclosures",
  4243	    "bibliography", "source corroboration", "evidence-support disclosure", "research report:",
  4244	)
  4245	_KNOWN_WORD_FIELDS = ("direct_quote", "statement", "title")
  4246	_SECTION_HEADER_RE = re.compile(r"^(#{1,6})\s+(.*\S)\s*$")
  4247	# I-wire-017 (#1339) FIX C1: the shallowest header LEVEL (``###`` = 3) that may be dropped when its
  4248	# sanitized body collapses to no claim-bearing prose. Top-level (``#``/``##``) report-structure
  4249	# headers are never dropped (a top-level empty section is left for the operator to see), only the
  4250	# per-claim ``###``-and-deeper content sections that the render seam emptied out.
  4251	_MIN_DROPPABLE_EMPTY_HEADER_LEVEL = 3
  4252	_LEADING_BULLET_RE = re.compile(r"^\s*-\s+")
  4253	# I-wire-013 (#1327) iter-3b D-P1-1: split on BOTH the numeric ``[N]`` marker AND the provenance
  4254	# ``[#ev:<id>:<start>-<end>]`` token (single capture group, inner alternation — keeps the
  4255	# text/marker pairing in ``_sanitize_report_line`` intact) so the render seam covers per-citation
  4256	# units on provenance-cited reports too, not just numeric-cited ones. ``[^\]]*`` captures the whole
  4257	# ``[#ev:...]`` body up to its closing bracket. Reports with only ``[N]`` are byte-identical (the
  4258	# numeric alternative is unchanged).
  4259	_CITATION_SPLIT_RE = re.compile(r"(\[\d+\]|\[#ev:[^\]]*\])")
  4260	_INLINE_HEADER_SPLIT_RE = re.compile(r"#{1,6}\s+[A-Za-z]")
  4261	
  4262	# I-deepfix-001 B6(a) (#1350): the per-claim "Source corroboration" section is a SCAFFOLDING title
  4263	# (byte-preserved above), so its worst chrome — a page-furniture scrape promoted to a basket HEADER
  4264	# bullet ("- **<masthead/ToC/affiliation>** — N verified independent source(s)") — never reaches the
  4265	# full containment predicate. This default-ON branch screens the corroboration section's HEADER
  4266	# bullets (only) through ``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable``; a chrome header has its CLAIM TEXT
  4267	# replaced by a neutral placeholder while the verified-source COUNT is preserved verbatim. LAW VI
  4268	# kill-switch ``PG_CORROBORATION_SANITIZE=0`` => the section stays byte-preserved (pre-B6 behaviour).
  4269	#
  4270	# §-1.3 CONSOLIDATE-don't-DROP (the dominant HARD RULE, outranks the spec's literal "screen each
  4271	# sub-bullet"): the ``- SUPPORT:`` / ``- GROUNDED-BUT-WEAK:`` / ``- CONTRADICTED:`` sub-bullets carry
  4272	# a SOURCE locator (url / evidence_id / tier / weight) — NOT a claim — so they are KEEP-ONLY here;
  4273	# screening them risks the chrome predicate's "bare DOI/URL row" leg dropping a corroborating source,
  4274	# which is a faithfulness violation. A divergence from the seam spec's literal wording, documented in
  4275	# the deepfix honest-gaps. Faithfulness-NEUTRAL: this only suppresses a chrome CLAIM string; it never
  4276	# drops a source, count, or verdict.
  4277	_CORROBORATION_SANITIZE_ENV = "PG_CORROBORATION_SANITIZE"
  4278	# The corroboration section's title prefix (lower-cased), matched to scope the branch to ONLY that
  4279	# section (Bibliography / Methods / Reliability stay truly byte-preserved).
  4280	_CORROBORATION_SECTION_PREFIX = "source corroboration"
  4281	# A corroboration HEADER bullet: a TOP-LEVEL ``- **<claim>** — <count> verified ...`` line. The claim
  4282	# text is the ``**bold**`` span; the ``— N verified independent source(s)`` suffix is the count. We
