  4283	# screen only the claim span and preserve the suffix verbatim. A sub-bullet (``  - SUPPORT: ...``) is
  4284	# INDENTED, so the no-leading-whitespace anchor here never matches it (sub-bullets are KEEP-ONLY).
  4285	_CORROBORATION_HEADER_RE = re.compile(r"^-\s+\*\*(?P<claim>.+?)\*\*(?P<suffix>\s*[—-].*)?$")
  4286	# The neutral placeholder a chrome basket header collapses to — the COUNT suffix still carries the
  4287	# corroboration; only the unrenderable page-furniture claim string is withheld.
  4288	_CORROBORATION_CHROME_PLACEHOLDER = "(claim text withheld — source page-furniture, not a finding)"
  4289	
  4290	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  4291	# I-deepfix-001 H1 (#1344) — SOURCE-INTERNAL inline reference-marker STRIP (REPAIR-first).
  4292	#
  4293	# THE GAP: a fetched source's OWN in-text citation apparatus ("... productivity rose (1, 2).",
  4294	# "... as shown (1; 3; 5).") is lifted verbatim into a verified span and rendered as a claim,
  4295	# leaving a bare "(1, 2)" numeral group in the body that is NOT one of the report's OWN ``[N]``
  4296	# provenance markers — it points at the SOURCE'S bibliography, not ours (dangling mis-attribution).
  4297	# This REPAIRS the sentence in place (removes only the leaked marker; the claim text survives) at
  4298	# the single render chokepoint, over every claim unit. High-precision: only a parenthetical whose
  4299	# WHOLE content is >=2 short integers separated by comma/semicolon is stripped, so a real
  4300	# parenthetical ("(1, 2, or 3 doses were compared)") is never touched (it has non-numeric words) and
  4301	# a solitary "(3)" is left alone (too ambiguous). The report's OWN citations use SQUARE brackets
  4302	# ``[N]`` / ``[#ev:...]`` and are never matched by this parenthesis rule. Faithfulness-NEUTRAL:
  4303	# render text only — no source, count, provenance token, or verdict is touched. LAW VI kill-switch
  4304	# ``PG_RENDER_SEAM_REF_STRIP=0`` => byte-identical (no strip).
  4305	_RENDER_SEAM_REF_STRIP_ENV = "PG_RENDER_SEAM_REF_STRIP"
  4306	# A leaked source-internal in-text citation: a parenthetical containing ONLY a comma/semicolon-
  4307	# separated run of >=2 integers (1-3 digits each), optional surrounding spaces. Matches "(1, 2)",
  4308	# "(1,2,3)", "(1; 2)", "( 10, 11 )". Does NOT match "(3)" (single), "(2020)" (4-digit year),
  4309	# "(1, 2 arms)" (has a word), or the report's square-bracket ``[N]`` markers.
  4310	_SOURCE_INTERNAL_REF_RE = re.compile(r"\(\s*\d{1,3}(?:\s*[,;]\s*\d{1,3})+\s*\)")
  4311	# A dangling space before sentence-final punctuation left by a stripped marker ("rose  .") is closed.
  4312	_PRE_PUNCT_SPACE_RE = re.compile(r"\s+([.!?,;:])")
  4313	_MULTISPACE_RE = re.compile(r"[ \t]{2,}")
  4314	
  4315	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  4316	# I-deepfix-001 H2 (#1344) — SPLIT the glued "Corroborated Weighted Findings" enrichment blob.
  4317	#
  4318	# THE GAP: the enrichment section body is composed by ``build_verified_span_draft`` (one verbatim
  4319	# span-unit per source-work, each already carrying ONLY its OWN work's ``[ev_id]`` markers) but
  4320	# ``_rewrite_draft_with_spans`` re-joins every unit with a SPACE, so the whole section renders as ONE
  4321	# thousands-of-character paragraph — many unrelated source findings concatenated, unreadable, and the
  4322	# reader cannot tell which ``[N]`` binds which finding. This splits that glued paragraph into ONE
  4323	# bullet per finding (sentence) at the render seam. Each finding keeps its OWN trailing ``[N]`` marker
  4324	# (the sentence splitter preserves ``.[N]``), so NO citation is re-attributed — the composer already
  4325	# guaranteed each unit carries only its own work's markers. Faithfulness-NEUTRAL: pure render reflow —
  4326	# no text, marker, source, or verdict is added/removed/re-bound. LAW VI kill-switch
  4327	# ``PG_CWF_SPLIT_FINDINGS=0`` => byte-identical (the glued paragraph is left as one line).
  4328	_CWF_SPLIT_FINDINGS_ENV = "PG_CWF_SPLIT_FINDINGS"
  4329	# The enrichment section TITLES (lower-cased prefixes) whose glued body is split into per-finding
  4330	# bullets. Mirrors ``_ENRICHMENT_TITLE`` / ``_ENRICHMENT_RESIDUAL_TITLE``.
  4331	_ENRICHMENT_SECTION_PREFIXES = (
  4332	    _ENRICHMENT_TITLE.lower(),
  4333	    _ENRICHMENT_RESIDUAL_TITLE.lower(),
  4334	)
  4335	
  4336	
  4337	def render_seam_ref_strip_enabled() -> bool:
  4338	    """True iff the default-ON H1 source-internal ref-marker strip is active (LAW VI kill-switch
  4339	    ``PG_RENDER_SEAM_REF_STRIP=0`` => no strip)."""
  4340	    return os.environ.get(_RENDER_SEAM_REF_STRIP_ENV, "1").strip().lower() in (
  4341	        "1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled",
  4342	    )
  4343	
  4344	
  4345	def cwf_split_findings_enabled() -> bool:
  4346	    """True iff the default-ON H2 CWF blob-split is active (LAW VI kill-switch
  4347	    ``PG_CWF_SPLIT_FINDINGS=0`` => the glued enrichment paragraph is left as one line)."""
  4348	    return os.environ.get(_CWF_SPLIT_FINDINGS_ENV, "1").strip().lower() in (
  4349	        "1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled",
  4350	    )
  4351	
  4352	
  4353	def strip_source_internal_refs(text: str) -> str:
  4354	    """H1 REPAIR: remove leaked source-internal in-text citation markers (bare "(1, 2)" numeral
  4355	    groups) from ``text`` and close the whitespace they leave, keeping the claim prose intact. PURE;
  4356	    faithfulness-neutral (the report's OWN ``[N]`` / ``[#ev:...]`` square-bracket markers are never
  4357	    matched). Returns ``text`` unchanged when the kill-switch is OFF or no marker is present."""
  4358	    if not text or not render_seam_ref_strip_enabled():
  4359	        return text
  4360	    if not _SOURCE_INTERNAL_REF_RE.search(text):
  4361	        return text
  4362	    # Preserve the line's ORIGINAL leading indentation (a nested markdown bullet that happens to
  4363	    # carry a leaked ref must not be de-indented into a top-level bullet).
  4364	    lead = text[: len(text) - len(text.lstrip())]
  4365	    out = _SOURCE_INTERNAL_REF_RE.sub("", text)
  4366	    out = _PRE_PUNCT_SPACE_RE.sub(r"\1", out)
  4367	    out = _MULTISPACE_RE.sub(" ", out)
  4368	    return lead + out.strip()
  4369	
  4370	
  4371	def _is_enrichment_section_title(title: str) -> bool:
  4372	    """True iff a header title names the flat/residual "Corroborated Weighted Findings" enrichment
  4373	    section whose glued body H2 splits into per-finding bullets. PURE."""
  4374	    low = title.strip().lower().lstrip("# ").strip()
  4375	    return any(low.startswith(p) for p in _ENRICHMENT_SECTION_PREFIXES)
  4376	
  4377	
  4378	def _split_enrichment_blob_line(
  4379	    line: str, known_words: "set[str] | frozenset[str] | None"
  4380	) -> "tuple[list[str], int]":
  4381	    """H2: split ONE glued enrichment body line (a space-joined run of ``sentence.[N]`` findings)
  4382	    into one Markdown bullet per finding, sanitizing each finding through the SAME per-line screen
  4383	    (``_sanitize_report_line``) so a chrome/truncated finding still drops. Returns
  4384	    ``(bullet_lines, dropped)``. A line that is a header, blank, already a bullet, or splits to a
  4385	    single sentence is returned as ``([sanitized_line], dropped)`` (no spurious bulletisation).
  4386	    PURE except the lazy sentence-splitter import; faithfulness-neutral."""
  4387	    stripped = line.strip()
  4388	    # Only split real glued prose. A blank / heading / existing bullet / short single clause is
  4389	    # sanitized-in-place, never bulletised (over-split is worse than a leak for a real single line).
  4390	    if not stripped or stripped.startswith(("#", "-", "*", "|", ">")):
  4391	        clean, dropped = _sanitize_report_line(line, known_words)
  4392	        # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-D: a bullet whose remainder — after removing the leading list
  4393	        # marker AND every citation marker — is empty carries NO claim ("- ", "- [12]"); drop it.
  4394	        if empty_bullet_drop_enabled() and clean.lstrip().startswith(("-", "*")):
  4395	            _residual = re.sub(r"^[-*]\s*", "", clean.strip())
  4396	            _residual = re.sub(r"\[[^\]]+\]", "", _residual)
  4397	            if not _residual.strip():
  4398	                return ([], dropped)
  4399	        return ([clean] if clean.strip() or not dropped else []), dropped
  4400	    try:
  4401	        from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (  # noqa: PLC0415
  4402	            split_into_sentences,
  4403	        )
  4404	        sentences = split_into_sentences(stripped)
  4405	    except Exception:  # pragma: no cover - provenance_generator is stable in-tree
  4406	        clean, dropped = _sanitize_report_line(line, known_words)
  4407	        return ([clean] if clean.strip() or not dropped else []), dropped
  4408	    if len(sentences) <= 1:
  4409	        clean, dropped = _sanitize_report_line(line, known_words)
  4410	        return ([clean] if clean.strip() or not dropped else []), dropped
  4411	    bullets: list[str] = []
  4412	    dropped = 0
  4413	    for sent in sentences:
  4414	        clean, drop = _sanitize_report_line(sent, known_words)
  4415	        dropped += drop
  4416	        clean = clean.strip()
  4417	        if clean:
  4418	            bullets.append(f"- {clean}")
  4419	    return bullets, dropped
  4420	
  4421	
  4422	def render_seam_sanitize_enabled() -> bool:
  4423	    """True iff the default-ON render-seam chokepoint is active (LAW VI kill-switch
  4424	    ``PG_RENDER_SEAM_SANITIZE=0`` => byte-identical pass-through)."""
  4425	    return os.environ.get(_RENDER_SEAM_SANITIZE_ENV, "1").strip().lower() in (
  4426	        "1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled",
  4427	    )
  4428	
  4429	
  4430	def corroboration_sanitize_enabled() -> bool:
  4431	    """True iff the default-ON B6(a) corroboration-header chrome screen is active (LAW VI kill-switch
  4432	    ``PG_CORROBORATION_SANITIZE=0`` => the corroboration section stays byte-preserved)."""
  4433	    return os.environ.get(_CORROBORATION_SANITIZE_ENV, "1").strip().lower() in (
  4434	        "1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled",
  4435	    )
  4436	
  4437	
  4438	def _is_corroboration_section_title(title: str) -> bool:
  4439	    """True iff a header title names the per-claim Source-corroboration rollup (B6(a) scope)."""
  4440	    return title.strip().lower().lstrip("# ").strip().startswith(_CORROBORATION_SECTION_PREFIX)
  4441	
  4442	
  4443	def _sanitize_corroboration_header(
  4444	    line: str, known_words: "set[str] | frozenset[str] | None"
  4445	) -> "tuple[str, int]":
  4446	    """B6(a): screen ONE corroboration HEADER bullet. A top-level ``- **<claim>** — N verified ...``
  4447	    whose CLAIM span is chrome (page furniture promoted to a basket header) has the claim string
  4448	    replaced by a neutral placeholder, preserving the verified-source COUNT suffix verbatim. Returns
  4449	    ``(clean_line, suppressed)`` where ``suppressed`` is 1 iff a chrome claim was withheld. A
  4450	    sub-bullet (indented) or a non-matching line is returned unchanged with 0. PURE; faithfulness-
  4451	    neutral (no source / count / verdict ever dropped)."""
  4452	    m = _CORROBORATION_HEADER_RE.match(line)
  4453	    if not m:
  4454	        return line, 0  # sub-bullet / blank / prose — KEEP-ONLY, untouched
  4455	    claim = m.group("claim").strip()
  4456	    suffix = m.group("suffix") or ""
  4457	    if claim and is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(claim, known_words=known_words):
  4458	        return f"- **{_CORROBORATION_CHROME_PLACEHOLDER}**{suffix}", 1
  4459	    return line, 0
  4460	
  4461	
  4462	def _known_word_floor() -> int:
  4463	    """The corpus known-word frequency floor (LAW VI). Fail-soft on a non-int / non-positive value
  4464	    to the detector default (the allowlist must never be silently emptied)."""
  4465	    raw = os.environ.get(_RENDER_SEAM_KNOWN_WORD_FLOOR_ENV, "").strip()
  4466	    if not raw:
  4467	        return _DEFAULT_KNOWN_WORD_FLOOR
  4468	    try:
  4469	        return max(1, int(raw))
  4470	    except ValueError:
  4471	        return _DEFAULT_KNOWN_WORD_FLOOR
  4472	
  4473	
  4474	def build_known_words_from_evidence(evidence_rows: Any, floor: int | None = None) -> set[str]:
  4475	    """The corpus-vocabulary allowlist (the truncation false-positive guard) built from the run's OWN
  4476	    fetched source text — every lowercase token occurring >= ``floor`` times across the evidence
  4477	    rows' ``direct_quote`` / ``statement`` / ``title`` fields. So a word the corpus genuinely uses
  4478	    ("labor", "Acemoglu", "computerisation") never false-flags as a span cut, while an absent
  4479	    fragment ("Resea", "hodology") does. Accepts a list of row dicts OR a ``{evidence_id: row}`` map
  4480	    (the in-memory ``ev_pool`` shape). PURE; returns an empty set when no source text is available
  4481	    (=> the caller's truncation leg is simply skipped, never a wrong drop)."""
  4482	    if floor is None:
  4483	        floor = _known_word_floor()
  4484	    if isinstance(evidence_rows, dict):
  4485	        rows: Any = evidence_rows.values()
  4486	    else:
  4487	        rows = evidence_rows or ()
  4488	    freq: Counter[str] = Counter()
  4489	    for row in rows:
  4490	        if not isinstance(row, dict):
  4491	            continue
  4492	        for field in _KNOWN_WORD_FIELDS:
  4493	            value = row.get(field)
  4494	            if isinstance(value, str) and value:
  4495	                for word in _BOUNDARY_VOCAB_RE.findall(value):
  4496	                    freq[word.lower()] += 1
  4497	    return {word for word, count in freq.items() if count >= floor}
  4498	
  4499	
  4500	# An alphabetic vocabulary token (mirrors the detector's _WORD_RE / key_findings._BOUNDARY_WORD_RE).
  4501	_BOUNDARY_VOCAB_RE = re.compile(r"[A-Za-z][A-Za-z'\-]*[A-Za-z]|[A-Za-z]")
  4502	
  4503	
  4504	def _unit_core_for_screen(text: str) -> str:
  4505	    """The screen-test text of a unit: leading ``- `` bullet marker and ``**bold**`` markers
  4506	    removed so the predicate judges the prose, not the markdown wrapper. PURE."""
  4507	    core = _LEADING_BULLET_RE.sub("", text.strip())
  4508	    return _BOLD_MARKER_RE.sub("", core).strip()
  4509	
  4510	
  4511	def _repair_glued_inline_header(text: str, known_words: "set[str] | frozenset[str] | None") -> "str | None":
  4512	    """If ``text`` is substantial real prose with a glued inline ``#`` header welded mid-unit, return
  4513	    the kept prefix (the header + remainder dropped) — but ONLY when the remainder independently
  4514	    re-tests as chrome, so a real paragraph is never over-stripped. Returns ``None`` when no
  4515	    repair applies (the caller then drops the whole unit)."""
  4516	    m = _INLINE_HEADER_SPLIT_RE.search(text)
  4517	    if not m or m.start() < _MIN_REPAIR_PREFIX_CHARS:
  4518	        return None
  4519	    prefix = text[:m.start()].rstrip()
  4520	    remainder = text[m.start():]
  4521	    prefix_core = _unit_core_for_screen(prefix)
  4522	    # Keep the prefix only if it is itself clean prose AND the excised remainder is independently
  4523	    # chrome (over-strip guard: never drop a remainder that re-tests clean).
  4524	    if not prefix_core or is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(prefix_core, known_words=known_words):
  4525	        return None
  4526	    if not is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(_unit_core_for_screen(remainder), known_words=known_words):
  4527	        return None
  4528	    return prefix
  4529	
  4530	
  4531	def _sanitize_report_line(line: str, known_words: "set[str] | frozenset[str] | None") -> "tuple[str, int]":
  4532	    """Sanitize ONE claim-section body line: split it into per-``[N]`` citation units, drop each unit
  4533	    (with its own trailing marker) that is chrome or a corpus-grounded truncation cut, and repair a
  4534	    unit that is real prose with a glued inline header. Returns ``(clean_line, dropped_count)``. A
  4535	    marker-less unit that is the whole short line is dropped iff it is chrome (a standalone ToC /
  4536	    masthead line). PURE."""
  4537	    parts = _CITATION_SPLIT_RE.split(line)
  4538	    segments: list[tuple[str, str]] = []
  4539	    i = 0
  4540	    while i < len(parts):
  4541	        seg_text = parts[i]
  4542	        seg_marker = parts[i + 1] if i + 1 < len(parts) else ""
  4543	        segments.append((seg_text, seg_marker))
  4544	        i += 2
  4545	    kept: list[str] = []
  4546	    dropped = 0
  4547	    # I-wire-017 (#1339) FIX B: when a prose segment is dropped as chrome, the SAME claim's trailing
  4548	    # continuation citation markers ("prose[6][7][5]" splits into a prose seg + two marker-only segs)
  4549	    # would otherwise survive orphaned. Track the drop and suppress the contiguous marker-only run
  4550	    # that immediately follows it. A marker-only run after a KEPT segment stays (it belongs to that
  4551	    # kept claim). Withhold-only — the dropped markers' evidence is untouched.
  4552	    suppress_trailing_markers = False
  4553	    for seg_text, seg_marker in segments:
  4554	        if not seg_text.strip() and not seg_marker:
  4555	            continue
  4556	        # A marker-only continuation segment (no prose, just "[N]") inherits the fate of the prose
  4557	        # segment it continues: dropped if that prose segment was dropped, kept otherwise.
  4558	        if not seg_text.strip():
  4559	            if suppress_trailing_markers:
  4560	                dropped += 1
  4561	                continue
  4562	            kept.append(seg_text + seg_marker)
  4563	            continue
  4564	        core = _unit_core_for_screen(seg_text)
  4565	        if core and is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(core, known_words=known_words):
  4566	            repaired = _repair_glued_inline_header(seg_text, known_words)
  4567	            if repaired is not None:
  4568	                # Real-prose prefix kept WITH its citation marker (the kept finding stays cited);
  4569	                # only the glued-header remainder is excised. The prose survives, so its trailing
  4570	                # continuation markers are NOT orphaned — keep them.
  4571	                kept.append(repaired + seg_marker)
  4572	                dropped += 1
  4573	                suppress_trailing_markers = False
  4574	                continue
  4575	            dropped += 1
  4576	            suppress_trailing_markers = True  # orphan this dropped claim's continuation markers
  4577	            continue  # whole chrome unit + its marker dropped
  4578	        kept.append(seg_text + seg_marker)
  4579	        suppress_trailing_markers = False
  4580	    # I-deepfix-001 H1 (#1344): REPAIR-first strip of leaked source-internal in-text ref markers
  4581	    # ("(1, 2)") on the kept prose. No-op (byte-identical) when the kill-switch is OFF or the line
  4582	    # carries no such marker; never touches the report's OWN ``[N]`` / ``[#ev:...]`` square-bracket
  4583	    # markers (they are seg_marker parts, and the rule matches PARENTHESES only). Faithfulness-neutral.
  4584	    # I-deepfix-006 A/B/C (#1376): also excise fixed boilerplate furniture fragments + raw markup that
  4585	    # were welded INSIDE the kept prose. Suppress-only; byte-identical when both kill-switches are OFF.
  4586	    cleaned = strip_source_internal_refs("".join(kept))
  4587	    cleaned = strip_inline_furniture(cleaned)
  4588	    cleaned = strip_inline_markup(cleaned)
  4589	    return cleaned, dropped
  4590	
  4591	
  4592	def _is_scaffolding_section_title(title: str) -> bool:
  4593	    """True iff a header title names a pipeline SCAFFOLDING section (excluded from sanitization)."""
  4594	    low = title.strip().lower().lstrip("# ").strip()
  4595	    return any(low.startswith(s) for s in _SCAFFOLDING_SECTION_TITLES)
  4596	
  4597	
  4598	def _line_has_claim_prose(line: str) -> bool:
  4599	    """True iff ``line`` carries claim-bearing prose (not just blanks or bare ``[N]`` /
  4600	    ``[#ev:...]`` citation markers). Strips leading bullet / ``**bold**`` markers and ALL citation
  4601	    markers, then checks any real alphabetic content remains. I-wire-017 (#1339) FIX C1 helper: used
  4602	    to decide whether a sanitized section body has collapsed to orphaned markers only. PURE."""
  4603	    text_only = "".join(_CITATION_SPLIT_RE.split(line)[::2])  # even indices = non-marker text
  4604	    return bool(_unit_core_for_screen(text_only).strip())
  4605	
  4606	
  4607	def _immediate_parent_is_scaffolding(level: int, header_stack: "list[tuple[int, bool]]") -> bool:
  4608	    """True iff the NEAREST strictly-shallower open header (the immediate markdown parent) is a
  4609	    scaffolding header — e.g. ``### references`` whose parent is ``## Bibliography``. A non-scaffolding
  4610	    header at an intermediate depth BREAKS the chain (it becomes the new parent), so a content section
  4611	    under a non-scaffolding parent is NOT protected even if a far ancestor is the report's scaffolding
  4612	    ``# Research Report:`` title. ``header_stack`` holds ``(level, is_scaffolding)`` for the open
  4613	    ancestor headers, shallowest-first. PURE."""
  4614	    for anc_level, anc_scaffolding in reversed(header_stack):
  4615	        if anc_level < level:
  4616	            return anc_scaffolding
  4617	    return False
  4618	
  4619	
  4620	def _drop_empty_claim_sections(lines: "list[str]") -> "tuple[list[str], int]":
  4621	    """I-wire-017 (#1339) FIX C1 post-pass: drop a non-scaffolding ``###``-or-deeper section header
  4622	    whose body — after the line-level sanitization already ran — has NO claim-bearing prose left
  4623	    (only blank lines / bare orphaned citation markers). Such a section renders as a dangling header
  4624	    over "[6][7][5]"; withholding the empty header is suppress-only (the evidence is untouched).
  4625	
  4626	    A SCAFFOLDING header — by its own title OR by having a scaffolding IMMEDIATE parent
  4627	    (``### references`` under ``## Bibliography``) — is always preserved. Any top-level (``#``/``##``)
  4628	    header is also preserved (a top-level empty section is left for the operator). Returns
  4629	    ``(kept_lines, headers_dropped)``. PURE."""
  4630	    kept: list[str] = []
  4631	    headers_dropped = 0
  4632	    # Open ancestor headers as (level, is_scaffolding), shallowest-first; a header at depth d closes
  4633	    # every open ancestor at depth >= d before it is pushed.
  4634	    header_stack: list[tuple[int, bool]] = []
  4635	    i = 0
  4636	    n = len(lines)
  4637	    while i < n:
  4638	        header = _SECTION_HEADER_RE.match(lines[i])
  4639	        if not header:
  4640	            kept.append(lines[i])
  4641	            i += 1
  4642	            continue
  4643	        level = len(header.group(1))
  4644	        title = header.group(2)
  4645	        parent_scaffolding = _immediate_parent_is_scaffolding(level, header_stack)
  4646	        header_stack = [hs for hs in header_stack if hs[0] < level]
  4647	        own_scaffolding = _is_scaffolding_section_title(title)
  4648	        header_stack.append((level, own_scaffolding))
  4649	        if (
  4650	            level < _MIN_DROPPABLE_EMPTY_HEADER_LEVEL
  4651	            or own_scaffolding
  4652	            or parent_scaffolding
  4653	        ):
  4654	            kept.append(lines[i])
  4655	            i += 1
  4656	            continue
  4657	        # Collect this section's body up to (not including) the next header of ANY level.
  4658	        body_start = i + 1
  4659	        j = body_start
  4660	        while j < n and not _SECTION_HEADER_RE.match(lines[j]):
  4661	            j += 1
  4662	        body = lines[body_start:j]
  4663	        if any(_line_has_claim_prose(b) for b in body):
  4664	            kept.extend(lines[i:j])  # real content survives -> keep header + body verbatim
  4665	        else:
  4666	            headers_dropped += 1  # empty content section -> drop header + its marker-only body
  4667	        i = j
  4668	    return kept, headers_dropped
  4669	
  4670	
  4671	def sanitize_rendered_report(
  4672	    report_md: str, known_words: "set[str] | frozenset[str] | None" = None
  4673	) -> "tuple[str, int]":
  4674	    """THE render-seam chokepoint (I-wire-013 #1327). Run ONE sanitization pass over every
  4675	    claim-bearing unit of the assembled ``report_md``, dropping/repairing chrome + truncated units
  4676	    with the unblinded ``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` predicate. Returns
  4677	    ``(clean_report_md, units_removed)``.
  4678	
  4679	    Scaffolding sections (Bibliography / Methods / disclosures / Reliability / Source corroboration /
  4680	    the H1 question echo) are byte-preserved. A glued-chrome HEADER line ("## Dennis Zami …" welded
  4681	    onto a title) is dropped; a clean section header is preserved. Default-ON kill-switch
  4682	    ``PG_RENDER_SEAM_SANITIZE``; faithfulness-neutral (suppress-only). PURE."""
  4683	    if not report_md or not render_seam_sanitize_enabled():
  4684	        return report_md, 0
  4685	    out_lines: list[str] = []
  4686	    removed = 0
  4687	    in_scaffolding = False
  4688	    # I-deepfix-001 B6(a): tracked SEPARATELY from in_scaffolding. The corroboration section is
  4689	    # scaffolding (byte-preserved DOIs/URLs) EXCEPT its per-claim HEADER bullets, which carry a
  4690	    # claim string that can be page-furniture chrome. When in_corroboration is set and the B6(a)
  4691	    # screen is enabled, header bullets are screened; sub-bullets stay byte-preserved (KEEP-ONLY).
  4692	    in_corroboration = False
  4693	    corroboration_screen = corroboration_sanitize_enabled()
  4694	    # I-deepfix-001 H2 (#1344): tracked separately — inside the flat/residual "Corroborated Weighted
  4695	    # Findings" enrichment section, split the glued single-paragraph body into one bullet per finding.
  4696	    in_enrichment = False
  4697	    cwf_split = cwf_split_findings_enabled()
  4698	    for line in report_md.split("\n"):
  4699	        header = _SECTION_HEADER_RE.match(line)
  4700	        if header:
  4701	            title = header.group(2)
  4702	            in_scaffolding = _is_scaffolding_section_title(title)
  4703	            in_corroboration = _is_corroboration_section_title(title)
  4704	            in_enrichment = _is_enrichment_section_title(title)
  4705	            # Screen a glued-chrome header by its TITLE (post-``#`` strip), but never a clean /
  4706	            # scaffolding header — dropping a real header would orphan its body. Gated by
  4707	            # ``render_chrome_screen_enabled()`` so this header path honours the same
  4708	            # ``PG_RENDER_CHROME_SCREEN=0`` kill-switch as ``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable``
  4709	            # (Codex P1 iter 1: the direct ``_contains_forensic_chrome`` call otherwise bypassed it).
  4710	            if (
  4711	                not in_scaffolding
  4712	                and render_chrome_screen_enabled()
  4713	                and _contains_forensic_chrome(title)
  4714	            ):
  4715	                removed += 1
  4716	                continue
  4717	            out_lines.append(line)
  4718	            continue
  4719	        if in_corroboration and corroboration_screen and line.strip():
  4720	            # B6(a): inside the corroboration rollup, screen ONLY the per-claim HEADER bullet's
  4721	            # claim string (sub-bullets / blanks pass through untouched via the (line, 0) branch).
  4722	            clean_line, suppressed = _sanitize_corroboration_header(line, known_words)
  4723	            removed += suppressed
  4724	            out_lines.append(clean_line)
  4725	            continue
  4726	        if in_scaffolding or not line.strip():
  4727	            out_lines.append(line)
  4728	            continue
  4729	        if in_enrichment and cwf_split:
  4730	            # H2: de-blob the enrichment section — split the glued ``sentence.[N] sentence.[N] ...``
  4731	            # paragraph into one bullet per finding, each sanitized through the SAME per-line screen
  4732	            # and keeping ONLY its own trailing ``[N]`` marker. Faithfulness-neutral render reflow.
  4733	            bullet_lines, dropped = _split_enrichment_blob_line(line, known_words)
  4734	            removed += dropped
  4735	            out_lines.extend(bullet_lines)
  4736	            continue
  4737	        clean_line, dropped = _sanitize_report_line(line, known_words)
  4738	        removed += dropped
  4739	        if clean_line.strip() or not dropped:
  4740	            out_lines.append(clean_line)
  4741	        # else: the line reduced entirely to chrome -> drop the now-empty line.
  4742	    # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-D belt: after the line-level pass, drop any surviving bullet that is
  4743	    # ONLY a list marker and/or orphan citation markers ("- ", "- [12]") — it carries no claim. A real
  4744	    # bibliography line ("1. Title") never matches (it is not a ``-``/``*`` bullet). SUPPRESS-ONLY.
  4745	    _empty_bullet_drop = empty_bullet_drop_enabled()
  4746	    if _empty_bullet_drop:
  4747	        _kept: list[str] = []
  4748	        _emptied = 0
  4749	        for _l in out_lines:
  4750	            if _EMPTY_BULLET_RE.match(_l):
  4751	                _emptied += 1
  4752	                continue
  4753	            _kept.append(_l)
  4754	        if _emptied:
  4755	            out_lines = _kept
  4756	            removed += _emptied
  4757	        logger.info("[activation] empty_bullet_drop: dropped=%d", _emptied)
  4758	    # I-wire-017 (#1339) FIX C1: after the line-level pass, drop any non-scaffolding ###-or-deeper
  4759	    # section whose body collapsed to no claim-bearing prose (blank / bare-marker only).
  4760	    out_lines, empty_headers_dropped = _drop_empty_claim_sections(out_lines)
  4761	    removed += empty_headers_dropped
  4762	    return "\n".join(out_lines), removed
  4763	
  4764	
  4765	def _make_junk_screen() -> Any:
  4766	    """Return THE shared render-side chrome+truncation predicate (I-wire-012 #1326).
  4767	
  4768	    Historically this returned a bespoke closure (boilerplate + web-chrome + CAPTCHA).
  4769	    It now returns ``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` so every consumer of this hub
  4770	    (``verified_compose._compose_junk_screen``, this module's own
  4771	    ``_substantive_units`` / ``build_verified_span_draft``) screens through the ONE
  4772	    predicate. The base screen still ALWAYS runs (so flag-OFF is byte-identical for
  4773	    these consumers); the new chrome categories are added when
  4774	    ``PG_RENDER_CHROME_SCREEN`` is ON (default)."""
  4775	    return is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable
  4776	
  4777	
  4778	def _emit_unit(unit: str, eids: Any) -> str:
  4779	    """Render one verbatim unit with its ``[ev_id]`` marker(s) INSIDE the sentence.
  4780	
  4781	    Strips trailing terminal punctuation then appends ``[eid]`` for each evidence_id
  4782	    (I-beatboth-011 #7 multi-citation: a same-work group emits ALL its grounding
  4783	    co-citation markers on the one unit) followed by ``.`` so every marker sits INSIDE
  4784	    the sentence unit and survives strict_verify's re-split (see ``_TERMINAL_PUNCT``).
  4785	    Accepts a single id (str) or an ordered list of ids; the order is preserved
  4786	    (representative first) and is deterministic.
  4787	    """
  4788	    if isinstance(eids, str):
  4789	        ids = [eids]
  4790	    else:
  4791	        ids = [str(e) for e in (eids or []) if str(e)]
  4792	    core = unit.rstrip()
  4793	    while core and core[-1] in _TERMINAL_PUNCT:
  4794	        core = core[:-1].rstrip()
  4795	    marker_str = "".join(f" [{eid}]" for eid in ids)
  4796	    return f"{core}{marker_str}."
  4797	
  4798	
  4799	def _substantive_units(direct_quote: str, *, is_junk: Any) -> list[str]:
  4800	    """The source's verbatim sentence-units that are citable claims, longest-first.
  4801	
  4802	    Splits with the SAME ``split_into_sentences`` strict_verify re-splits with, so
  4803	    each emitted unit is one gate unit. Keeps a unit only if it clears
  4804	    ``_MIN_UNIT_CHARS``, carries a real letter, is NOT boilerplate/chrome per the
  4805	    shared ``is_junk`` screen, and carries no ``[...]`` (which would be mis-read as a
  4806	    marker). Ordered longest-first so the per-source budget keeps the most
  4807	    content-bearing sentences (most likely the real finding).
  4808	    """
  4809	    from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (  # noqa: PLC0415
  4810	        split_into_sentences,
  4811	    )
  4812	
  4813	    max_chars = max_unit_chars()
  4814	    # I-deepfix-006 D (#1376): a nav/search SHELL source (dominated by empty-anchor links / search-query
  4815	    # URLs, no finding sentence — ev_716) is held OUT of the drafting INPUT. The source stays in the
  4816	    # pool + bibliography + disclosure; only its verbatim spans are withheld from drafting. Default-ON;
  4817	    # byte-identical when PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN=0 (``is_shell_source_quote`` returns False).
  4818	    if is_shell_source_quote(direct_quote):
  4819	        return []
  4820	    units: list[str] = []
  4821	    for raw_unit in split_into_sentences(direct_quote) or []:
  4822	        # I-beatboth-011 #4 (#1289): strip C0 control bytes (incl. a literal NUL) from
  4823	        # the unit BEFORE any length/screen check so a control byte can never reach the
  4824	        # render and the bound measures clean printable chars.
  4825	        unit = _strip_control_bytes(raw_unit or "").strip()
  4826	        # I-deepfix-006 A/B/C (#1376): excise fixed boilerplate furniture fragments + raw markup from
  4827	        # INSIDE the unit while keeping the surrounding clause. Suppress-only, faithfulness-neutral;
  4828	        # byte-identical when both kill-switches are OFF.
  4829	        unit = strip_inline_furniture(unit)
  4830	        unit = strip_inline_markup(unit)
  4831	        # I-deepfix-006 D (#1376): withhold a per-unit shell-narration sentence ("The span consists of …",
  4832	        # "repository collection link", "search query for all results") lifted into an otherwise-real source.
  4833	        if _shell_source_input_screen_enabled() and _is_shell_narration(unit):
  4834	            continue
  4835	        if len(unit) < _MIN_UNIT_CHARS:
  4836	            continue
  4837	        # I-beatboth-011 #4 (#1289): a unit longer than the render bound is structurally
  4838	        # a fetch-shell / raw-extraction blob (the 75K equation dump), never a clinical
  4839	        # sentence — DROP it. NOT a breadth cap (source count uncapped); NOT a verify
  4840	        # gate (strict_verify untouched). A real long quote is sentence-split upstream.
  4841	        if len(unit) > max_chars:
  4842	            continue
  4843	        if not any(ch.isalpha() for ch in unit):
  4844	            continue
  4845	        # `[...]`-shaped substrings inside a quote would be mis-read as markers
  4846	        # by _rewrite_draft_with_spans; a unit carrying one is skipped (rare; keeps
  4847	        # the marker contract unambiguous rather than risk a false token bind).
  4848	        if "[" in unit and "]" in unit:
  4849	            continue
  4850	        if is_junk(unit):
  4851	            continue
  4852	        units.append(unit)
  4853	    units.sort(key=len, reverse=True)
  4854	    return units
  4855	
  4856	
  4857	# I-beatboth-011 #7 (#1289) — SAME-WORK CONSOLIDATION identity (§-1.3 CONSOLIDATE-
  4858	# DON'T-DROP). Two unbound SUPPORTS members are the SAME WORK when they share a
  4859	# normalized DOI, else a folded title PLUS a corroborating discriminator. KEEP ALL
  4860	# their URLs as corroborating locators of the ONE work, but COUNT/PRESENT them as ONE
  4861	# source (multi-URL corroboration), never N independent sources. Identity ladder
  4862	# mirrors the existing ``_m51_canonical_identity`` convention (evidence_selector.py:
  4863	# 2781): DOI first, else title(+discriminator), else (fallback) the evidence_id itself
  4864	# so a member with neither stays its own distinct unit (never wrongly merged).
  4865	#
  4866	# I-beatboth-011 #4 (#1289) — P1 OVER-MERGE FIX (§-1.3: NEVER merge distinct works;
  4867	# under-merge is safe, over-merge corrupts breadth/attribution). The no-DOI branch
  4868	# MUST NOT merge on folded TITLE ALONE — two genuinely DIFFERENT works can share a
  4869	# normalized title and would be wrongly collapsed, losing distinct corroborators. So
  4870	# the no-DOI key requires the folded title PLUS the FIRST PRESENT corroborating
  4871	# discriminator the records share, in this fixed priority order: publication YEAR →
  4872	# first-author SURNAME → VENUE/journal → URL HOST. A priority-ordered composite (NOT
  4873	# pairwise OR / union-find, which is non-transitive and over-merges through chains) is
  4874	# a plain equality key, biased to UNDER-merge. Title-with-no-discriminator stays its
  4875	# own ev-id singleton (distinct). This key computation is the SHARED canonical contract
  4876	# with ``synthesis/finding_dedup.py`` and is duplicated BYTE-FOR-BYTE there (the
  4877	# no-new-source-file rule forbids a shared module).
  4878	_DOI_PREFIX_RE = re.compile(r"^\s*(?:doi\s*:?\s*|https?://(?:dx\.)?doi\.org/)", re.IGNORECASE)
  4879	_TITLE_NORMALIZE_RE = re.compile(r"[^a-z0-9]+")
  4880	_WHITESPACE_RUN_RE = re.compile(r"\s+")
  4881	# Publication-year validity bounds (SHARED with the selector's _row_year convention
  4882	# at evidence_selector.py:769-770 and finding_dedup._row_year). Outside => absent.
  4883	_MIN_YEAR = 1900
  4884	_MAX_YEAR = 2100
  4885	
  4886	
  4887	def _normalize_doi(raw: Any) -> str:
  4888	    """Normalized DOI for same-work grouping ('' when absent/unusable).
  4889	
  4890	    SHARED contract with ``finding_dedup._normalize_doi``: strip a leading
  4891	    ``doi:`` / ``https://doi.org/`` / ``http://dx.doi.org/`` prefix, lowercase,
  4892	    ``rstrip("/")``; a USABLE DOI starts with the ``10.`` registrant prefix.
  4893	    """
  4894	    doi = str(raw or "").strip()
  4895	    if not doi:
  4896	        return ""
  4897	    doi = _DOI_PREFIX_RE.sub("", doi).strip().lower().rstrip("/")
  4898	    # A usable DOI starts with the ``10.`` registrant prefix; anything else is noise.
  4899	    return doi if doi.startswith("10.") else ""
  4900	
  4901	
  4902	def _normalize_title(raw: Any) -> str:
  4903	    """Normalized title key for same-work grouping ('' when too short to be safe).
  4904	
  4905	    SHARED with ``finding_dedup._fold_title``: lowercase, collapse non-alphanumeric
  4906	    runs to a single space, strip; require >= 12 chars (a tiny/generic title is an
  4907	    over-merge risk).
  4908	    """
  4909	    title = str(raw or "").strip().lower()
  4910	    title = _TITLE_NORMALIZE_RE.sub(" ", title).strip()
  4911	    # Guard against an over-merge on a tiny/generic title: require real substance.
  4912	    return title if len(title) >= 12 else ""
  4913	
  4914	
  4915	def _record_title(ev: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  4916	    """The record's title across the schema aliases (``source_title`` is canonical;
  4917	    ``title`` / ``page_title`` / ``name`` are the validator-mapped variants).
  4918	
  4919	    SHARED precedence with ``finding_dedup._row_title`` so the two consolidators
  4920	    fold the SAME title field.
  4921	    """
  4922	    for key in ("source_title", "title", "page_title", "name"):
  4923	        value = ev.get(key)
  4924	        if value:
  4925	            return str(value)
  4926	    return ""
  4927	
  4928	
  4929	def _record_year(ev: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  4930	    """Publication year as a discriminator token ('' when absent/invalid).
  4931	
  4932	    Reads ``ev['year']`` else ``ev['metadata']['year']`` and validates [1900, 2100]
  4933	    — the SHARED convention with the selector's ``_row_year`` (evidence_selector.py:
  4934	    793-809) and ``finding_dedup._row_year``.
  4935	    """
  4936	    val = ev.get("year")
  4937	    if val is None:
  4938	        meta = ev.get("metadata")
  4939	        if isinstance(meta, dict):
  4940	            val = meta.get("year")
  4941	    if val is None:
  4942	        return ""
  4943	    try:
  4944	        year = int(val)
  4945	    except (TypeError, ValueError):
  4946	        return ""
  4947	    return str(year) if _MIN_YEAR <= year <= _MAX_YEAR else ""
  4948	
  4949	
  4950	def _first_author_surname(ev: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  4951	    """First-author surname (folded) as a discriminator token ('' when absent).
  4952	
  4953	    Records carry ``authors`` (a list, family-name-first, e.g. ``["Autor D", ...]``)
  4954	    or a singular ``author`` string. The surname is the FIRST whitespace token of the
  4955	    first author, lowercased + non-alphanumerics stripped. SHARED with
  4956	    ``finding_dedup._first_author_surname``.
  4957	    """
  4958	    raw = ev.get("authors")
  4959	    first = ""
  4960	    if isinstance(raw, (list, tuple)):
  4961	        for entry in raw:
  4962	            if entry and str(entry).strip():
  4963	                first = str(entry).strip()
  4964	                break
  4965	    elif raw:
  4966	        first = str(raw).strip()
  4967	    if not first:
  4968	        single = ev.get("author")
  4969	        if single and str(single).strip():
  4970	            first = str(single).strip()
  4971	    if not first:
  4972	        return ""
  4973	    surname = first.split()[0] if first.split() else ""
  4974	    surname = _TITLE_NORMALIZE_RE.sub("", surname.lower())
  4975	    return surname
  4976	
  4977	
  4978	def _record_venue(ev: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  4979	    """Venue/journal (folded) as a discriminator token ('' when absent).
  4980	
  4981	    Reads ``venue`` else ``journal``, lowercased with non-alphanumeric runs
  4982	    collapsed to a single space and trimmed. SHARED with ``finding_dedup._row_venue``.
  4983	    """
  4984	    raw = ev.get("venue") or ev.get("journal") or ""
  4985	    text = str(raw).strip().lower()
  4986	    if not text:
  4987	        return ""
  4988	    text = _TITLE_NORMALIZE_RE.sub(" ", text)
  4989	    return _WHITESPACE_RUN_RE.sub(" ", text).strip()
  4990	
  4991	
  4992	def _record_host(ev: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  4993	    """URL host (no leading ``www.``) as the WEAKEST discriminator token.
  4994	
  4995	    Same-work fetches usually span DIFFERENT hosts, so host merges almost nothing —
  4996	    it is last in the priority order purely as a safety net. SHARED with
  4997	    ``finding_dedup._row_host`` (which delegates to ``_host_of``); the host reduction
  4998	    here is inlined (no urllib import already present) but produces the SAME token.
  4999	    """
  5000	    from urllib.parse import urlparse  # noqa: PLC0415
  5001	
  5002	    url = str(ev.get("source_url", "") or ev.get("url", "") or "")
  5003	    if not url:
  5004	        return ""
  5005	    host = (urlparse(url).hostname or "").lower().strip()
  5006	    if host.startswith("www."):
  5007	        host = host[4:]
  5008	    return host
  5009	
  5010	
  5011	def _title_discriminator(ev: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  5012	    """The STRICT corroborating discriminator for the no-DOI title branch.
  5013	
  5014	    I-beatboth-011 #4 P2 hardening (#1289): the no-DOI key MUST be strong enough that
  5015	    two DISTINCT works sharing a title cannot merge on a single weak signal. A single
  5016	    weak signal alone (year-only or host-only) is NOT enough. The token requires the
  5017	    folded title PLUS either:
  5018	      * a STRONG discriminator (first-author surname and/or venue) — every present
  5019	        STRONG/year signal is folded in (year → author → venue, fixed order), so a
  5020	        differing year OR differing author OR differing venue yields a DIFFERENT token
  5021	        and the two works do NOT merge; OR
  5022	      * two INDEPENDENT WEAK signals (year AND host) when no strong signal is present.
  5023	
  5024	    HOST IS ENABLING-ONLY, NEVER BLOCKING. Same-work members are the same work fetched
  5025	    at DIFFERENT URLs, so they (almost) always differ on host (the ``_record_host``
  5026	    safety-net premise + §-1.3). Host therefore appears ONLY as the SECOND weak signal
  5027	    alongside year, and NEVER in the strong-path token — otherwise every legitimate
  5028	    same-work merge (which spans different hosts) would be blocked.
  5029	
  5030	    Returns '' when neither a strong signal nor (year AND host) is present, so the record
  5031	    stays a title-only singleton and is never merged on title alone. SHARED contract with
  5032	    ``finding_dedup._title_discriminator`` (byte-identical key string).
  5033	    """
  5034	    year = _record_year(ev)
  5035	    surname = _first_author_surname(ev)
  5036	    venue = _record_venue(ev)
  5037	    host = _record_host(ev)
  5038	    if surname or venue:
  5039	        parts: list[str] = []
  5040	        if year:
  5041	            parts.append("y:" + year)
  5042	        if surname:
  5043	            parts.append("a:" + surname)
  5044	        if venue:
  5045	            parts.append("v:" + venue)
  5046	        return "|".join(parts)
  5047	    if year and host:
  5048	        return "y:" + year + "|h:" + host
  5049	    return ""
  5050	
  5051	
  5052	def _samework_url_leg_on() -> bool:
  5053	    """Render-side mirror of ``finding_dedup._samework_url_leg_enabled`` — reads the SAME
  5054	    ``PG_SAMEWORK_URL_LEG`` env flag (default ON) so the two same-work consolidators are
  5055	    always in lockstep. OFF => the url leg is skipped and ``_work_identity`` is byte-identical
  5056	    to the prior DOI/title-only keying."""
  5057	    import os  # noqa: PLC0415
  5058	    return os.getenv("PG_SAMEWORK_URL_LEG", "1").strip().lower() not in (
  5059	        "0", "false", "no", "off", "",
  5060	    )
  5061	
  5062	
  5063	def _samework_url_norm(ev: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  5064	    """Byte-identical mirror of ``finding_dedup._normalize_source_url`` (GH I-deepfix-003
  5065	    #1374, Fable gate P1-C). scheme + lowercased host (leading ``www.`` stripped) + path
  5066	    (trailing ``/`` stripped); FRAGMENT dropped, QUERY KEPT (dropping it would over-merge
  5067	    identity-in-query works). Requires a NON-EMPTY path (a host-only URL is too coarse => "").
  5068	    A blank / unparseable URL returns "" so ``_work_identity`` falls through to DOI/title."""
  5069	    from urllib.parse import urlparse  # noqa: PLC0415
  5070	    raw = str(ev.get("source_url", "") or ev.get("url", "") or "").strip()
  5071	    if not raw:
  5072	        return ""
  5073	    parsed = urlparse(raw)
  5074	    host = (parsed.hostname or "").lower().strip()
  5075	    if host.startswith("www."):
  5076	        host = host[4:]
  5077	    path = (parsed.path or "").rstrip("/")
  5078	    if not path:
  5079	        return ""
  5080	    scheme = (parsed.scheme or "").lower()
  5081	    prefix = (scheme + "://" + host) if host else ""
  5082	    query = parsed.query
  5083	    return prefix + path + (("?" + query) if query else "")
  5084	
  5085	
  5086	def _work_identity(eid: str, ev: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  5087	    """Same-work group key for one member: DOI, else title(+discriminator), else its
  5088	    own ev_id.
  5089	
  5090	    I-beatboth-011 #4 (#1289): the no-DOI branch NEVER merges on folded title ALONE
  5091	    (two different works can share a title). It requires the folded title AND the
  5092	    FIRST present discriminator (year → first-author surname → venue → host).
  5093	    Title-with-no-discriminator falls through to the evidence_id (never a constant),
  5094	    so a member with neither a DOI nor (usable title + discriminator) stays its OWN
  5095	    distinct unit — consolidation can only MERGE genuine same-work duplicates, never
  5096	    collapse unrelated works. Matches ``finding_dedup._same_work_key``.
  5097	    """
  5098	    # STEP 4 render-parity (GH I-deepfix-003 #1374, Fable gate P1-C): FIRST url leg mirrors
  5099	    # finding_dedup._normalize_source_url behind the SAME PG_SAMEWORK_URL_LEG switch, so a
  5100	    # no-DOI / weak-title multi-chunk PDF collapses to ONE Evidence-base / CWF entry (not 18).
  5101	    if _samework_url_leg_on():
  5102	        _u = _samework_url_norm(ev)
  5103	        if _u:
  5104	            return f"url:{_u}"
  5105	    doi = _normalize_doi(ev.get("doi"))
  5106	    if doi:
  5107	        return f"doi:{doi}"
  5108	    title = _normalize_title(_record_title(ev))
  5109	    if title:
  5110	        discriminator = _title_discriminator(ev)
  5111	        if discriminator:
  5112	            return f"title:{title}|{discriminator}"
  5113	    return f"ev:{eid}"
  5114	
  5115	
  5116	def _member_quote(ev: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  5117	    """The member's render-safe direct quote (control bytes stripped)."""
  5118	    raw = (ev.get("direct_quote") or ev.get("statement") or "")
  5119	    return _strip_control_bytes(str(raw)).strip()
  5120	
  5121	
  5122	def build_verified_span_draft(
  5123	    ev_ids: Any, evidence_pool: Any, *, research_question: str = ""
  5124	) -> str:
  5125	    """Deterministic verbatim-span draft for the enrichment section (FIX K).
  5126	
  5127	    Emits, in the caller's relevance/weight order, up to ``spans_per_source()`` of each
  5128	    WORK's own verbatim sentence-units, each with its legacy ``[ev_id]`` marker placed
  5129	    INSIDE the sentence, so ``_rewrite_draft_with_spans`` binds each unit to its best
  5130	    in-quote span and ``strict_verify`` validates it.
  5131	
  5132	    I-beatboth-011 #4 (#1289) — RENDER SAFETY: every emitted span is control-byte
  5133	    sanitized (NO NUL / C0 bytes ever reach the report) and a unit exceeding the render
  5134	    char bound (a 75K raw-extraction blob) is dropped. A CAPTCHA / Cloudflare security
  5135	    stub member is dropped by the junk screen.
  5136	
  5137	    I-beatboth-011 #7 (#1289) — SAME-WORK CONSOLIDATION (§-1.3 CONSOLIDATE-DON'T-DROP):
  5138	    members that are the SAME WORK (same normalized DOI, else title) are grouped into
  5139	    ONE multi-citation unit-set — counted/presented as ONE source — instead of N. ALL
  5140	    the work's URLs are KEPT as corroborating locators: a corroborator's ``[ev_id]``
  5141	    marker is attached to a unit ONLY when that corroborator's OWN quote actually
  5142	    contains the emitted unit, so every emitted marker is span-grounded by construction
  5143	    (this NEVER changes which members verify — the representative would verify alone;
  5144	    corroborators only ADD already-grounding co-citations). A truncated-intro duplicate
  5145	    of the representative contributes its URL as a corroborator, not a separate source.
  5146	
  5147	    A source whose quote is boilerplate/chrome/CAPTCHA, pool-absent, or has no
  5148	    substantive unit contributes nothing. Returns the joined draft ("" => caller renders
  5149	    the existing gap stub, never a silent success). NO LLM, NO faithfulness-gate touch.
  5150	    """
  5151	    pool = evidence_pool or {}
  5152	    is_junk = _make_junk_screen()
  5153	    budget = spans_per_source()
  5154	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1344 SPAN-TOPICALITY): precision-safe per-span off-topic WITHHOLD
  5155	    # inputs (empty question OR flag OFF => empty term set => no span ever withheld =>
  5156	    # byte-identical). §-1.3 WITHHOLD-and-disclose per span; the source stays in the pool.
  5157	    span_question_terms = (
  5158	        _question_topic_terms(research_question)
  5159	        if offtopic_span_suppress_enabled()
  5160	        else frozenset()
  5161	    )
  5162	    span_min_content_words = _offtopic_span_min_content_words()
  5163	    span_min_local_terms = _offtopic_span_min_local_terms()
  5164	    # Corpus-wide on-topic vocabulary, computed ONCE (Codex-P1 iter-2 answer): the per-span
  5165	    # off-topic gate KEEPS any span sharing vocabulary with the whole corpus, so lower-level /
  5166	    # synonym / acronym on-topic spans are retained; only spans foreign to the ENTIRE corpus
  5167	    # are withheld. Empty when the gate is disabled (byte-identical no-op).
  5168	    span_corpus_terms = _corpus_topic_terms(pool) if span_question_terms else set()
  5169	
  5170	    # Group ev_ids into same-work buckets, PRESERVING the caller's relevance/weight
  5171	    # order: a work's bucket is keyed by its FIRST-seen member, so the highest-ordered
  5172	    # member of each work is the representative and the bucket order is the work order.
  5173	    work_order: list[str] = []
  5174	    work_members: dict[str, list[str]] = {}
  5175	    for ev_id in (ev_ids or []):
  5176	        eid = str(ev_id or "")
  5177	        if not eid:
  5178	            continue
  5179	        ev = pool.get(eid)
  5180	        if not isinstance(ev, dict):
  5181	            continue
  5182	        direct_quote = _member_quote(ev)
  5183	        # Drop CAPTCHA stubs / boilerplate at the WHOLE-member level up front.
  5184	        if not direct_quote or is_junk(direct_quote):
  5185	            continue
  5186	        key = _work_identity(eid, ev)
  5187	        if key not in work_members:
  5188	            work_members[key] = []
  5189	            work_order.append(key)
  5190	        work_members[key].append(eid)
  5191	
  5192	    parts: list[str] = []
  5193	    for key in work_order:
  5194	        member_eids = work_members[key]
  5195	        representative = member_eids[0]
  5196	        rep_ev = pool.get(representative)
  5197	        if not isinstance(rep_ev, dict):
  5198	            continue
  5199	        rep_quote = _member_quote(rep_ev)
  5200	        units = _substantive_units(rep_quote, is_junk=is_junk)
  5201	        # I-deepfix-001 (#1344 SPAN-TOPICALITY): WITHHOLD confidently-foreign spans of an
  5202	        # otherwise-on-topic source from citation (fail-open; source never dropped).
  5203	        units = _withhold_offtopic_spans(
  5204	            units, rep_ev, span_question_terms,
  5205	            span_min_content_words, span_min_local_terms,
  5206	            corpus_topic_terms=span_corpus_terms,
  5207	        )
  5208	        if not units:
  5209	            continue
  5210	        # Pre-compute each corroborator's sanitized quote ONCE for the contains-check.
  5211	        corroborator_quotes = [
  5212	            (m, _member_quote(pool[m]))
  5213	            for m in member_eids[1:]
  5214	            if isinstance(pool.get(m), dict)
  5215	        ]
  5216	        for unit in units[:budget]:
  5217	            # The representative ALWAYS grounds (its own quote contains the unit). Attach
  5218	            # a corroborator marker ONLY when that corroborator's own quote also contains
  5219	            # the unit — so every emitted marker is span-grounded and no member's verify
  5220	            # status changes. ALL same-work members retain their URL as a co-locator;
  5221	            # those whose fetch differs simply do not add a (would-fail) marker.
  5222	            markers = [representative]
  5223	            for m_eid, m_quote in corroborator_quotes:
  5224	                if unit in m_quote and m_eid not in markers:
  5225	                    markers.append(m_eid)
  5226	            parts.append(_emit_unit(unit, markers))
  5227	    return " ".join(parts)
  5228	
  5229	
  5230	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  5231	# I-deepfix-001 WS-3 (#1344) — NUMBERED "Evidence base" breadth surface.
  5232	#
  5233	# THE LEAK (drb_72 "12 of 88 cited"): the FULL ordered unbound-SUPPORTS surface from
  5234	# ``select_unbound_supports_by_weight`` is already UNCAPPED (weighted_enrichment.py:295,469,573),
  5235	# but nothing RENDERS it as a numbered reference block, so most span-verified sources never
  5236	# receive a ``[N]`` citation. This surfaces EVERY source that carries a surviving isolated-
  5237	# ``SUPPORTS`` span into ONE numbered "Evidence base" section: one numbered entry per distinct
  5238	# WORK (same-work CONSOLIDATION, §-1.3 — never N entries for one work), each entry = that work's
  5239	# OWN verbatim span unit(s) tagged with its ``[ev_id]`` marker(s) so the downstream bibliography
  5240	# numberer assigns each a real ``[N]``.
  5241	#
  5242	# §-1.3 — WEIGHT-and-CONSOLIDATE, never FILTER-and-CAP: this is SURFACING breadth (keep-all), NOT a
  5243	# cap / floor / thinner. The input ``ev_ids`` is already the uncapped ordered surface; this ONLY
  5244	# renders it. Faithfulness is UNTOUCHED — each emitted unit is a verbatim span carrying a legacy
  5245	# ``[ev_id]`` marker that flows through the UNCHANGED ``_rewrite_draft_with_spans`` -> ``strict_verify``
  5246	# exactly like every other section; a unit that cannot ground is dropped by that gate, never padded.
  5247	# The SAME render-safety screens as ``build_verified_span_draft`` apply (control-byte strip, junk
  5248	# screen, per-unit char bound, same-work consolidation). Default-ON;
  5249	# ``PG_BREADTH_EVIDENCE_BASE_SECTION=0`` => returns "" => no section => byte-identical legacy output.
  5250	_ENV_EVIDENCE_BASE_SECTION = "PG_BREADTH_EVIDENCE_BASE_SECTION"
  5251	_EVIDENCE_BASE_TITLE = "Evidence base"
  5252	
  5253	
  5254	def evidence_base_section_enabled() -> bool:
  5255	    """Kill-switch ``PG_BREADTH_EVIDENCE_BASE_SECTION`` (default ON). OFF => the numbered
  5256	    Evidence base section is not rendered (``build_evidence_base_section`` returns "") =>
  5257	    byte-identical legacy output."""
  5258	    return os.environ.get(_ENV_EVIDENCE_BASE_SECTION, "1").strip().lower() not in (
  5259	        "0", "false", "no", "off",
  5260	    )
  5261	
  5262	
  5263	def build_evidence_base_section(
  5264	    ev_ids: Any,
  5265	    evidence_pool: Any,
  5266	    *,
  5267	    start_index: int = 1,
  5268	    research_question: str = "",
  5269	) -> str:
  5270	    """Render the FULL ordered unbound-SUPPORTS surface as ONE numbered "Evidence base" markdown
  5271	    section so EVERY source with a surviving span gets a ``[N]`` citation.
  5272	
  5273	    ``ev_ids`` is the ordered surface from ``select_unbound_supports_by_weight`` (already uncapped —
  5274	    NO cap / floor / thinner is applied here). Members are CONSOLIDATED into same-work buckets
  5275	    (§-1.3 keep-all-count-once): one numbered entry per distinct work, in the caller's
  5276	    relevance/weight order, each carrying its verbatim span unit(s) + the ``[ev_id]`` marker(s) the
  5277	    downstream span-binder + ``strict_verify`` re-check.
  5278	
  5279	    Returns "" when the flag is OFF, ``ev_ids`` is empty, or no surfaced source yields a substantive
  5280	    verbatim unit (caller renders nothing — byte-identical). NO LLM; NO faithfulness-gate touch.
  5281	    """
  5282	    if not evidence_base_section_enabled():
  5283	        return ""
  5284	    ev_ids = list(ev_ids or [])
  5285	    if not ev_ids:
  5286	        return ""
  5287	    pool = evidence_pool or {}
  5288	    is_junk = _make_junk_screen()
  5289	    budget = spans_per_source()
  5290	    # I-deepfix-001 (#1344 SPAN-TOPICALITY): precision-safe per-span off-topic WITHHOLD
  5291	    # inputs (empty question OR flag OFF => empty term set => no span ever withheld).
  5292	    span_question_terms = (
  5293	        _question_topic_terms(research_question)
  5294	        if offtopic_span_suppress_enabled()
  5295	        else frozenset()
  5296	    )
  5297	    span_min_content_words = _offtopic_span_min_content_words()
  5298	    span_min_local_terms = _offtopic_span_min_local_terms()
  5299	    # Corpus-wide on-topic vocabulary, computed ONCE (Codex-P1 iter-2 answer): the per-span
  5300	    # off-topic gate KEEPS any span sharing vocabulary with the whole corpus, so lower-level /
  5301	    # synonym / acronym on-topic spans are retained; only spans foreign to the ENTIRE corpus
  5302	    # are withheld. Empty when the gate is disabled (byte-identical no-op).
  5303	    span_corpus_terms = _corpus_topic_terms(pool) if span_question_terms else set()
  5304	
  5305	    # Same-work grouping, PRESERVING the caller's relevance/weight order (mirrors
  5306	    # ``build_verified_span_draft``: a work's bucket is keyed by its FIRST-seen member so the
  5307	    # highest-ordered member of each work is the representative and bucket order is work order).
  5308	    work_order: list[str] = []
  5309	    work_members: dict[str, list[str]] = {}
  5310	    for ev_id in ev_ids:
  5311	        eid = str(ev_id or "")
  5312	        if not eid:
  5313	            continue
  5314	        ev = pool.get(eid)
  5315	        if not isinstance(ev, dict):
  5316	            continue
  5317	        direct_quote = _member_quote(ev)
  5318	        if not direct_quote or is_junk(direct_quote):
  5319	            continue
  5320	        key = _work_identity(eid, ev)
  5321	        if key not in work_members:
  5322	            work_members[key] = []
  5323	            work_order.append(key)
  5324	        work_members[key].append(eid)
  5325	
  5326	    lines: list[str] = []
  5327	    number = start_index
  5328	    for key in work_order:
  5329	        member_eids = work_members[key]
  5330	        representative = member_eids[0]
  5331	        rep_ev = pool.get(representative)
  5332	        if not isinstance(rep_ev, dict):
  5333	            continue
  5334	        rep_quote = _member_quote(rep_ev)
  5335	        units = _substantive_units(rep_quote, is_junk=is_junk)
  5336	        # I-deepfix-001 (#1344 SPAN-TOPICALITY): WITHHOLD confidently-foreign spans of an
  5337	        # otherwise-on-topic source from the numbered breadth surface (fail-open).
  5338	        units = _withhold_offtopic_spans(
  5339	            units, rep_ev, span_question_terms,
  5340	            span_min_content_words, span_min_local_terms,
  5341	            corpus_topic_terms=span_corpus_terms,
  5342	        )
  5343	        if not units:
  5344	            continue
  5345	        # Pre-compute each corroborator's sanitized quote ONCE for the contains-check (same-work URLs
  5346	        # co-cite ONLY when their own fetch actually contains the emitted unit — span-grounded markers).
  5347	        corroborator_quotes = [
  5348	            (m, _member_quote(pool[m]))
  5349	            for m in member_eids[1:]
  5350	            if isinstance(pool.get(m), dict)
  5351	        ]
  5352	        emitted: list[str] = []
  5353	        for unit in units[:budget]:
  5354	            markers = [representative]
  5355	            for m_eid, m_quote in corroborator_quotes:
  5356	                if unit in m_quote and m_eid not in markers:
  5357	                    markers.append(m_eid)
  5358	            emitted.append(_emit_unit(unit, markers))
  5359	        if not emitted:
  5360	            continue
  5361	        lines.append(f"{number}. {' '.join(emitted)}")
  5362	        number += 1
  5363	
  5364	    if not lines:
  5365	        return ""
  5366	    return f"## {_EVIDENCE_BASE_TITLE}\n\n" + "\n".join(lines)
